He said: "This is my stick, whereon I lean, and wherewith I beat down branches for my sheep, and wherein I find other uses."

# 2367

(Allah) said: "Cast it down, O Musa!"

# 2368

He cast it down, and behold! It was a snake, moving quickly.

# 2369

Allah said: "Grasp it and fear not; We shall return it to its former state."

# 2370

"And press your (right) hand to your (left) side: it will come forth white (and shining), without any disease as another sign,"

# 2371

"That We may show you (some) of Our greater signs."

# 2372

"Go to Fir\`awn! Verily, he has transgressed."

# 2373

He said: "O my Lord! Open for me my chest."

# 2374

"And ease my task for me;"

# 2375

"And loosen the knot from my tongue,"

# 2376

"That they understand my speech."

# 2377

"And appoint for me a helper from my family,"

# 2378

"Harun, my brother."

# 2379

"Increase my strength with him,"

# 2380

"And let him share my task,"

# 2381

"That we may glorify You much,"

# 2382

"And remember You much,"

# 2383

"Verily, You are ever seeing us."

# 2384

(Allah) said: "You are granted your request, O Musa!"

# 2385

"And indeed We conferred a favor on you another time (before)."

# 2386

"When We inspired your mother with that which We inspired."

# 2387

"Saying: \`Put him (the child) into the Tabut and put it into the river; then the river shall cast it up on the bank, and there, an enemy of Mine and an enemy of his shall take him.' And I endued you with love from Me, in order that you may be brought up under My Eye."

# 2388

"When your sister went and said: \`Shall I show you one who will nurse him' So We restored you to your mother, that she might cool her eyes and she should not grieve. Then you did kill a man, but We saved you from great distress and tried you with a heavy trial." Then you stayed a number of years with the people of Madyan. Then you came here according to the fixed term which I ordained (for you), O Musa!

# 2389

And I have chosen you for Myself.

# 2390

Go you and your brother with My Ayat, and do not, you both, slacken and become weak in My remembrance.

# 2391

Go both of you to Fir\`awn, verily, he has transgressed.

# 2392

And speak to him mildly, perhaps he may accept admonition or fear (Allah).

# 2393

Both of them said: "Our Lord! Verily, we fear lest he should hasten to punish us or lest he should transgress."

# 2394

He (Allah) said: "Fear not, verily, I am with you both, hearing and seeing."

# 2395

"So go you both to him, and say: 'Verily, we are both Messengers of your Lord, so let the Children of Israel go with us, and torment them not; indeed, we have come with a sign from your Lord! And peace will be upon him who follows the guidance!"

# 2396

\`Truly, it has been revealed to us that the torment will be for him who denies, and turns away.\`"

# 2397

Fir\`awn said: "Who then, O Musa, is the Lord of you two"

# 2398

\[Musa\] said: "Our Lord is He Who gave to each thing its form and nature, then guided it aright."

# 2399

\[Fir\`awn\] said: "What about the generations of old"

# 2400

\[Musa\] said: "The knowledge thereof is with my Lord, in a Record. My Lord neither errs nor forgets."

# 2401

Who has made earth for you like a bed; and has opened ways for you therein, and has sent down water (rain) from the sky. And We have brought forth with it various kinds of vegetation.

# 2402

Eat and pasture your cattle; verily, in this are Ayat for men of understanding.

# 2403

Thereof We created you, and into it We shall return you, and from it We shall bring you out once again.

# 2404

And indeed We showed him (Fir\`awn) all Our Ayat, but he denied and refused.

# 2405

He (Fir\`awn) said: "Have you come to drive us out of our land with your magic, O Musa"

# 2406

"Then verily, we can produce magic the like thereof; so appoint a meeting between us and you, which neither we nor you shall fail to keep, in an open place where both shall have a just and equal chance."

# 2407

(Musa) said: "Your appointed meeting is the day of the festival, and let the people assemble when the sun has risen (forenoon)."

# 2408

So Fir\`awn withdrew, devised his plot and then came back.

# 2409

Musa said to them: "Woe unto you! Invent not a lie against Allah, lest He should destroy you completely by a torment. And surely, he who invents a lie (against Allah) will fail miserably."

# 2410

Then they debated one with another what they must do, and they kept their talk secret.

# 2411

They said: "Verily, these are two magicians. Their object is to drive you out from your land with magic, and to take you away from your exemplary way."

# 2412

"So devise your plot, and then assemble in line. And whoever overcomes this day will be indeed successful."

# 2413

They said: "O Musa! Either you throw first or we be the first to throw"

# 2414

\[Musa\] said: "Nay, throw you (first)!" Then behold! their ropes and their sticks, by their magic, appeared to him as though they moved fast.

# 2415

So Musa conceived fear in himself.

# 2416

We (Allah) said: "Fear not! Surely, you will have the upper hand."

# 2417

"And throw that which is in your right hand! It will swallow up that which they have made. That which they have made is only a magician's trick, and the magician will never be successful, to whatever amount (of skill) he may attain."

# 2418

So the magicians fell down prostrate. They said: "We believe in the Lord of Harun and Musa."

# 2419

(Fir\`awn) said: "Believe you in him before I give you permission Verily, he is your chief who has taught you magic. So I will surely cut off your hands and feet on opposite sides, and I will surely crucify you on the trunks of date palms, and you shall surely know which of us can give the severe and more lasting torment. "

# 2420

They said: "We prefer you not over what have come to us of the clear signs and to Him (Allah) Who created us. So, decree whatever you desire to decree, for you can only' decree (regarding) this life of the world."

# 2421

"Verily, we have believed in our Lord, that He may forgive us our faults, and the magic to which you did compel us. And Allah is better as regards reward in comparison to your reward, and more lasting."

# 2422

Verily, whoever comes to his Lord as a criminal, then surely, for him is Hell, wherein he will neither die nor live.

# 2423

But whoever comes to Him as a believer, and has done righteous good deeds, for such are the high ranks,

# 2424

\`Adn Gardens, under which rivers flow, wherein they will abide forever, and such is the reward of those who purify themselves.

# 2425

And indeed We revealed to Musa: "Travel by night with My servants and strike a dry path for them in the sea, fearing neither to be overtaken nor being afraid."

# 2426

Then Fir\`awn pursued them with his hosts, but the sea \[Al-Yamm\] completely overwhelmed them and covered them up.

# 2427

And Fir\`awn led his people astray, and he did not guide them.

# 2428

O Children of Israel! We delivered you from your enemy, and We made a covenant with you on the right side of the Mount, and We sent down to you manna and quail,

# 2429

(Saying) eat of the Tayyibat wherewith We have provided you, and commit no transgression or oppression therein, lest My anger should justly descend on you. And he on whom My anger descends, he is indeed perished.

# 2430

And verily, I am indeed forgiving to him who repents, believes and does righteous deeds, and then Ihtada.

# 2431

"And what made you hasten from your people, O Musa

# 2432

He said: "They are close on my footsteps, and I hastened to You, O my Lord, that You might be pleased."

# 2433

(Allah) said: "Verily, We have tried your people in your absence, and As-Samiri has led them astray."

# 2434

Then Musa returned to his people in a state of anger and sorrow \[Asif\]. He said: "O my people! Did not your Lord promise you a fair promise Did then the promise seem to you long in coming Or did you desire that wrath should descend from your Lord on you, that you broke your promise to me"

# 2435

They said: "We broke not the promise to you, of our own will, but we were made to carry the weight of the ornaments of the people, then we cast them, and that was what As-Samiri suggested."

# 2436

Then he took out for them a calf which was mooing. They said: "This is your god, and the god of Musa," but he had forgotten.

# 2437

Did they not see that it could not return them a word (for answer), and that it had no power either to harm them or to do them good

# 2438

And Harun indeed had said to them beforehand: "O my people! You are being tried in this, and verily, your Lord is (Allah) the Most Gracious, so follow me and obey my order."

# 2439

They said: "We will not stop worshipping it, until Musa returns to us."

# 2440

(Musa) said: "O Harun! What prevented you when you saw them going astray;"

# 2441

"That you followed me not (according to my advice to you) Have you then disobeyed my order"

# 2442

He (Harun) said: "O son of my mother! Seize (me) not by my beard, nor by my head! Verily, I feared lest you should say: \`You have caused a division among the Children of Israel, and you have not respected my word!"'

# 2443

(Musa) said: "And what is the matter with you. O Samiri"

# 2444

(Samiri) said: "I saw what they saw not, so I took a (Qabdah) handful (of dust) from the (hoof) print of the messenger and threw it. Thus my inner self suggested to me."

# 2445

Musa said: "Then go away! And verily, your (punishment) in this life will be that you will say: \`Touch me not;' and verily, you have a promise that will not fail. And look at your god to which you have been devoted. We will certainly burn it, and scatter its particles in the sea."

# 2446

Your God is only Allah, there is no God but Him. He has full knowledge of all things.

# 2447

Thus We relate to you some information of what happened before. And indeed We have given you from Us a Reminder.

# 2448

Whoever turns away from it, verily, they will bear a heavy burden on the Day of Resurrection.

# 2449

They will abide in that -- and evil indeed will it be that load for them on the Day of Resurrection.

# 2450

The Day when the Sur will be blown: that Day, We shall gather the criminals blue-eyed.

# 2451

They will speak in a very low voice to each other (saying): "You stayed not longer than ten."

# 2452

We know very well what they will say, when the best among them in knowledge and wisdom will say: "You stayed no longer than a day!"

# 2453

And they ask you concerning the mountains. Say: "My Lord will blast them and scatter them as particles of dust."

# 2454

"Then He shall leave it as a level smooth plain."

# 2455

"You will see therein no crookedness nor curve."

# 2456

On that Day mankind will follow strictly (the voice of) Allah's caller, no crookedness (that is without going to the right or left of that voice) will they show him (Allah's caller). And all voices will be humbled for the Most Gracious (Allah), and nothing shall you hear except Hamsa.

# 2457

On that day no intercession shall avail, except the one for whom the Most Gracious has given permission and whose word is acceptable to Him.

# 2458

He knows what happens to them, and what will happen to them, but they will never encompass anything of His knowledge.

# 2459

And (all) faces shall be humbled before the Ever Living, the Sustainer. And he who carried wrongdoing, will be indeed a complete failure.

# 2460

And he who works deeds of righteousness, while he is a believer, then he will have no fear of injustice, nor of any curtailment.

# 2461

And thus We have sent it down as a Qur'an in Arabic, and have explained therein in detail the warnings, in order that they may have Taqwa, or that it may cause them to have a lesson from it.

# 2462

Then High above all be Allah, the True King. And be not in haste with the Qur'an before its revelation is completed to you, and say: "My Lord! Increase me in knowledge."

# 2463

And indeed We made a covenant with Adam before, but he forgot, and We found on his part no firm willpower.

# 2464

And (remember) when We said to the angels: "Prostrate yourselves to Adam." They prostrated themselves (all) except Iblis; he refused.

# 2465

Then We said: "O Adam! Verily, this is an enemy to you and to your wife. So let him not get you both out of Paradise, so that you will be distressed."

# 2466

"You will never be hungry therein nor naked."

# 2467

"And you (will) suffer not from thirst therein nor from the sun's heat."

# 2468

Then Shaytan whispered to him, saying: "O Adam! Shall I lead you to the Tree of Eternity and to a kingdom that will never waste away"

# 2469

Then they both ate of the Tree, and so their private parts became manifest to them, and they began to cover themselves with the leaves of the Paradise for their covering. Thus Adam disobeyd his Lord, so he went astray.

# 2470

Then his Lord chose him, and turned to him with forgiveness, and gave him guidance.

# 2471

He (Allah) said: "Get you down, both of you, together, some of you are an enemy to some others. Then if there comes to you guidance from Me, then whoever follows My guidance he shall neither go astray nor shall be distressed.

# 2472

But whosoever turns away from My Reminder, verily, for him is a life of hardship, and We shall raise him up blind on the Day of Resurrection."

# 2473

He will say: "O my Lord! Why have you raised me up blind, while I had sight (before)."

# 2474

(Allah) will say: "Like this Our Ayat came unto you, but you disregarded them, and so this Day, you will be neglected."

# 2475

And thus do We requite him who transgresses beyond bounds and believes not in the Ayat of his Lord; and the torment of the Hereafter is far more severe and more lasting.

# 2476

Is it not a guidance for them (to know) how many generations We have destroyed before them, in whose dwellings they walk Verily, in this are signs indeed for men of understanding.

# 2477

And had it not been for a Word that went forth before from your Lord, and a term determined, (their punishment) must necessarily have come (in this world).

# 2478

So bear patiently what they say, and glorify the praises of your Lord before the rising of the sun, and before its setting, and during some hours of the night, and at the ends of the day, that you may become pleased with the reward which Allah shall give you.

# 2479

And strain not your eyes in longing for the things We have given for enjoyment to various groups of them, the splendor of the life of this world, that We may test them thereby. But the provision of your Lord is better and more lasting.

# 2480

And enjoin Salah on your family, and be patient in offering them. We ask not of you a provision: We provide for you. And the good end is for those who have Taqwa.

# 2481

And they say, "Why does he not bring us a sign from his Lord?" Has there not come to them evidence of what was in the former scriptures?

# 2482

And if We had destroyed them with a torment before this, they would surely have said: "Our Lord! If only You had sent us a Messenger we should certainly have followed Your Ayat, before we were humiliated and disgraced."

# 2483

(Say) "Say, O Muhammad, to those who deny you, oppose you and continue in their disbelief and obstinance."

# 2484

Draws near for mankind their reckoning, while they turn away in heedlessness.

# 2485

Comes not unto them an admonition from their Lord as a recent revelation but they listen to it while they play.

# 2486

With their hearts occupied. Those who do wrong, conceal their private counsels, (saying): "Is this more than a human being like you Will you submit to magic while you see it"

# 2487

He said: "My Lord knows what is said in the heavens and on earth. And He is the All-Hearer, the All-Knower."

# 2488

Nay, they say: "These are mixed up false dreams! Nay, he has invented it! -- Nay, he is a poet! Let him then bring us an Ayah like the ones that were sent before!"

# 2489

Not one of the towns of those which We destroyed, believed before them; will they then believe.

# 2490

And We sent not before you but men to whom We revealed. So ask the people of the Reminder if you do not know.

# 2491

And We did not place them in bodies that did not eat food, nor were they immortals.

# 2492

Then We fulfilled to them the promise. So We saved them and those whom We willed, but We destroyed Al-Musrifin.

# 2493

Indeed, We have sent down for you a Book in which there is Dhikrukum. Will you not then understand

# 2494

How many a town given to wrongdoing, have We destroyed, and raised up after them another people!

# 2495

Then, when they sensed Our torment, behold, they (tried to) flee from it.

# 2496

Flee not, but return to that wherein you lived a luxurious life, and to your homes, in order that you may be questioned.

# 2497

They cried: "Woe to us! Certainly we have been wrongdoers."

# 2498

And that cry of theirs ceased not, till We made them as a field that is reaped, extinct.

# 2499

We created not the heavens and the earth and all that is between them for play.

# 2500

Had We intended to take a pastime, We could surely have taken it from Us, if We were going to do (that).

# 2501

Nay, We fling the truth against the falsehood, so it destroys it, and behold, it disappears. And woe to you for that which you ascribe.

# 2502

To Him belongs whosoever is in the heavens and on earth. And those who are near Him are not too proud to worship Him, nor are they weary.

# 2503

They glorify His praises night and day, they never slacken.

# 2504

Or have they taken (for worship) gods from the earth who raise the dead

# 2505

Had there been therein (in the heavens and the earth) gods besides Allah, then verily, both would have been ruined. Glorified be Allah, the Lord of the Throne, (High is He) above all that (evil) they associate with Him!

# 2506

He cannot be questioned as to what He does, while they will be questioned.

# 2507

Or have they taken for worship gods besides Him Say: "Bring your proof. This is the Reminder for those with me and the Reminder for those before me." But most of them know not the Truth, so they are averse.

# 2508

And We did not send any Messenger before you but We revealed to him (saying): "There is no God but I, so worship Me."

# 2509

And they say: "The Most Gracious has begotten children." Glory to Him! They are but honored servants.

# 2510

They speak not until He has spoken, and they act on His command.

# 2511

He knows what is before them, and what is behind them, and they cannot intercede except for him with whom He is pleased. And they stand in awe for fear of Him.

# 2512

And if any of them should say: "Verily, I am a god besides Him," such We should recompense with Hell. Thus We recompense the wrongdoers.

# 2513

Have not those who disbelieve known that the heavens and the earth were joined together as one united piece, then We parted them And We have made from water every living thing. Will they not then believe

# 2514

And We have placed on the earth firm mountains, lest it should shake with them, and We placed therein broad highways for them to pass through, that they may be guided.

# 2515

And We have made the heaven a roof, safe and well-guarded. Yet they turn away from its signs.

# 2516

And He it is Who has created the night and the day, and the sun and the moon, each in an orbit floating.

# 2517

And We granted not to any human being immortality before you; then if you die, would they live forever

# 2518

Everyone is going to taste death, and We shall test you with evil and with good by way of trial. And to Us you will be returned.

# 2519

And when those who disbelieved see you, they take you not except for mockery (saying): "Is this the one who talks about your gods" While they disbelieve at the mention of the Most Gracious.

# 2520

Man is created of haste. I will show you My Ayat. So ask Me not to hasten (them).

# 2521

And they say: "When will this promise (come to pass), if you are truthful."

# 2522

If only those who disbelieved knew (the time) when they will not be able to ward off the Fire from their faces, nor from their backs, and they will not be helped.

# 2523

Nay, it will come upon them all of a sudden and will perplex them, and they will have no power to avert it nor will they get respite.

# 2524

Indeed (many) Messengers were mocked before you, but the scoffers were surrounded by what they used to mock.

# 2525

Say: "Who can guard and protect you in the night or in the day from the Most Gracious" Nay, but they turn away from the remembrance of their Lord.

# 2526

Or have they gods who can guard them from Us They have no power to help themselves, nor can they be protected from Us.

# 2527

Nay, We gave the luxuries of this life to these men and their fathers until the period grew long for them. See they not that We gradually reduce the land from its outlying borders Is it then they who will overcome

# 2528

Say: "I warn you only by the revelation. "But the deaf will not hear the call, (even) when they are warned.

# 2529

And if a breath of the torment of your Lord touches them, they will surely cry: "Woe unto us! Indeed we have been wrongdoers."

# 2530

And We shall set up Balances of justice on the Day of Resurrection, then none will be dealt with unjustly in anything. And if there be the weight of a mustard seed, We will bring it. And sufficient are We to take account.

# 2531

And indeed We granted to Musa and Harun the criterion, and a shining light and a Reminder for those who have Taqwa.

# 2532

Those who fear their Lord in the unseen, and they are afraid of the Hour.

# 2533

And this is a blessed Reminder which We have sent down; will you then deny it

# 2534

And indeed We bestowed aforetime on Ibrahim his guidance, and We were Well-Acquainted with him.

# 2535

When he said to his father and his people: "What are these images to which you are devoted"

# 2536

They said: "We found our fathers worshipping them."

# 2537

He said: "Indeed you and your fathers have been in manifest error."

# 2538

They said: "Have you brought us the Truth, or are you one of those who play about"

# 2539

He said: "Nay, your Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth, Who created them and to that I am one of the witnesses."

# 2540

"And by Allah, I shall plot a plan for your idols after you have gone away and turned your backs."

# 2541

So he broke them to pieces, except the biggest of them, that they might turn to it.

# 2542

They said: "Who has done this to our gods He must indeed be one of the wrongdoers."

# 2543

They said: "We heard a young man talking against them, who is called Ibrahim."

# 2544

They said: "Then bring him before the eyes of the people, that they may testify."

# 2545

They said: "Are you the one who has done this to our gods, O Ibrahim"

# 2546

He said: "Nay, this one, the biggest of them did it. Ask them, if they can speak!"

# 2547

So they turned to themselves and said: "Verily, you are the wrongdoers."

# 2548

Then they turned to themselves: "Indeed you know well that these speak not!"

# 2549

He said: "Do you then worship besides Allah, things that can neither profit you nor harm you"

# 2550

"Fie upon you, and upon that which you worship besides Allah! Have you then no sense"

# 2551

They said: "Burn him and help your gods, if you will be doing."

# 2552

We said: "O fire! Be you cool and safety for Ibrahim!"

# 2553

And they wanted to harm him, but We made them the worst losers.

# 2554

And We rescued him and Lut to the land which We have blessed for the nations.

# 2555

And We bestowed upon him Ishaq, and Ya\`qub Nafilatan. Each one We made righteous.

# 2556

And We made them leaders, guiding by Our command, and We revealed to them the doing of good deeds, performing Salah, and the giving of Zakah, and of Us (Alone) they were the worshippers.

# 2557

And (remember) Lut, We gave him wisdom and knowledge, and We saved him from the town who practised Al-Khaba'ith. Verily, they were a people given to evil, and were rebellious.

# 2558

And We admitted him to Our mercy; truly, he was of the righteous.

# 2559

And (remember) Nuh, when he cried (to Us) aforetime. We answered to his invocation and saved him and his family from the great distress.

# 2560

We helped him against the people who denied Our Ayat. Verily, they were a people given to evil. So We drowned them all.

# 2561

And (remember) Dawud and Sulayman, when they gave judgement in the case of the field in which the sheep of certain people had Nafashat; and We were witness to their judgement.

# 2562

And We made Sulayman to understand (the case); and to each of them We gave wisdom (Hukm) and knowledge. And We subjected the mountains and the birds to glorify Our praises along with Dawud. And it was We Who were the doer (of all these things).

# 2563

And We taught him the making of metal coats of mail (for battles), to protect you in your fighting. Are you then grateful

# 2564

And to Sulayman (We subjected) the wind strongly raging, running by his command towards the land which We had blessed. And of everything We are the All-Knower.

# 2565

And of the Shayatin were some who dived for him, and did other work besides that; and it was We Who guarded them.

# 2566

And (remember) Ayyub, when he cried to his Lord: "Verily, distress has seized me, and You are the Most Merciful of all those who show mercy."

# 2567

So We answered his call, and We removed the distress that was on him, and We restored his family to him, and the like thereof along with them as a mercy from Ourselves and a Reminder for all those who worship Us.

# 2568

And (remember) Isma\`il, Idris and Dhul-Kifl: All were from among the patient.

# 2569

And We admitted them to Our mercy. Verily, they were of the righteous.

# 2570

And (remember) Dhun-Nun, when he went off in anger, and imagined that We shall not punish him! But he cried through the darknesses (Zulumat) (saying): "There is no God but You, Glorified be You! Truly, I have been of the Zalimin wrongdoers."

# 2571

So We answered his call, and delivered him from the distress. And thus We do deliver the believers.

# 2572

And (remember) Zakariyya, when he cried to his Lord: "O My Lord! Leave me not single (childless), though You are the Best of the inheritors."

# 2573

So We answered his call, and We bestowed upon him Yahya, and cured his wife for him. Verily, they used to hasten on to do good deeds, and they used to call on Us with hope and fear, and they were Khashi\`in before Us.

# 2574

And she who guarded her chastity, We breathed into her through Our Ruh, and We made her and her son a sign for nations.

# 2575

Truly, this, your Ummah is one, and I am your Lord, therefore worship Me.

# 2576

But they have broken up and differed in their religion among themselves. (And) they all shall return to Us.

# 2577

So whoever does righteous good deeds while he is a believer, his efforts will not be rejected. Verily, We record it for him (in his Book of deeds).

# 2578

And a ban is laid on every town which We have destroyed that they shall not return.

# 2579

Until, when Ya'juj and Ma'juj (Gog and Magog people) are let loose, and they swoop down from every Hadab.

# 2580

And the true promise shall draw near. Then, you shall see the eyes of the disbelievers fixedly staring in horror. (They will say:) "Woe to us! We were indeed heedless of this -- nay, but we were wrongdoers."

# 2581

Certainly you and that which you are worshipping now besides Allah, are (but) fuel (Hasab) for Hell! (Surely) you will enter it.

# 2582

Had these been gods, they would not have entered there (Hell), and all of them will abide therein forever.

# 2583

Therein they will be breathing out with deep sighs and roaring and therein they will hear not.

# 2584

Verily, those for whom the good has preceded from Us, they will be removed far therefrom (Hell).

# 2585

They shall not hear the slightest sound of it (Hell), while they abide in that which their own selves desire.

# 2586

The greatest terror will not grieve them, and the angels will meet them, (with the greeting:) "This is your Day which you were promised."

# 2587

And (remember) the Day when We shall roll up the heaven like a Sijill for books. As We began the first creation, We shall repeat it. (It is) a promise binding upon Us. Truly, We shall do it.

# 2588

And indeed We have written in Az-Zabur after Adh-Dhikr that My righteous servants shall inherit the land.

# 2589

Verily, in this there is a plain Message for people who worship Allah.

# 2590

And We have sent you (O Muhammad) not but as a mercy for the \`Alamin.

# 2591

Say: "It is revealed to me that your God is only one God. Will you then be Muslims"

# 2592

But if they turn away say: "I give you a notice to be known to us all alike. And I know not whether that which you are promised is near or far."

# 2593

"Verily, He knows that which is spoken aloud and He knows that which you conceal."

# 2594

"And I know not, perhaps it may be a trial for you, and an enjoyment for a while."

# 2595

He said:"My Lord! Judge You in truth! Our Lord is the Most Gracious, Whose help is to be sought against that which you attribute!"

# 2596

O mankind! Have Taqwa of your Lord! Verily, the earthquake of the Hour is a terrible thing.

# 2597

The Day you shall see it, every nursing mother will forget her nursling, and every pregnant one will drop her load, and you shall see mankind as in a drunken state, yet they will not be drunk, but Allah's torment is severe.

# 2598

And among mankind is he who disputes about Allah, without knowledge, and follows every rebellious Shaytan.

# 2599

For him (the devil) it is decreed that whosoever follows him, he will mislead him, and will drive him to the torment of the Fire.

# 2600

O mankind! If you are in doubt about the Resurrection, then verily, We have created you from dust, then from a Nutfah, then from a clot then from a little lump of flesh -- some formed and some unformed -- that We may make (it) clear to you. And We cause whom We will to remain in the wombs for an appointed term, then We bring you out as infants, then (give you growth) that you may reach your age of full strength. And among you there is he who dies (young), and among you there is he who is brought back to the miserable old age, so that he knows nothing after having known. And you see the earth Hamidatan, but when We send down water on it, it is stirred (to life), and it swells and puts forth every lovely kind (of growth).

# 2601

That is because Allah: He is the Truth, and it is He Who gives life to the dead, and it is He Who is able to do all things.

# 2602

And surely, the Hour is coming, there is no doubt about it; and certainly, Allah will resurrect those who are in the graves.

# 2603

And among men is he who disputes about Allah, without knowledge or guidance, or a Book giving light (from Allah).

# 2604

Bending his neck in pride, and leading (others) too (far) astray from the path of Allah. For him there is disgrace in this worldly life, and on the Day of Resurrection We shall make him taste the torment of burning.

# 2605

That is because of what your hands have sent forth, and verily, Allah is not unjust to servants.

# 2606

And among mankind is he who worships Allah as it were upon the edge: if good befalls him, he is content therewith; but if a Fitnah strikes him, he turns back on his face. He loses both this world and the Hereafter. That is the evident loss.

# 2607

He calls besides Allah unto that which can neither harm him nor profit him. That is a straying far away.

# 2608

He calls unto him whose harm is nearer than his profit; certainly an evil Mawla and certainly an evil \`Ashir!

# 2609

Truly, Allah will admit those who believe and do righteous good deeds to Gardens underneath which rivers flow. Verily, Allah does what He wills.

# 2610

Whoever thinks that Allah will not help him in this world and in the Hereafter, let him stretch out a rope to the ceiling and let him strangle himself. Then let him see whether his plan will remove that whereat he rages!

# 2611

Thus have We sent it down as clear Ayat, and surely, Allah guides whom He wills.

# 2612

Verily, those who believe, and those who are Jews, and the Sabians, and the Christians, and the Majus, and those who worship others besides Allah; truly, Allah will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection. Verily, Allah is over all things a Witness.

# 2613

See you not that whoever is in the heavens and whoever is on the earth, and the sun, and the moon, and the stars, and the mountains, and the trees, and Ad-Dawabb, and many of mankind prostrate themselves to Allah. But there are many (men) on whom the punishment is justified. And whomsoever Allah disgraces, none can honor him. Verily, Allah does what He wills.

# 2614

These two opponents dispute with each other about their Lord; then as for those who disbelieved, garments of fire will be cut out for them, boiling water will be poured down over their heads.

# 2615

With it will melt (or vanish away) what is within their bellies, as well as (their) skins.

# 2616

And for them are hooked rods of iron.

# 2617

Every time they seek to get away therefrom, from anguish, they will be driven back therein, and (it will be) said to them: "Taste the torment of burning!"

# 2618

Truly, Allah will admit those who believe and do righteous good deeds, to Gardens underneath which rivers flow (in Paradise), wherein they will be adorned with bracelets of gold and pearls and their garments therein will be of silk.

# 2619

And they are guided unto goodly speech and they are guided to the path of Him, Who is Worthy of all praises.

# 2620

Verily, those who disbelieved and hinder (men) from the path of Allah, and from Al-Masjid Al-Haram which We have made (open) to (all) men, the dweller in it and the visitor from the country are equal there, and whoever inclines to evil actions therein or to do wrong, him We shall cause to taste from a painful torment.

# 2621

And (remember) when We showed Ibrahim the site of the House (saying): "Associate not anything with Me, and sanctify My House for those who circumambulate it, and those who stand up (for prayer), and those who bow and make prostration (in prayer);"

# 2622

And proclaim to mankind the Hajj (pilgrimage). They will come to you on foot and on every lean camel, they will come from every Fajj \`Amiq.

# 2623

That they may witness things that are of benefit to them, and mention the Name of Allah on appointed days, over the beast of cattle that He has provided for them. Then eat thereof and feed therewith the poor having a hard time.

# 2624

Then let them complete their prescribed duties and perform their vows, and circumambulate the \`Atiq House.

# 2625

That and whoever honors the sacred things of Allah, then that is better for him with his Lord. The cattle are lawful to you, except those (that will be) mentioned to you. So shun the Rijs of the idols, and shun false speech.

# 2626

Hunafa' Lillah, not associating partners unto Him; and whoever assigns partners to Allah, it is as if he had fallen from the sky, the birds caught him in midair, or the wind had thrown him to a far off place.

# 2627

Thus it is, and whosoever honors the Sha\`a'ir of Allah, then it is truly from the Taqwa of the hearts.

# 2628

In them are benefits for you for an appointed term, and afterwards they are brought for sacrifice to the \`Atiq House.

# 2629

And for every nation We have appointed religious ceremonies, that they may mention the Name of Allah over the beast of cattle that He has given them for food. And your God is One God, so you must submit to Him Alone. And give glad tidings to the Mukhbitin.

# 2630

Whose hearts are filled with fear when Allah is mentioned, and the patient who bear whatever may befall them, and who perform the Salah, and who spend out of what We have provided for them.

# 2631

And the Budn, We have made them for you as among the symbols of Allah, wherein you have much good. So mention the Name of Allah over them when they are drawn up in lines (for sacrifice). Then, when they are down on their sides (after slaughter), eat thereof, and feed the Qani\` and the Mu\`tarr. Thus have We made them subject to you that you may be grateful.

# 2632

It is neither their meat nor their blood that reaches Allah, but it is Taqwa from you that reaches Him. Thus have We made them subject to you that you may proclaim Allah's greatness for His guidance to you. And give glad tidings to the doers of good.

# 2633

Truly, Allah defends those who believe. Verily, Allah likes not any treacherous ingrate.

# 2634

Permission (to fight) is given to those (believers) who are fought against, because they have been wronged; and surely, Allah is able to give them victory.

# 2635

Those who have been expelled from their homes unjustly only because they said: "Our Lord is Allah." For had it not been that Allah checks one set of people by means of another, Sawami\`, Biya\`, Salawat, and Masjids, wherein the Name of Allah is mentioned much, would surely have been pulled down. Verily, Allah will help those who help His (cause). Truly, Allah is All-Strong, All-Mighty.

# 2636

Those who, if We give them power in the land, establish the Salah, enforce the Zakah, and they enjoin the good and forbid the evil. And with Allah rests the end of (all) matters.

# 2637

And if they deny you, so did deny before them the people of Nuh, \`Ad and Thamud.

# 2638

And the people of Ibrahim and the people of Lut,

# 2639

And the dwellers of Madyan; and denied was Musa. But I granted respite to the disbelievers for a while, then I seized them, and how (terrible) was My punishment!

# 2640

And many a township did We destroy while they were given to wrongdoing, so that it lie in ruins, and a deserted well and castle Mashid!

# 2641

Have they not traveled through the land, and have they hearts wherewith to understand and ears wherewith to hear Verily, it is not the eyes that grow blind, but it is the hearts which are in the breasts that grow blind.

# 2642

And they ask you to hasten on the torment! And Allah fails not His promise. And verily a day with your Lord is as a thousand years of what you reckon.

# 2643

And many a township did I give respite while it was given to wrongdoing. Then I seized it (with punishment). And to Me is the (final) return (of all).

# 2644

Say: "O mankind! I am (sent) to you only as a plain warner."

# 2645

So those who believe and do righteous good deeds, for them is forgiveness and Rizq Karim.

# 2646

But those who strive against Our Ayat to frustrate them, they will be dwellers of the Hellfire.

# 2647

Never did We send a Messenger or a Prophet before you but when he did recite (the revelation or narrated or spoke), Shaytan threw (some falsehood) in his recitation (of the revelation). But Yansakh Allah that which Shaytan throws in. Then Allah establishes His revelations. And Allah is All-Knower, All-Wise:

# 2648

That He (Allah) may make what is thrown in by Shaytan a trial for those in whose hearts is a disease and whose hearts are hardened. And certainly, the wrongdoers are in an opposition far-off (from the truth).

# 2649

And that those who have been given knowledge may know that it (this Qur'an) is the truth from your Lord, so that they may believe therein, and their hearts may submit to it with humility. And verily, Allah is the Guide of those who believe, to the straight path.

# 2650

And those who disbelieved, will not cease to be in doubt about it until the Hour comes suddenly upon them, or there comes to them the torment of Yawm \`Aqim.

# 2651

The sovereignty on that Day will be that of Allah. He will judge between them. So those who believed and did righteous good deeds will be in Gardens of Delight.

# 2652

And those who disbelieved and denied Our Ayat, for them will be a humiliating torment (in Hell).

# 2653

Those who emigrated in the cause of Allah and after that were killed or died, surely, Allah will provide a good provision for them. And verily, it is Allah Who indeed is the Best of those who make provision.

# 2654

Truly, He will make them enter an entrance with which they shall be well-pleased, and verily, Allah indeed is All-Knowing, Most Forbearing.

# 2655

That is so. And whoever has retaliated with the like of that which he was made to suffer, and then has again been wronged, Allah will surely help him. Verily, Allah indeed is Oft-Pardoning, Oft-Forgiving.

# 2656

That is because Allah merges the night into the day, and He merges the day into the night. And verily, Allah is All-Hearer, All-Seer.

# 2657

That is because Allah -- He is the Truth, and what they invoke besides Him, it is false. And verily, Allah -- He is the Most High, the Most Great.

# 2658

See you not that Allah sends down water from the sky, and then the earth becomes green Verily, Allah is the Most Kind and Courteous, Well-Acquainted with all things.

# 2659

To Him belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is on the earth. And verily, Allah -- He is Rich, Worthy of all praise.

# 2660

See you not that Allah has subjected to you all that is on the earth, and the ships that sail through the sea by His command He withholds the heaven from falling on the earth except by His leave. Verily, Allah is for mankind, full of kindness, Most Merciful.

# 2661

It is He, Who gave you life, and then will cause you to die, and will again give you life. Verily, man is indeed Kafurun.

# 2662

For every nation We have made Mansak which they must follow; so let them not dispute with you on the matter, but invite them to your Lord. Verily, you indeed are on the straight guidance.

# 2663

And if they argue with you, say: "Allah knows best of what you do."

# 2664

"Allah will judge between you on the Day of Resurrection about that wherein you used to differ."

# 2665

Know you not that Allah knows all that is in the heaven and on the earth Verily, it is (all) in the Book. Verily, that is easy for Allah.

# 2666

And they worship besides Allah others for which He has sent down no authority, and of which they have no knowledge; and for the wrongdoers there is no helper.

# 2667

And when Our clear Ayat are recited to them, you will notice a denial on the faces of the disbelievers! They are nearly ready to attack with violence those who recite Our Ayat to them. Say: "Shall I tell you of something worse than that The Fire which Allah has promised to those who disbelieved, and worst indeed is that destination!"

# 2668

O mankind! A parable has been made, so listen to it: Verily, those on whom you call besides Allah, cannot create a fly, even though they combine together for the purpose. And if the fly snatches away a thing from them, they will have no power to release it from the fly. So weak are the seeker and the sought.

# 2669

They have not regarded Allah with His rightful esteem. Verily, Allah is All-Strong, All-Mighty.

# 2670

Allah chooses Messengers from angels and from men. Verily, Allah is All-Hearer, All-Seer.

# 2671

He knows what is before them, and what is behind them. And to Allah return all matters.

# 2672

O you who believe! Bow down, and prostrate yourselves, and worship your Lord and do good that you may be successful.

# 2673

And strive hard in Allah's cause as you ought to strive. He has chosen you, and has not laid upon you in religion any hardship: it is the religion of your father Ibrahim. He has named you Muslims both before and in this (Qur'an), that the Messenger may be a witness over you and you be witnesses over mankind! So, perform the Salah, give the Zakah and hold fast to Allah. He is your Mawla, what an Excellent Mawla and what an Excellent Helper!

# 2674

Successful indeed are the believers.

# 2675

Those who with their Salah are Khashi\`un.

# 2676

And those who turn away from Al-Laghw.

# 2677

And those who pay the Zakah.

# 2678

And those who guard their private parts.

# 2679

Except from their wives or their right hand possessions, for then, they are free from blame.

# 2680

But whoever seeks beyond that, then those are the transgressors.

# 2681

Those who are faithfully true to their Amanat and to their covenants are Ra\`un.

# 2682

And those who strictly guard their Salawat.

# 2683

These are indeed the heirs.

# 2684

Who shall inherit Firdaws. They shall dwell therein forever.

# 2685

And indeed We created man out of an extract of Tin.

# 2686

Thereafter We made him a Nutfah in a safe lodging.

# 2687

Then We made the Nutfah into a clot, then We made the clot into a little lump of flesh, then We made out of that little lump of flesh bones, then We clothed the bones with flesh, and then We brought it forth as another creation. So Blessed is Allah, the Best of creators.

# 2688

After that, surely you will die.

# 2689

Then (again), surely you will be resurrected on the Day of Resurrection.

# 2690

And indeed We have created above you seven Tara'iq, and We are never unaware of the creation.

# 2691

And We sent down from the sky water in measure, and We gave it lodging in the earth, and verily, We are able to take it away.

# 2692

Then We brought forth for you therewith gardens of date palms and grapes, wherein is much fruit for you, and whereof you eat.

# 2693

And a tree that springs forth from Tur Sinai, that grows oil, and relish for the eaters.

# 2694

And verily, in the cattle there is indeed a lesson for you. We give you to drink of that which is in their bellies. And there are, in them, numerous benefits for you, and of them you eat.

# 2695

And on them, and on ships you are carried.

# 2696

And indeed We sent Nuh to his people, and he said: "O my people! Worship Allah! You have no other God but Him. Will you not then have Taqwa"

# 2697

But the chiefs of his people who disbelieved said: "He is no more than a human being like you, he seeks to make himself superior to you. Had Allah willed, He surely could have sent down angels. Never did we hear such a thing among our fathers of old."

# 2698

"He is only a man in whom is madness, so wait for him a while."

# 2699

He said: "O my Lord! Help me because they deny me."

# 2700

So, We revealed to him: "Construct the ship under Our Eyes and under Our revelation. Then, when Our command comes, and (water) gushes forth from the oven, take on board of each kind two, and your family, except those thereof against whom the Word has already gone forth. And address Me not in favor of those who have done wrong. Verily, they are to be drowned."

# 2701

"And when you have embarked on the ship, you and whoever is with you, then say: \`All the praise be to Allah, Who has saved us from the people who are wrongdoers."

# 2702

"And say: \`My Lord! Cause me to land at a blessed landing place, for You are the Best of those who bring to land."'

# 2703

Verily, in this, there are indeed Ayat, for sure We are ever putting (men) to the test.

# 2704

Then, after them, We created another generation.

# 2705

And We sent to them a Messenger from among themselves (saying): "Worship Allah! You have no other God but Him. Will you not then have Taqwa"

# 2706

And the chiefs of his people who disbelieved and denied the meeting in the Hereafter, and whom We had given the luxuries and comforts of worldly life, said: "He is no more than a human being like you, he eats of that which you eat, and drinks of what you drink."

# 2707

"If you were to obey a human being like yourselves, then verily, you indeed would be losers."

# 2708

"Does he promise you that when you have died and have become dust and bones, you shall come out alive"

# 2709

"Far, very far is that which you are promised!"

# 2710

"There is nothing but our life of this world! We die and we live! And we are not going to be resurrected!"

# 2711

"He is only a man who has invented a lie against Allah, and we are not going to believe in him."

# 2712

He said: "O my Lord! Help me because they deny me."

# 2713

(Allah) said: "In a little while, they are sure to be regretful."

# 2714

So, the Sayhah overtook them in truth, and We made them as rubbish of dead plants. So, away with the people who are wrongdoers.

# 2715

Then, after them, We created other generations.

# 2716

No nation can advance their term, nor can they delay it.

# 2717

Then We sent Our Messengers in succession. Every time there came to a nation their Messenger, they denied him; so, We made them follow one another, and We made them as Ahadith. So, away with a people who believe not!

# 2718

Then We sent Musa and his brother Harun, with Our Ayat and manifest authority,

# 2719

To Fir\`awn and his chiefs, but they behaved insolently and they were people self-exalting (by disobeying their Lord).

# 2720

They said: "Shall we believe in two men like ourselves, and their people are obedient to us with humility!"

# 2721

So, they denied them both and became of those who were destroyed.

# 2722

And indeed We gave Musa the Scripture, that they may be guided.

# 2723

And We made the son of Maryam and his mother as a sign, and We gave them refuge on a Rabwah, Dhat Qarar, and Ma\`in.

# 2724

O Messengers! Eat of the Tayyibat and do righteous deeds. Verily, I am Well-Acquainted with what you do.

# 2725

And verily, this your religion is one religion, and I am your Lord, so have Taqwa."

# 2726

But they have broken their religion among them into sects, each group rejoicing in what is with it.

# 2727

So, leave them in their error for a time.

# 2728

Do they think that in wealth and children with which We prolong them

# 2729

We hasten unto them with good things. Nay, but they perceive not.

# 2730

Verily, those who live in awe for fear of their Lord;

# 2731

And those who believe in the Ayat of their Lord;

# 2732

And those who join not anyone as partners with their Lord;

# 2733

And those who give that which they give with their hearts full of fear, because they are sure to return to their Lord.

# 2734

It is these who hasten in the good deeds, and they are foremost in them.

# 2735

And We task not any person except according to his capacity, and with Us is a Record which speaks the truth, and they will not be wronged.

# 2736

Nay, but their hearts are covered from this, and they have other deeds, besides which they are doing.

# 2737

Until when We seize those of them who lead a luxurious life with punishment; behold, they make humble invocation with a loud voice.

# 2738

Invoke not loudly this day! Certainly you shall not be helped by Us.

# 2739

Indeed My Ayat used to be recited to you, but you used to turn back on your heels.

# 2740

In pride, talking evil about it by night.

# 2741

Have they not pondered over the Word, or has there come to them what had not come to their fathers of old

# 2742

Or is it that they did not recognize their Messenger so they deny him

# 2743

Or they say: There is madness in him Nay, but he brought them the truth, but most of them are averse to the truth.

# 2744

And if Al-Haqq had followed their desires, verily, the heavens and the earth, and whosoever is therein would have been corrupted! Nay, We have brought them their reminder, but they turn away from their reminder.

# 2745

Or is it that you ask them for some Kharj But the recompense of your Lord is better, and He is the Best of those who give sustenance.

# 2746

And certainly, you call them to the straight path.

# 2747

And verily, those who believe not in the Hereafter are indeed deviating far astray from the path.

# 2748

And though We had mercy on them and removed the distress which is on them, still they would obstinately persist in their transgression, wandering blindly.

# 2749

And indeed We seized them with punishment, but they humbled not themselves to their Lord, nor did they invoke with submission to Him.

# 2750

Until, when We open for them the gate of severe punishment, then lo! they will be plunged in despair.

# 2751

It is He Who has created for you hearing, eyes, and hearts. Little thanks you give.

# 2752

And it is He Who has created you on the earth, and to Him you shall be gathered back.

# 2753

And it is He Who gives life and causes death, and His is the alternation of night and day. Will you not then understand

# 2754

Nay, but they say the like of what the men of old said.

# 2755

They said: "When we are dead and have become dust and bones, shall we be resurrected indeed"

# 2756

"Verily, this we have been promised -- we and our fathers before! This is only (from) tales of the ancients!") Allah's saying:

# 2757

Say: "Whose is the earth and whosoever is therein If you know!"

# 2758

They will say: "It is Allah's!" Say: "Will you not then remember"

# 2759

Say: "Who is (the) Lord of the seven heavens, and (the) Lord of the Great Throne"

# 2760

They will say: "Allah." Say: "Will you not then have Taqwa"

# 2761

Say: "In Whose Hand is the sovereignty of everything And He protects, while against Whom there is no protector, if you know"

# 2762

They will say: "(All that belongs) to Allah." Say: "How then are you deceived and turn away from the truth"

# 2763

Nay, but We have brought them the truth, and verily, they are liars.

# 2764

No son (or offspring) did Allah beget, nor is there any god along with Him. (If there had been many gods), then each god would have taken away what he had created, and some would have tried to overcome others! Glorified be Allah above all that they attribute to Him!

# 2765

All-Knower of the unseen and the seen! Exalted be He over all that they associate as partners to Him!

# 2766

Say: "My Lord! If You would show me that with which they are threatened, "

# 2767

"My Lord! Then, put me not amongst the people who are the wrongdoers."

# 2768

And indeed We are able to show you that with which We have threatened them.

# 2769

Repel evil with that which is better. We are best-acquainted with the things they utter.

# 2770

And say: "My Lord! I seek refuge with You from the whisperings of the Shayatin."

# 2771

"And I seek refuge with You, My Lord! lest they should come near me."

# 2772

Until, when death comes to one of them, he says: "My Lord! Send me back,"

# 2773

"So that I may do good in that which I have left behind!" No! (Kalla) It is but a word that he speaks; and in front of them is Barzakh until the Day when they will be resurrected.

# 2774

Then, when the Trumpet is blown, there will be no kinship among them that Day, nor will they ask of one another.

# 2775

Then, those whose Scales (of good deeds) are heavy, these! they are the successful.

# 2776

And those whose Scales (of good deeds) are light, they are those who lose themselves, in Hell will they abide.

# 2777

The Fire will burn their faces, and therein they will grin, with displaced lips (disfigured).

# 2778

"Were not My Ayat recited to you, and then you used to deny them"

# 2779

They will say: "Our Lord! Our wretchedness overcame us, and we were (an) erring people."

# 2780

"Our Lord! Bring us out of this. If ever we return (to evil), then indeed we shall be wrongdoers."

# 2781

He (Allah) will say: "Remain you in it with ignominy! And speak you not to Me!"

# 2782

Verily, there was a party of My servants who used to say: "Our Lord! We believe, so forgive us and have mercy on us, for You are the Best of all who show mercy!"

# 2783

But you took them for a laughing stock, so much so that they made you forget My remembrance while you used to laugh at them!

# 2784

Verily, I have rewarded them this Day for their patience; they are indeed the ones that are successful.

# 2785

He will say: "What number of years did you stay on earth"

# 2786

They will say: "We stayed a day or part of a day. Ask of those who keep account."

# 2787

He will say: "You stayed not but a little, if you had only known!"

# 2788

"Did you think that We had created you in play, and that you would not be brought back to Us"

# 2789

So Exalted be Allah, the True King: None has the right to be worshipped but He, the Lord of Al-\`Arsh Al-Karim!

# 2790

And whoever invokes besides Allah, any other god, of whom he has no proof; then his reckoning is only with his Lord. Surely, disbelievers will not be successful.

# 2791

And say: "My Lord! Forgive and have mercy, for You are the Best of those who show mercy!"

# 2792

A Surah which We have sent down and which We have enjoined (Faradnaha), and in it We have revealed manifest Ayat, that you may remember.

# 2793

The Zaniyah and the Zani, flog each of them with a hundred stripes. Let not pity withhold you in their case, in a punishment prescribed by Allah, if you believe in Allah and the Last Day. And let a party of the believers witness their punishment.

# 2794

The Zani marries not but a Zaniyah or a Mushrikah; and the Zaniyah, none marries her except a Zani or a Mushrik. Such a thing is forbidden to the believers.

# 2795

And those who accuse chaste women, and produce not four witnesses, flog them with eighty stripes, and reject their testimony forever. They indeed are the rebellious.

# 2796

Except those who repent thereafter and do righteous deeds; (for such) verily, Allah is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 2797

And for those who accuse their wives, but have no witnesses except themselves, let the testimony of one of them be four testimonies by Allah that he is one of those who speak the truth.

# 2798

And the fifth (testimony); invoking of the curse of Allah on him if he be of those who tell a lie.

# 2799

But she shall avert the punishment from her, if she bears witness four times by Allah, that he is telling a lie.

# 2800

And the fifth; should be that the wrath of Allah be upon her if he speaks the truth.

# 2801

And had it not been for the grace of Allah and His mercy on you! And that Allah is the One Who forgives and accepts repentance, the All-Wise.

# 2802

Verily, those who brought forth the slander are a group among you. Consider it not a bad thing for you. Nay, it is good for you. Unto every man among them will be paid that which he had earned of the sin, and as for him among them who had the greater share therein, his will be a great torment.

# 2803

Why then, did not the believers, men and women, when you heard it, think good of their own people and say: "This is an obvious lie"

# 2804

Why did they not produce four witnesses against him Since they have not produced witnesses! Then with Allah, they are the liars.

# 2805

Had it not been for the grace of Allah and His mercy unto you in this world and in the Hereafter, a great torment would have touched you for that whereof you had spoken.

# 2806

When you were propagating it with your tongues, and uttering with your mouths that whereof you had no knowledge, you counted it a little thing, while with Allah it was very great.

# 2807

And why did you not, when you heard it, say: "It is not right for us to speak of this. Glory be to You (O Allah)! This is a great lie."

# 2808

Allah forbids you from it and warns you not to repeat the like of it forever, if you are believers.

# 2809

And Allah makes the Ayat plain to you, and Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.

# 2810

Verily, those who like that Fahishah should be circulated among those who believe, they will have a painful torment in this world and in the Hereafter. And Allah knows and you know not.

# 2811

And had it not been for the grace of Allah and His mercy on you, and that Allah is full of kindness, Most Merciful.

# 2812

O you who believe! Follow not the Khutuwat of Shaytan. And whosoever follows the footsteps of Shaytan, then, verily, he commands Al-Fahsha' and the evil deeds. And had it not been for the grace of Allah and His mercy on you, not one of you would ever have been pure from sins. But Allah purifies whom He wills, and Allah is All-Hearer, All-Knower.

# 2813

And let not those among you who are blessed with graces and wealth swear not to give to their kinsmen, the poor, and those who left their homes for Allah's cause. Let them pardon and forgive. Do you not love that Allah should forgive you And Allah is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 2814

Verily, those who accuse chaste believing women, who never even think of anything touching their chastity and are good believers -- are cursed in this life and in the Hereafter, and for them will be a great torment.

# 2815

On the Day when their tongues, their hands, and their legs will bear witness against them as to what they used to do.

# 2816

On that Day Allah will pay them the recompense of their deeds in full, and they will know that Allah, He is the Manifest Truth.

# 2817

Bad statements are for bad people and bad people for bad statements. Good statements are for good people and good people for good statements: such are innocent of (every) bad statement which they say; for them is forgiveness, and honored provision.

# 2818

O you who believe! Enter not houses other than your own, until you have asked permission and greeted those in them; that is better for you, in order that you may remember.

# 2819

And if you find no one therein, still enter not until permission has been given. And if you are asked to go back, go back, for it is purer for you. And Allah is All-Knower of what you do.

# 2820

There is no sin on you that you enter houses uninhabited, you have any interest in them. And Allah has knowledge of what you reveal and what you conceal.

# 2821

Tell the believing men to lower their gaze, and protect their private parts. That is purer for them. Verily, Allah is All-Aware of what they do.

# 2822

And tell the believing women to lower their gaze, and protect their private parts and not to show off their adornment except that which is apparent, and to draw their veils all over their Juyub and not to reveal their adornment except to their husbands, or their fathers, or their husband's fathers, or their sons, or their husband's sons, or their brothers or their brother's sons, or their sister's sons, or their women, or their right hand possessions, or the Tabi\`in among men who do not have desire, or children who are not aware of the nakedness of women. And let them not stamp their feet so as to reveal what they hide of their adornment. And all of you beg Allah to forgive you all, O believers, that you may be successful.

# 2823

And marry those among you who are single (Al-Ayama) and the pious of your servants and maidservants. If they be poor, Allah will enrich them out of His bounty. And Allah is All-Sufficent, All-Knowing.

# 2824

And let those who find not the financial means for marriage keep themselves chaste, until Allah enriches them of His bounty. And such of your servants as seek a writing (of emancipation), give them such writing, if you find that there is good and honesty in them. And give them something (yourselves) out of the wealth of Allah which He has bestowed upon you. And force not your slave-girls to prostitution, if they desire chastity, in order that you may make a gain in the goods of this worldly life. But if anyone compels them, then after such compulsion, Allah is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 2825

And indeed We have sent down for you Ayat that make things plain, and the example of those who passed away before you, and an admonition for those who have Taqwa.

# 2826

Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth. The parable of His Light is as a niche and within it a lamp: the lamp is in a glass, the glass as it were a star Durriyyun, lit from a blessed tree, an olive, neither of the east nor of the west, whose oil would almost glow forth, though no fire touched it. Light upon Light! Allah guides to His Light whom He wills. And Allah sets forth parables for mankind, and Allah is All-Knower of everything.

# 2827

In houses which Allah has ordered to be raised, in them His Name is remembered. Therein glorify Him in the mornings and in the evenings,

# 2828

Men whom neither trade nor business diverts from the remembrance of Allah nor from performing the Salah nor from giving the Zakah. They fear a Day when hearts and eyes will be overturned.

# 2829

That Allah may reward them according to the best of their deeds, and add even more for them out of His grace. And Allah provides without measure to whom He wills.

# 2830

As for those who disbelieved, their deeds are like a mirage in a Qi\`ah. The thirsty one thinks it to be water until he comes up to it, he finds it to be nothing; but he finds Allah with him, Who will pay him his due. And Allah is swift in taking account.

# 2831

Or like the darkness in a vast deep sea, overwhelmed with waves topped by waves, topped by dark clouds, (layers of) darkness upon darkness: if a man stretches out his hand, he can hardly see it! And he for whom Allah has not appointed light, for him there is no light.

# 2832

See you not that Allah, He it is Whom glorify whosoever is in the heavens and the earth, and the birds with wings outspread Of each one He knows indeed his Salah and his glorification; and Allah is All-Aware of what they do.

# 2833

And to Allah belongs the sovereignty of the heavens and the earth, and to Allah is the return.

# 2834

See you not that Allah drives the clouds gently, then joins them together, then makes them into a heap of layers, and you see the rain come forth from between them; and He sends down from the sky, from mountains in it of ice, and strikes therewith whom He wills, and averts it from whom He wills. The vivid flash of its (clouds) lightning nearly blinds the sight.

# 2835

Allah causes the night and the day to succeed each other. Truly, in this is indeed a lesson for those who have insight.

# 2836

Allah has created every moving creature from water. Of them there are some that creep on their bellies, and some that walk on two legs, and some that walk on four. Allah creates what He wills. Verily, Allah is able to do all things.

# 2837

We have indeed sent down manifest Ayat. And Allah guides whom He wills to the straight path.

# 2838

They say: "We have believed in Allah and in the Messenger, and we obey," then a party of them turn away thereafter, such are not believers.

# 2839

And when they are called to Allah and His Messenger, to judge between them, lo! a party of them refuses and turns away.

# 2840

But if the truth is on their side, they come to him willingly with submission.

# 2841

Is there a disease in their hearts Or do they doubt or fear lest Allah and His Messenger should wrong them in judgement. Nay, it is they themselves who are the wrongdoers.

# 2842

The only saying of the faithful believers, when they are called to Allah and His Messenger, to judge between them, is that they say: "We hear and we obey." And such are the successful.

# 2843

And whosoever obeys Allah and His Messenger, fears Allah, and has Taqwa of Him, such are the successful.

# 2844

They swear by Allah their strongest oaths that if only you would order them, they would leave. Say: "Swear you not; obedience is known. Verily, Allah knows well what you do."

# 2845

Say: "Obey Allah and obey the Messenger, but if you turn away, he is only responsible for the duty placed on him and you for that placed on you. If you obey him, you shall be on the right guidance. The Messenger's duty is only to convey (the Message) in a clear way.") Allah says about the hypocrites who had promised the Messenger and sworn that if he were to command them to go out for battle, they would go:

# 2846

Allah has promised those among you who believe and do righteous good deeds, that He will certainly grant them succession in the land, as He granted it to those before them, and that He will grant them the authority to practise their religion which He has chosen for them. And He will surely give them in exchange a safe security after their fear if they worship Me and do not associate anything with Me. But whoever disbelieved after this, they are the rebellious.

# 2847

And perform the Salah, and give the Zakah and obey the Messenger that you may receive mercy.

# 2848

Consider not that the disbelievers can escape in the land. Their abode shall be the Fire -- and worst indeed is that destination.

# 2849

O you who believe! Let your slaves and slave-girls, and those among you who have not come to the age of puberty ask your permission on three occasions: before the Fajr prayer, and while you put off your clothes during the afternoon, and after the \`Isha' prayer. (These) three (times) are of privacy for you; other than these times there is no sin on you or on them to move about, attending to each other. Thus Allah makes clear the Ayat to you. And Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.

# 2850

And when the children among you come to puberty, then let them (also) ask for permission, as those senior to them (in age) ask permission. Thus Allah makes clear His Ayat for you. And Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.

# 2851

And the Qawa\`id among women who do not hope for marriage, it is no sin on them if they discard their (outer) clothing in such a way as not to show their adornment. But to refrain is better for them. And Allah is All-Hearer, All-Knower.

# 2852

There is no restriction on the blind, nor any restriction on the lame, nor any restriction on the sick, nor on yourselves, if you eat from your houses, or the houses of your fathers, or the houses of your mothers, or the houses of your brothers, or the houses of your sisters, or the houses of your father's brothers, or the houses of your father's sisters, or the houses of your mother's brothers, or the houses of your mother's sisters, or (from that) whereof you hold keys, or (from the house) of a friend. No sin on you whether you eat together or apart. But when you enter the houses, greet one another with a greeting from Allah, blessed and good. Thus Allah makes clear the Ayat to you that you may understand.

# 2853

The believers are only those who believe in Allah and His Messenger; and when they are with him on some common matter, they go not away until they have asked his permission. Verily, those who ask your permission, those are they who (really) believe in Allah and His Messenger. So if they ask your permission for some affairs of theirs, give permission to whom you will of them, and ask Allah for their forgiveness. Truly, Allah is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 2854

Make not the calling of the Messenger among you as your calling one of another. Allah knows those of you who slip away under shelter. And let those beware who oppose the Messenger's commandment, lest some Fitnah should befall them or a painful torment be inflicted on them.

# 2855

Certainly, to Allah belongs all that is in the heavens and the earth. Indeed, He knows your condition and the Day when they will be brought back to Him, then He will inform them of what they did. And Allah is All-Knower of everything.

# 2856

Blessed be He Who sent down (Nazzala) the criterion to His servant that he may be a warner to all nations.

# 2857

He to Whom belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth, and Who has begotten no son and for Whom there is no partner in the dominion. He has created everything, and has measured it exactly according to its due measurements.

# 2858

Yet they have taken besides Him other gods who created nothing but are themselves created, and possess neither harm nor benefit for themselves, and possess no power (of causing) death, nor (of giving) life, nor of raising the dead.

# 2859

Those who disbelieve say: "This is nothing but a lie that he has invented, and others have helped him in it." In fact, they have produced an unjust wrong and a lie.

# 2860

And they say: "Tales of the ancients which he has written down, and they are dictated to him morning and afternoon. "

# 2861

Say: "It has been sent down by Him Who knows the secret of the heavens and the earth. Truly, He is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful."

# 2862

And they say: "Why does this Messenger eat food, and walk about in the markets. Why is not an angel sent down to him to be a warner with him"

# 2863

"Or (why) has not a treasure been granted to him, or why has he not a garden whereof he may eat" And the wrongdoers say: "You follow none but a man bewitched."

# 2864

See how they coin similitudes for you, so they have gone astray, and they cannot find a path.

# 2865

Blessed be He Who, if He wills, will assign you better than (all) that -- Gardens under which rivers flow and will assign you palaces.

# 2866

Nay, they deny the Hour, and for those who deny the Hour, We have prepared a flaming Fire.

# 2867

When it sees them from a far place, they will hear its raging and its roaring.

# 2868

And when they shall be thrown into a narrow place thereof, chained together, they will exclaim therein for destruction.

# 2869

Exclaim not today for one destruction, but exclaim for many destructions.

# 2870

Say: "Is that better or the Paradise of Eternity which is promised to those who have Taqwa" It will be theirs as a reward and final destination.

# 2871

For them there will be therein all that they desire, and they will abide (therein forever). It is upon your Lord a Wa\`dan Mas'ula.

# 2872

And on the Day when He will gather them together and that which they worship besides Allah. He will say: "Was it you who misled these My servants or did they stray from the path"

# 2873

They will say: "Glorified be You! It was not for us to take any Awliya' besides You, but You gave them and their fathers comfort till they forgot the warning, and became a lost people."

# 2874

Thus they will deny you in what you say; then you can neither avert nor find help. And whoever among you does wrong, We shall make him taste a great torment.

# 2875

And We never sent before you any of the Messengers but verily, they ate food and walked in the markets. And We have made some of you as a trial for others; will you have patience And your Lord is Ever All-Seer.

# 2876

And those who expect not a meeting with Us said: "Why are not the angels sent down to us, or why do we not see our Lord" Indeed they think too highly of themselves, and are scornful with great pride.

# 2877

On the Day they will see the angels -- no good news will there be for the criminals that day. And they will say: "Hijran Mahjura."

# 2878

And We shall turn to whatever deeds they did, and We shall make such deeds as scattered floating particles of dust.

# 2879

The dwellers of Paradise will, on that Day, have the best abode, and have the fairest of places for repose.

# 2880

And (remember) the Day when the heaven shall be rent asunder with clouds, and the angels will be sent down, with a grand descending.

# 2881

The sovereignty on that Day will be the true (sovereignty) of the Most Gracious, and it will be a hard Day for the disbelievers.

# 2882

And (remember) the Day when the wrongdoer will bite at his hands, he will say: "Oh! Would that I had taken a path with the Messenger."

# 2883

"Ah! Woe to me! Would that I had never taken so-and-so as an intimate friend!"

# 2884

"He indeed led me astray from the Reminder after it had come to me. And Shaytan is to man ever a deserter."

# 2885

And the Messenger will say: "O my Lord! Verily, my people deserted this Qur'an."

# 2886

Thus have We made for every Prophet an enemy among the criminals. But sufficient is your Lord as a Guide and Helper.

# 2887

And those who disbelieve say: "Why is not the Qur'an revealed to him all at once" Thus, that We may strengthen your heart thereby. And We have revealed it to you gradually, in stages.

# 2888

And no example or parable do they bring, but We reveal to you the truth, and the better explanation thereof.

# 2889

Those who will be gathered to Hell on their faces, such will be in an evil state, and most astray from the path.

# 2890

And indeed We gave Musa the Scripture, and placed his brother Harun with him as a helper;

# 2891

And We said: "Go you both to the people who have denied Our Ayat." Then We destroyed them with utter destruction.

# 2892

And Nuh's people, when they denied the Messengers, We drowned them, and We made them as a sign for mankind. And We have prepared a painful torment for the wrongdoers.

# 2893

And (also) \`Ad and Thamud, and the Dwellers of Ar-Rass, and many generations in between.

# 2894

And for each We put forward examples, and each We brought to utter ruin.

# 2895

And indeed they have passed by the town on which was rained the evil rain. Did they not then see it Nay! But they used not to expect any resurrection.

# 2896

And when they see you, they treat you only in mockery (saying): "Is this the one whom Allah has sent as a Messenger"

# 2897

"He would have nearly misled us from our gods, had it not been that we were patient and constant in their worship!" And they will know, when they see the torment, who it is that is most astray from the path!

# 2898

Have you seen him who has taken as his god his own vain desire Would you then be a guardian over him

# 2899

Or do you think that most of them hear or understand They are only like cattle -- nay, they are even farther astray from the path.

# 2900

Have you not seen how your Lord spread the shadow. If He willed, He could have made it still -- but We have made the sun its guide.

# 2901

Then We withdraw it towards Ourselves -- a gradual withdrawal.

# 2902

And it is He Who makes the night a covering for you, and the sleep (as) a repose, and makes the day Nushur.

# 2903

And it is He Who sends the winds as heralds of glad tidings, going before His mercy; and We send down pure water from the sky,

# 2904

That We may give life thereby to a dead land, and We give to drink thereof many of the cattle and men that We have created.

# 2905

And indeed We have distributed it among them in order that they may remember the grace of Allah, but most men refuse (out of) gratitude.

# 2906

And had We willed, We would have raised a warner in every town.

# 2907

So obey not the disbelievers, but strive against them with the utmost endeavor with it.

# 2908

And it is He Who has let free the two seas, this is palatable and sweet, and that is salty and bitter; and He has set a barrier and a complete partition between them.

# 2909

And it is He Who has created man from water, and has appointed for him kindred by blood, and kindred by marriage. And your Lord is Ever All-Powerful to do what He wills.

# 2910

And they worship besides Allah, that which can neither profit them nor harm them; and the disbeliever is ever a helper against his Lord.

# 2911

And We have sent you only as a bearer of good news and a warner.

# 2912

Say: "No reward do I ask of you for this, save that whosoever wills may take a path to his Lord."

# 2913

And put your trust in the Ever Living One Who dies not, and glorify His praises, and sufficient is He as the All-Knower of the sins of His servants,

# 2914

Who created the heavens and the earth and all that is between them in six Days. Then He rose over (Istawa) the Throne. The Most Gracious! Ask Him, as He is the All-Knower.

# 2915

And when it is said to them: "Prostrate yourselves to Ar-Rahman!" They say: "And what is Ar-Rahman Shall we fall down in prostration to that which you command us" And it increases in them only aversion.

# 2916

Blessed be He Who has placed in the heaven Al-Buruj, and has placed therein a great lamp, and a moon giving light.

# 2917

And He it is Who has put the night and the day in succession (Khilfatan), for such who desires to remember or desires to show his gratitude.

# 2918

And the servants of the Most Gracious are those who walk on the earth Hawna, and when the foolish address them they say; "Salama."

# 2919

And those who spend the night in worship of their Lord, prostrate and standing.

# 2920
