And those who say: "Our Lord! Avert from us the torment of Hell. Verily, its torment is ever an inseparable, permanent punishment."

# 2921

Evil indeed it is as an abode and as a place to rest in.

# 2922

And those who, when they spend, are neither extravagant nor stingy, but are in a just balance between them.

# 2923

And those who invoke not any other god along with Allah, nor kill such person as Allah has forbidden, except for just cause, nor commit illegal sexual intercourse -- and whoever does this shall receive Athama.

# 2924

The torment will be doubled for him on the Day of Resurrection, and he will abide therein in disgrace;

# 2925

Except those who repent and believe, and do righteous deeds; for those, Allah will change their sins into good deeds, and Allah is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 2926

And whosoever repents and does righteous good deeds; then indeed he has repented to Allah Mataba.

# 2927

And those who do not bear witness to falsehood, and if they pass by some evil play or evil talk, they pass by it with dignity.

# 2928

And those who, when they are reminded of the Ayat of their Lord, fall not deaf and blind thereat.

# 2929

And those who say: "Our Lord! Bestow on us from our wives and our offspring the comfort of our eyes, and make us leaders of those who have Taqwa."

# 2930

Those will be rewarded with the highest place because of their patience. Therein they shall be met with greetings and the word of peace and respect.

# 2931

Abiding therein -- excellent it is as an abode, and as a place to rest in.

# 2932

Say: "My Lord pays attention to you only because of your invocation to Him. But now you have indeed denied. So the torment will be yours forever."

# 2933

Ta Sin Mim.

# 2934

These are Ayat of the Book Mubin.

# 2935

It may be that you are going Bakhi\` yourself, that they do not become believers.

# 2936

If We will, We could send down to them from the heaven a sign, to which they would bend their necks in humility.

# 2937

And never comes there unto them a Reminder as a recent revelation from the Most Gracious, but they turn away therefrom.

# 2938

So, they have indeed denied, then the news of what they mocked at will come to them.

# 2939

Do they not observe the earth -- how much of every good kind We cause to grow therein

# 2940

Verily, in this is an Ayah, yet most of them are not believers.

# 2941

And verily your Lord, He is truly the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful.

# 2942

And (remember) when your Lord called Musa (saying): "Go to the people who are wrongdoers."

# 2943

"The people of Fira\`wn. Will they not have Taqwa"

# 2944

He said: "My Lord! Verily, I fear that they will deny me,"

# 2945

"And my breast straitens, and my tongue expresses not well. So send for Harun."

# 2946

"And they have a charge of crime against me, and I fear they will kill me. "

# 2947

(Allah) said: "Nay! Go you both with Our signs. Verily, We shall be with you, listening."

# 2948

"And go both of you to Fira\`wn, and say: \`We are the Messengers of the Lord of Al-\`Alamin,'

# 2949

\`So allow the Children of Israel to go with us."'

# 2950

(Fir\`awn) said (to Musa): "Did we not bring you up among us as a child And you did dwell many years of your life with us."

# 2951

"And you did your deed, which you did. While you were one of the ingrates."

# 2952

Musa said: "I did it then, when I was in error."

# 2953

"So, I fled from you when I feared you. But my Lord has granted me Hukm, and made me one of the Messengers."

# 2954

"And this is the past favor with which you reproach me, -- that you have enslaved the Children of Israel."

# 2955

Fir\`awn said: "And what is the Lord of Al-\`Alamin"

# 2956

(Musa) said: "The Lord of the heavens and the earth, and all that is between them, if you seek to be convinced with certainty."

# 2957

(Fir\`awn) said to those around: "Do you not hear (what he says)"

# 2958

(Musa) said: "Your Lord and the Lord of your ancient fathers!"

# 2959

(Fir\`awn) said: "Verily, your Messenger who has been sent to you is a madman!"

# 2960

(Musa) said: "Lord of the east and the west, and all that is between them, if you did but understand!"

# 2961

He said: "If you choose a god other than me, I will certainly put you among the prisoners."

# 2962

He said: "Even if I bring you something manifest"

# 2963

He said: "Bring it forth then, if you are of the truthful!"

# 2964

So he threw his stick, and behold, it was a serpent, manifest.

# 2965

And he drew out his hand, and behold, it was white to all beholders!

# 2966

He said to the chiefs around him: "Verily, this is indeed a well-versed sorcerer."

# 2967

"He wants to drive you out of your land by his sorcery: what is it then that you command"

# 2968

They said: "Put him off and his brother (for a while), and send callers to the cities;"

# 2969

"To bring up to you every well-versed sorcerer."

# 2970

So, the sorcerers were assembled at a fixed time on a day appointed.

# 2971

And it was said to the people: "Are you (too) going to assemble"

# 2972

"That we may follow the sorcerers if they are the winners."

# 2973

So, when the sorcerers arrived, they said to Fir\`awn: "Will there surely be a reward for us if we are the winners"

# 2974

He said: "Yes, and you shall then verily be of those brought near (to myself)."

# 2975

Musa said to them: "Throw what you are going to throw!"

# 2976

So, they threw their ropes and their sticks, and said: "By the might of Fir\`awn, it is we who will certainly win!"

# 2977

Then Musa threw his stick, and behold, it swallowed up all that they falsely showed!

# 2978

And the sorcerers fell down prostrate.

# 2979

Saying: "We believe in the Lord of Al-\`Alamin."

# 2980

"The Lord of Musa and Harun."

# 2981

He said: "You have believed in him before I give you leave. Surely, he indeed is your chief, who has taught you magic! So verily, you shall come to know. Verily, I will cut off your hands and your feet on opposite sides, and I will crucify you all."

# 2982

They said: "No harm! Surely, to our Lord we are to return."

# 2983

"Verily, we really hope that our Lord will forgive us our sins, as we are the first of the believers."

# 2984

And We revealed to Musa, saying: "Depart by night with My servants, verily, you will be pursued."

# 2985

Then Fir\`awn sent callers to (all) the cities.

# 2986

(Saying): "Verily, these indeed are but a small band."

# 2987

"And verily, they have done what has enraged us."

# 2988

"But we are a host all assembled, amply forewarned."

# 2989

So, We expelled them from gardens and springs,

# 2990

Treasures, and every kind of honorable place.

# 2991

Thus and We caused the Children of Israel to inherit them.

# 2992

So, they pursued them at sunrise.

# 2993

And when the two hosts saw each other, the companions of Musa said: "We are sure to be overtaken."

# 2994

(Musa) said: "Nay, verily with me is my Lord. He will guide me."

# 2995

Then We revealed to Musa (saying): "Strike the sea with your stick." And it parted, and each separate part became like huge mountain.

# 2996

Then We brought near the others to that place.

# 2997

And We saved Musa and all those with him.

# 2998

Then We drowned the others.

# 2999

Verily, in this is indeed a sign, yet most of them are not believers.

# 3000

And verily your Lord, He is truly the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful.

# 3001

And recite to them the story of Ibrahim.

# 3002

When he said to his father and his people: "What do you worship"

# 3003

They said: "We worship idols, and to them we are ever devoted."

# 3004

He said: "Do they hear you when you call"

# 3005

"Or do they benefit you or do they cause harm"

# 3006

They said: "(Nay) but we found our fathers doing so."

# 3007

He said: "Do you observe that which you have been worshipping --"

# 3008

"You and your ancient fathers"

# 3009

"Verily, they are enemies to me, save the Lord of Al-\`Alamin,"

# 3010

Who has created me, and it is He Who guides me.

# 3011

And it is He Who feeds me and gives me to drink.

# 3012

And when I am ill, it is He Who cures me.

# 3013

And Who will cause me to die, and then will bring me to life.

# 3014

And Who, I hope, will forgive me my faults on the Day of Recompense.

# 3015

My Lord! Bestow Hukm on me, and join me with the righteous.

# 3016

And grant me an honorable mention in later generations.

# 3017

And make me one of the inheritors of the Paradise of Delight.

# 3018

And forgive my father, verily, he is of the erring.

# 3019

And disgrace me not on the Day when they will be resurrected.

# 3020

The Day whereon neither wealth nor sons will avail,

# 3021

Except him who brings to Allah a clean heart.

# 3022

And Paradise will be brought near to those who had Taqwa.

# 3023

And the (Hell) Fire will be placed in full view of the astray.

# 3024

And it will be said to them: "Where are those that you used to worship."

# 3025

"Instead of Allah Can they help you or help themselves"

# 3026

Then they will be thrown on their faces into it (the Fire), they and the astray.

# 3027

And all of the hosts of Iblis together.

# 3028

They will say while contending therein,

# 3029

"By Allah, we were truly in a manifest error,

# 3030

"When we held you as equals with the Lord of all that exists;"

# 3031

"And none has brought us into error except the criminals."

# 3032

"Now we have no intercessors,"

# 3033

"Nor a close friend."

# 3034

"(Alas!) If we only had a chance to return, we shall truly be among the believers!"

# 3035

Verily, in this is indeed a sign, yet most of them are not believers.

# 3036

And verily your Lord, He is truly the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful.

# 3037

The people of Nuh denied the Messengers.

# 3038

When their brother Nuh said to them: "Will you not have Taqwa"

# 3039

"I am a trustworthy Messenger to you."

# 3040

"So have Taqwa of Allah, and obey me."

# 3041

"No reward do I ask of you for it; my reward is only from the Lord of all that exists."

# 3042

"So have Taqwa of Allah, and obey me."

# 3043

They said: "Shall we believe in you, when the inferior follow you"

# 3044

He said: "And what knowledge have I of what they used to do"

# 3045

"Their account is only with my Lord, if you could (but) know."

# 3046

"And I am not going to drive away the believers."

# 3047

"I am only a plain warner."

# 3048

They said: "If you cease not, O Nuh you will surely be among those stoned."

# 3049

He said: "My Lord! Verily, my people have denied me."

# 3050

"Therefore judge You between me and them, and save me and those of the believers who are with me."

# 3051

And We saved him and those with him in the laden ship.

# 3052

Then We drowned the rest thereafter.

# 3053

Verily, in this is indeed a sign, yet most of them are not believers.

# 3054

And verily your Lord, He is indeed the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful.

# 3055

\`Ad denied the Messengers.

# 3056

When their brother Hud said to them: "Will you not have Taqwa"

# 3057

"Verily, I am a trustworthy Messenger to you."

# 3058

"So, have Taqwa of Allah, and obey me."

# 3059

"No reward do I ask of you for it; my reward is only from the Lord of all that exists."

# 3060

"Do you build on every Ri\` an Ayah for your amusement"

# 3061

"And do you get for yourselves Masani\` as if you will live therein forever"

# 3062

"And when you seize (somebody), seize you (him) as tyrants"

# 3063

"So have Taqwa of Allah, and obey me."

# 3064

"And have Taqwa of Him, fear Him Who has aided you with all (good things) that you know."

# 3065

# 3066

# 3067

"Verily, I fear for you the torment of a Great Day."

# 3068

# 3069

# 3070

# 3071

So they denied him, and We destroyed them. Verily, in this is indeed a sign, yet most of them are not believers.

# 3072

When their brother Salih said to them: "Will you not have Taqwa"

# 3075

# 3076

"So, have Taqwa of Allah, and obey me."

# 3077

# 3078

# 3079

"In gardens and springs."

# 3080

"And crops and date palms with soft clusters."

# 3081

"And you hew out in the mountains, houses with great skill."

# 3082

"So, have Taqwa of Allah, and obey me."

# 3083

# 3084

Who make mischief in the land, and reform not."

# 3085

They said: "You are only of those bewitched!"

# 3086

"You are but a human being like us. Then bring us a sign if you are of the truthful."

# 3087

He said: "Here is a she-camel: it has a right to drink (water), and you have a right to drink (water) (each) on a day, known."

# 3088

"And touch her not with harm, lest the torment of a Great Day should seize you."

# 3089

But they killed her, and then they became regretful.

# 3090

So, the torment overtook them. Verily, in this is indeed a sign, yet most of them are not believers.

# 3091

And verily, your Lord He is indeed the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful.

# 3092

The people of Lut denied the Messengers.

# 3093

When their brother Lut said to them: "Will you not have Taqwa"

# 3094

"Verily, I am a trustworthy Messenger to you."

# 3095

"So, have Taqwa of Allah, and obey me."

# 3096

# 3097

# 3098

# 3099

They said: "If you cease not, O Lut, verily, you will be one of those who are driven out!"

# 3100

He said: "I am indeed of those who disapprove with severe anger and fury your behavior."

# 3101

"My Lord! Save me and my family from what they do."

# 3102

So, We saved him and his family, all,

# 3103

Except an old woman among those who remained behind.

# 3104

Then afterward We destroyed the others.

# 3105

And We rained on them a rain, and how evil was the rain of those who had been warned!

# 3106

Verily, in this is indeed a sign, yet most of them are not believers.

# 3107

# 3109

"I am a trustworthy Messenger to you."

# 3112

# 3113

"Give full measure, and cause no loss (to others)."

# 3114

"And weigh with the true and straight balance."

# 3115

"And defraud not people by reducing their things, nor do evil, making corruption and mischief in the land."

# 3116

"And have Taqwa of Him Who created you and the generations of the men of old."

# 3117

They said: "You are only one of those bewitched!"

# 3118

"You are but a human being like us and verily, we think that you are one of the liars!"

# 3119

"So, cause a piece of the heaven to fall on us, if you are of the truthful!"

# 3120

He said: "My Lord is the Best Knower of what you do."

# 3121

But they denied him, so the torment of the Day of Shadow (a gloomy cloud) seized them. Indeed that was the torment of a Great Day.

# 3122

Verily, in this is indeed a sign, yet most of them are not believers.

# 3123

And verily your Lord, He is indeed the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful.

# 3124

And truly, this is a revelation from the Lord of all that exists,

# 3125

Which the trustworthy Ruh (Jibril) has brought down.

# 3126

Upon your heart that you may be (one) of the warners,

# 3127

In the plain Arabic language.

# 3128

And verily, it is in the Zubur of the former people.

# 3129

Is it not a sign to them that the learned scholars of the Children of Israel knew it

# 3130

And if We had revealed it unto any of the non-Arabs,

# 3131

And he had recited it unto them, they would not have believed in it.

# 3132

Thus have We caused it to enter the hearts of the criminals.

# 3133

They will not believe in it until they see the painful torment.

# 3134

It shall come to them of a sudden, while they perceive it not.

# 3135

Then they will say: "Can we be respited"

# 3136

Would they then wish for Our torment to be hastened on

# 3137

Think, if We do let them enjoy for years,

# 3138

And afterwards comes to them that which they had been promised.

# 3139

All that with which they used to enjoy shall not avail them.

# 3140

And never did We destroy a township but it had its warners

# 3141

By way of reminder, and We have never been unjust.

# 3142

And it is not the Shayatin (devils) who have brought it down.

# 3143

Neither would it suit them nor are they able.

# 3144

Verily, they have been removed far from hearing it.

# 3145

So, invoke not with Allah another god lest you should be among those who receive punishment.

# 3146

And warn your tribe of near kindred.

# 3147

And be kind and humble to the believers who follow you.

# 3148

Then if they disobey you, say: "I am innocent of what you do."

# 3149

And put your trust in the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful,

# 3150

Who sees you when you stand up.

# 3151

And your movements among those who fall prostrate.

# 3152

Verily, He, only He, is the All-Hearer, the All-Knower.

# 3153

Shall I inform you upon whom the Shayatin descend

# 3154

They descend on every lying, sinful person (Athim).

# 3155

Who gives ear, and most of them are liars.

# 3156

As for the poets, the astray follow them,

# 3157

See you not that they speak about every subject in their poetry

# 3158

And that they say what they do not do.

# 3159

Except those who believe and do righteous deeds, and remember Allah much and vindicate themselves after they have been wronged. And those who do wrong will come to know by what overturning they will be overturned.

# 3160

Ta Sin. These are the Ayat of the Qur'an, and (it is) a Book (that is) clear.

# 3161

A guide and glad tidings for the believers.

# 3162

Those who perform the Salah and give the Zakah and they believe with certainty in the Hereafter.

# 3163

Verily, those who believe not in the Hereafter, We have made their deeds fair seeming to them, so that they wander about blindly.

# 3164

They are those for whom there will be an evil torment. And in the Hereafter they will be the greatest losers.

# 3165

And verily, you are being taught the Qur'an from One, All-Wise, All-Knowing.

# 3166

(Remember) when Musa said to his household: "Verily, I have seen a fire; I will bring you from there some information, or I will bring you a burning ember, that you may warm yourselves."

# 3167

But when he came to it, he was called: "Blessed is whosoever is in the fire, and whosoever is round about it! And glorified be Allah, the Lord of all that exists."

# 3168

"O Musa! Verily, it is I, Allah, the All-Mighty, the All-Wise."

# 3169

"And throw down your stick!" But when he saw it moving as if it were a snake, he turned in flight, and did not look back. (It was said:) "O Musa! Fear not: verily, the Messengers fear not in front of Me."

# 3170

"Except him who has done wrong and afterwards has changed evil for good; then surely, I am Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful."

# 3171

"And put your hand into opening of your garment, it will come forth white without hurt. (These are) among the nine signs (you will take) to Fir\`awn and his people. Verily, they are a people who are rebellious."

# 3172

But when Our Ayat came to them, clear to see, they said: "This is a manifest magic."

# 3173

And they belied them wrongfully and arrogantly, though they themselves were convinced thereof. So, see what was the end of the mischief-makers.

# 3174

And indeed We gave knowledge to Dawud and Sulayman, and they both said: "All praise be to Allah, Who has preferred us above many of His believing servants!"

# 3175

And Sulayman inherited from Dawud. He said: "O mankind! We have been taught the language of birds, and we have been given from everything. This, verily, is an evident grace."

# 3176

And there were gathered before Sulayman his hosts of Jinn and men, and birds, and they all were set in battle order (marching forward).

# 3177

Till, when they came to the valley of the ants, one of the ants said: "O ants! Enter your dwellings, lest Sulayman and his armies should crush you, while they perceive not."

# 3178

So he (Sulayman) smiled, amused at her speech and said: "My Lord! Grant me the power and ability that I may be grateful for Your favors which You have bestowed on me and on my parents, and that I may do righteous good deeds that will please You, and admit me by Your mercy among Your righteous servants."

# 3179

He inspected the birds, and said: "What is the matter that I see not the hoopoe Or is he among the absentees"

# 3180

"I will surely punish him with a severe torment or slaughter him, unless he brings me a clear reason."

# 3181

But (the hoopoe) stayed not long, he said: "I have grasped which you have not grasped and I have come to you from Saba' with true news."

# 3182

"I found a woman ruling over them, she has been given all things, and she has a great throne."

# 3183

"I found her and her people worshipping the sun instead of Allah, and Shaytan has made their deeds fair seeming to them to prevent them from the way, so they have no guidance."

# 3184

So they do not prostrate themselves before Allah, Who brings to light what is hidden in the heavens and the earth, and knows what you conceal and what you reveal.

# 3185

Allah, La ilaha illa Huwa, the Lord of the Supreme Throne!"

# 3186

(Sulayman) said: "We shall see whether you speak the truth or you are (one) of the liars."

# 3187

"Go you with this letter of mine and deliver it to them, then draw back from them and see what they return."

# 3188

She said: "O chiefs! Verily, here is delivered to me a noble letter, "

# 3189

"Verily, it is from Sulayman, and it (reads): \`In the Name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful;'

# 3190

\`Be you not exalted against me, but come to me submitting (as Muslims).' "

# 3191

She said: "O chiefs! Advise me in case of mine. I decide no case till you are present with me."

# 3192

They said: "We have great strength, and great ability for war, but it is for you to command; so think over what you will command."

# 3193

She said: "Verily, kings, when they enter a town, they destroy it and make the most honorable among its people the lowest. And thus they do."

# 3194

"But verily, I am going to send him a present, and see with what (answer) the messengers return."

# 3195

So, when (the messengers with the gift) came to Sulayman, he said: "Will you help me in wealth What Allah has given me is better than that which He has given you! Nay, you rejoice in your gift!"

# 3196

"Go back to them. We verily, shall come to them with armies that they cannot resist, and we shall drive them out from there in disgrace, and they will be abased."

# 3197

He said: "O chiefs! Which of you can bring me her throne before they come to me surrendering themselves in obedience (as Muslims)"

# 3198

An \`Ifrit from the Jinn said: "I will bring it to you before you rise from your place. And verily, I am indeed strong and trustworthy for such work."

# 3199

One with whom was knowledge of the Scripture, said: "I will bring it to you within the twinkling of an eye!" Then when he saw it placed before him, he said: "This is by the grace of my Lord -- to test me whether I am grateful or ungrateful! And whoever is grateful, truly, his gratitude is for himself; and whoever is ungrateful, certainly my Lord is Rich, Bountiful."

# 3200

He said: "Disguise her throne for her that we may see whether she will be guided, or she will be one of those not guided."

# 3201

So when she came, it was said, "Is your throne like this" She said: "As though it were the very same." And he said, "Knowledge was bestowed on us before her, and we had submitted to Allah (as Muslims)."

# 3202

And Saddaha that which she used to worship besides Allah has prevented her (from Islam), for she was of a disbelieving people.

# 3203

It was said to her: "Enter As-Sarh," but when she saw it, she thought it was a pool, and she (tucked up her clothes) uncovering her legs. Sulayman said: "Verily, it is a Sarh Mumarrad of Qawarir." She said: "My Lord! Verily, I have wronged myself, and I submit, together with Sulayman to Allah, the Lord of all that exits."

# 3204

And indeed We sent to Thamud their brother Salih, (saying): "Worship Allah." Then look! They became two parties quarreling with each other.

# 3205

He said: "O my people! Why do you seek to hasten the evil before the good Why seek you not the forgiveness of Allah, that you may receive mercy"

# 3206

They said: "We augur an omen from you and those with you." He said: "Your omen is of Allah; nay, but you are a people that are being tested."

# 3207

And there were in the city nine Rahtin, who made mischief in the land, and would not reform.

# 3208

They said: "Swear one to another by Allah that we shall make a secret night attack on him and his household, and thereafter we will surely say to his near relatives: \`We witnessed not the destruction of his household, and verily, we are telling the truth."'

# 3209

So, they plotted a plot, and We planned a plan, while they perceived not.

# 3210

Then see how was the end of their plot! Verily, We destroyed them and their nation all together.

# 3211

These are their houses in utter ruin, for they did wrong. Verily, in this is indeed an Ayah for people who know.

# 3212

And We saved those who believed, and had Taqwa of Allah.

# 3213

And (remember) Lut! When he said to his people: "Do you commit immoral sins while you see"

# 3214

"Do you practice your lusts on men instead of women Nay, but you are a people who behave senselessly."

# 3215

There was no other answer given by his people except that they said: "Drive out the family of Lut from your city. Verily, these are men who want to be clean and pure!"

# 3216

So, We saved him and his family, except his wife. We destined her to be of those who remained behind.

# 3217

And We rained down on them a rain. So, evil was the rain of those who were warned.

# 3218

Say: "Praise and thanks be to Allah, and peace be on His servants whom He has chosen! Is Allah better, or what they ascribe as partners"

# 3219

Is not He Who created the heavens and the earth, and sends down for you water from the sky, whereby We cause to grow wonderful gardens full of beauty and delight It is not in your ability to cause the growth of their trees. Is there any god with Allah Nay, but they are a people who ascribe equals!

# 3220

Is not He Who has made the earth as a fixed abode, and has placed rivers in its midst, and has placed firm mountains therein, and has set a barrier between the two seas (of salt and sweet water) Is there any ilah (god) with Allah Nay, but most of them know not!

# 3221

Is not He Who responds to the distressed one, when he calls on Him, and Who removes the evil, and makes you inheritors of the earth, generations after generations Is there any god with Allah Little is that you remember!

# 3222

Is not He Who guides you in the darkness of the land and the sea, and Who sends the winds as heralds of glad tidings, going before His mercy Is there any god with Allah Exalted be Allah above all that they associate as partners!

# 3223

Is not He Who originates creation, and shall thereafter repeat it, and Who provides for you from heaven and earth Is there any god with Allah Say: "Bring forth your proofs, if you are truthful."

# 3224

Say: "None in the heavens and the earth knows the Unseen except Allah, nor can they perceive when they shall be resurrected."

# 3225

Nay, their knowledge will perceive that in the Hereafter. Nay, they are in doubt about it. Nay, they are in complete blindness about it.

# 3226

And those who disbelieve say: "When we have become dust -- we and our fathers -- shall we really be brought forth"

# 3227

"Indeed we were promised this -- we and our forefathers before, verily, these are nothing but tales of ancients."

# 3228

Say to them: "Travel in the land and see how has been the end of the criminals."

# 3229

And grieve you not over them, nor be straitened (in distress) because of what they plot.

# 3230

And they say: "When this promise, if you are truthful"

# 3231

Say: "Perhaps that which you wish to hasten on, may be close behind you."

# 3232

Verily, your Lord is full of grace for mankind, yet most of them do not give thanks.

# 3233

And verily, your Lord knows what their breasts conceal and what they reveal.

# 3234

And there is nothing hidden in the heaven and the earth but it is in a Clear Book.

# 3235

Verily, this Qur'an narrates to the Children of Israel most of that in which they differ.

# 3236

And truly, it is a guide and a mercy for the believers.

# 3237

Verily, your Lord will decide between them by His judgement. And He is the All-Mighty, the All-Knowing.

# 3238

So, put your trust in Allah; surely, you are on manifest truth.

# 3239

Verily, you cannot make the dead to hear nor can you make the deaf to hear the call, when they flee, turning their backs.

# 3240

Nor can you lead the blind out of their error. You can only make to hear those who believe in Our Ayat, so they submit (became Muslims).

# 3241

And when the Word is fulfilled against them, We shall bring out from the earth a beast for them, to speak to them because mankind believed not with certainty in Our Ayat.

# 3242

And (remember) the Day when We shall gather out of every nation a Fawj of those who denied Our Ayat, and they shall be driven,

# 3243

Till, when they come, He will say: "Did you deny My Ayat whereas you comprehended them not by knowledge, or what was it that you used to do"

# 3244

And the Word will be fulfilled against them, because they have done wrong, and they will be unable to speak.

# 3245

See they not that We have made the night for them to rest therein, and the day sight-giving Verily, in this are Ayat for the people who believe.

# 3246

And (remember) the Day on which the Trumpet (Sur) will be blown -- and all who are in the heavens and all who are on the earth, will be terrified except him whom Allah wills. And all shall come to Him, humbled.

# 3247

And you will see the mountains and think them solid, but they shall pass away as the passing away of the clouds. The work of Allah, Who perfected all things, verily, He is well-acquainted with what you do.

# 3248

Whoever brings a good deed, will have better than its worth; and they will be safe from the terror on that Day.

# 3249

And whoever brings an evil deed, they will be cast down on their faces in the Fire. (And it will be said to them) "Are you being recompensed anything except what you used to do"

# 3250

I have been commanded only to worship the Lord of this city, Who has sanctified it and to Whom belongs everything. And I am commanded to be from among the Muslims.

# 3251

And that I should recite the Qur'an, then whosoever receives guidance, receives it for the good of himself; and whosoever goes astray, say (to him): "I am only one of the warners."

# 3252

And say: "All the praises and thanks be to Allah. He will show you His Ayat, and you shall recognize them. And your Lord is not unaware of what you do."

# 3253

Ta Sin Mim

# 3254

These are the Ayat of the manifest Book.

# 3255

We recite to you some of the news of Musa and Fir\`awn in truth, for a people who believe.

# 3256

Verily, Fir\`awn exalted himself in the land and made its people Shiya\`a, weakening a group among them: killing their sons, and letting their females live. Verily, he was of the mischief-makers.

# 3257

And We wished to do a favor to those who were weak in the land, and to make them rulers and to make them the inheritors,

# 3258

And to establish them in the land, and We let Fir\`awn and Haman and their armies receive from them that which they feared.

# 3259

And We inspired the mother of Musa: "Suckle him (Musa), but when you fear for him, then cast him into the river and fear not, nor grieve. Verily, We shall bring him back to you, and shall make him one of the Messengers."

# 3260

Then the household of Fir\`awn picked him up, that he might become for them an enemy and a (cause of) grief. Verily, Fir\`awn, Haman and their armies were sinners.

# 3261

And the wife of Fir\`awn said: "A comfort of the eye for me and for you. Kill him not, perhaps he may be of benefit to us, or we may adopt him as a son." And they perceived not.

# 3262

And the heart of the mother of Musa became empty. She was very near to disclose his (case), had We not strengthened her heart, so that she might remain as one of the believers.

# 3263

And she said to his sister: "Follow him." So she watched him from a far place (secretly), while they perceived not.

# 3264

And We had already forbidden foster suckling mothers for him, until she said: "Shall I direct you to a household who will rear him for you, and look after him in a good manner"

# 3265

So We restored him to his mother, that her eye might be comforted, and that she might not grieve, and that she might know that the promise of Allah is true. But most of them know not.

# 3266

And when he reached maturity, and was complete, We bestowed on him Hukm and knowledge. And thus do We reward the doers of good.

# 3267

And he entered the city when its people were unaware: and he found there two men fighting, -- one of his party, and the other of his foes. The man of his (own) party asked him for help against his foe, so Musa struck him with his fist and he died. He said: "This is of Shaytan's doing, verily, he is a plain misleading enemy."

# 3268

He said: "My Lord! Verily, I have wronged myself, so forgive me." Then He forgave him. Verily, He is the Oft-Forgiving, the Most Merciful.

# 3269

He said: "My Lord! For that with which You have favored me, I will nevermore be a helper of the criminals!"

# 3270

So he became afraid, looking about in the city, when behold, the man who had sought his help the day before, called for his help (again). Musa said to him: "Verily, you are a plain misleader!"

# 3271

Then when he decided to seize the man who was an enemy to both of them, the man said: "O Musa! Is it your intention to kill me as you killed a man yesterday Your aim is nothing but to become a tyrant in the land, and not to be one of those who do right."

# 3272

And there came a man running, from the farthest end of the city. He said: "O Musa! Verily, the chiefs are taking counsel together about you, to kill you, so escape. Truly, I am one of the good advisers to you."

# 3273

So he escaped from there, looking about in a state of fear. He said: "My Lord! Save me from the people who are wrongdoers!"

# 3274

And when he went towards Madyan, he said: "It may be that my Lord guides me to the right way."

# 3275

And when he arrived at the water of Madyan, he found there a group of men watering, and besides them he found two women who were keeping back (their flocks). He said: "What is the matter with you" They said: "We cannot water (our flocks) until the shepherds take (their flocks). And our father is a very old man."

# 3276

So he watered (their flocks) for them, then he turned back to shade, and said: "My Lord! Truly, I am in need of whatever good that You bestow on me!"

# 3277

Then there came to him one of them, walking shyly. She said: "Verily, my father calls you that he may reward you for having watered (our flocks) for us." So when he came to him and narrated the story, he said: "Fear you not. You have escaped from the people who are wrongdoers."

# 3278

And said one of them (the two women): "O my father! Hire him! Verily, the best of men for you to hire is the strong, the trustworthy."

# 3279

He said: "I intend to wed one of these two daughters of mine to you, on condition that you serve me for eight years; but if you complete ten years, it will be (a favor) from you. But I intend not to place you under a difficulty. If Allah wills, you will find me one of the righteous."

# 3280

He (Musa) said: "That (is settled) between me and you: whichever of the two terms I fulfill, there will be no injustice to me, and Allah is Surety over what we say."

# 3281

Then, when Musa had fulfilled the term, and was traveling with his family, he saw a fire in the direction of At-Tur. He said to his family: "Wait, I have seen a fire; perhaps I may bring to you from there some information, or a burning firebrand that you may warm yourselves."

# 3282

So when he reached it, he was called from the right side of the valley, in the blessed place, from the tree: "O Musa! Verily, I am Allah, the Lord of all that exists!"

# 3283

"And throw your stick!" But when he saw it moving as if it were a snake, he turned in flight, and looked not back. (It was said:) "O Musa! Draw near, and fear not. Verily, you are of those who are secure."

# 3284

"Put your hand into the opening of your garment, it will come forth white without a disease; and draw your hand close to your side to be free from the fear. These are two proofs from your Lord to Fir\`awn and his chiefs. Verily, they are the people who are rebellious."

# 3285

He said: "My Lord! I have killed a man among them, and I fear that they will kill me."

# 3286

"And my brother Harun -- he is more eloquent in speech than me, so send him with me as a helper to confirm me. Verily, I fear that they will deny me."

# 3287

Allah said: "We will strengthen your arm through your brother, and give you both power, so they shall not be able to harm you, with Our Ayat; you two as well as those who follow you, will be the victors."

# 3288

Then when Musa came to them with Our Clear Ayat, they said: "This is nothing but invented magic. Never did we hear of this among our fathers of old."

# 3289

Musa said: "My Lord knows best him who came with guidance from Him, and whose will be the happy end in the Hereafter. Verily, the wrongdoers will not be successful."

# 3290

Fir\`awn said: "O chiefs! I know not that you have a god other than me. So kindle for me (a fire), O Haman, to bake clay, and set up for me a Sarh in order that I may look at the God of Musa; and verily, I think that he (Musa) is one of the liars."

# 3291

And he and his armies were arrogant in the land, without right, and they thought that they would never return to Us.

# 3292

So, We seized him and his armies, and We threw them all into the sea. So, behold what was the end of the wrongdoers.

# 3293

And We made them leaders inviting to the Fire: and on the Day of Resurrection, they will not be helped.

# 3294

And We made a curse to follow them in this world, and on the Day of Resurrection, they will be among disgraced.

# 3295

And indeed We gave Musa -- after We had destroyed the generations of old -- the Scripture as an enlightenment for mankind, and a guidance and a mercy, that they might remember.

# 3296

And you were not on the western side (of the Mount), when We made clear to Musa the commandment, and you were not among the witnesses.

# 3297

But We created generations, and long were the ages that passed over them. And you were not a dweller among the people of Madyan, reciting Our Ayat to them. But it is We Who kept sending (Messengers).

# 3298

And you were not at the side of At-Tur when We called. But (you are sent) as a mercy from your Lord, to give warning to a people to whom no warner had come before you, in order that they may remember or receive admonition.

# 3299

And if (We had) not (sent you to the people of Makkah) in case a calamity should seize them for what their hands have sent forth, they would have said: "Our Lord! Why did You not send us a Messenger We would then have followed Your Ayat and would have been among the believers."

# 3300

But when the truth has come to them from Us, they say: "Why is he not given the like of what was given to Musa Did they not disbelieve in that which was given to Musa of old" They say: "Two kinds of magic, each helping the other!" And they say: "Verily, in both we are disbelievers."

# 3301

Say: "Then bring a Book from Allah, which is a better guide than these two, that I may follow it, if you are truthful."

# 3302

But if they answer you not, then know that they only follow their own lusts. And who is more astray than one who follows his own lusts, without guidance from Allah Verily, Allah guides not the people who are wrongdoers.

# 3303

And indeed now We have conveyed the Word to them, in order that they may remember.

# 3304

Those to whom We gave the Scripture before it, they believe in it.

# 3305

And when it is recited to them, they say: "We believe in it. Verily, it is the truth from our Lord. Indeed even before it we have been from Muslims."

# 3306

These will be given their reward twice over, because they are patient, and repel evil with good, and spend out of what We have provided for them.

# 3307

And when they hear evil vain talk, they withdraw from it and say: "To us our deeds, and to you your deeds. Peace be to you. We seek not (the way of) the ignorant."

# 3308

Verily, you guide not whom you like, but Allah guides whom He wills. And He knows best those who are the guided.

# 3309

And they say: "If we follow the guidance with you, we would be snatched away from our land." Have We not established for them a secure sanctuary, to which are brought fruits of all kinds, a provision from Ourselves, but most of them know not.

# 3310

And how many a town have We destroyed, which was thankless for its means of livelihood! And those are their dwellings, which have not been inhabited after them except a little. And verily, We have been the heirs.

# 3311

And never will your Lord destroy the towns until He sends to their mother town a Messenger reciting to them Our Ayat. And never would We destroy the towns unless the people thereof are wrongdoers.

# 3312

And whatever you have been given is an enjoyment of the life of the world and its adornment, and that which is with Allah is better and will remain forever. Have you then no sense

# 3313

Is he whom We have promised an excellent promise -- which he will find true -- like him whom We have made to enjoy the luxuries of the life of the world, then on the Day of Resurrection, he will be among those brought up

# 3314

And (remember) the Day when He will call to them and say: "Where are My (so-called) partners whom you used to assert"

# 3315

Those about whom the Word will have been fulfilled will say: "Our Lord! These are they whom we led astray. We led them astray, as we were astray ourselves. We declare our innocence before You. It was not us they worshipped."

# 3316

And it will be said: "Call upon your partners," and they will call upon them, but they will give no answer to them, and they will see the torment. If only they had been guided!

# 3317

And the Day He will call to them, and say: "What answer gave you to the Messengers"

# 3318

Then the news of a good answer will be obscured to them on that Day, and they will not be able to ask one another.

# 3319

But as for him who repented, believed, and did righteous deeds, then perhaps he will be among those who are successful.

# 3320

And your Lord creates whatsoever He wills and chooses, no choice have they. Glorified is Allah, and exalted above all that they associate.

# 3321

And your Lord knows what their breasts conceal, and what they reveal.

# 3322

And He is Allah; La ilaha illa Huwa, His is the praise in the first and in the last, and His is the decision, and to Him shall you be returned.

# 3323

Say: "Tell me! If Allah made the night continuous for you till the Day of Resurrection, which god besides Allah could bring you light Will you not then hear"

# 3324

Say: "Tell me! If Allah made the day continuous for you till the Day of Resurrection, which god besides Allah could bring you night wherein you rest Will you not then see"

# 3325

It is out of His mercy that He has made for you the night and the day that you may rest therein and that you may seek of His bounty -- and in order that you may be grateful.

# 3326

And the Day when He will call to them, and will say: "Where are My (so-called) partners, whom you used to assert"

# 3327

And We shall take out from every nation a witness, and We shall say: "Bring your proof." Then they shall know that the truth is with Allah, and the lies which they invented will disappear from them.

# 3328

Verily, Qarun was of Musa's people, but he behaved arrogantly towards them. And We gave him of the treasures, that of which the keys would have been a burden to a body of strong men. Remember when his people said to him: "Do not exult. Verily, Allah likes not those who exult."

# 3329

"But seek, with that which Allah has bestowed on you, the home of the Hereafter, and forget not your portion of lawful enjoyment in this world; and be generous as Allah has been generous to you, and seek not mischief in the land. Verily, Allah likes not the mischief-makers."

# 3330

He said: "This has been given to me only because of the knowledge I possess." Did he not know that Allah had destroyed before him generations, men who were stronger than him in might and greater in the amount they had collected But the criminals will not be questioned of their sins.

# 3331

So, he went forth before his people in his finery. Those who were desirous of the life of the world, said: "Ah, would that we had the like of what Qarun has been given! Verily, he is the owner of a great fortune."

# 3332

But those who had been given knowledge said: "Woe to you! The reward of Allah is better for those who believe and do righteous deeds, and this none shall attain except the patient."

# 3333

So, We caused the earth to swallow him and his dwelling place. Then he had no group to help him against Allah, nor was he one of those who could save themselves.

# 3334

And those who desired his position the day before, began to say: "Know you not that it is Allah Who expands the provision or restricts it to whomsoever He pleases of His servants. Had it not been that Allah was Gracious to us, He could have caused the earth to swallow us up! Know you not that the disbelievers will never be successful."

# 3335

That is the home of the Hereafter, We shall assign to those who do not want to exalt themselves in the land nor cause corruption. And the good end is for those who have Taqwa.

# 3336

Whosoever brings good, he shall have the better thereof; and whosoever brings evil, then those who do evil deeds will only be requited for what they used to do.

# 3337

Verily, He Who has given you the Qur'an, will surely bring you back to the return. Say: "My Lord is Aware of him who brings guidance, and of him who is in manifest error."

# 3338

And you were not expecting that the Book would be sent down to you, but it is a mercy from your Lord. So never be a supporter of the disbelievers.

# 3339

And let them not turn you away from the Ayat of Allah after they have been sent down to you, and invite to your Lord and be not of idolators.

# 3340

And invoke not any other god along with Allah, La ilaha illa Huwa. Everything will perish save His Face. His is the decision, and to Him you shall be returned.

# 3341

Alif Lam Mim.

# 3342

Do people think that they will be left alone because they say: "We believe," and will not be tested.

# 3343

And We indeed tested those who were before them so that Allah will indeed know those who are true, and He will know those who are liars.

# 3344

Or think those who do evil deeds that they can outstrip Us Evil is that which they judge!

# 3345

Whoever hopes in meeting with Allah, then Allah's term is surely coming, and He is the All-Hearer, the All-Knower.

# 3346

And whosoever strives, he strives only for himself. Verily, Allah stands not in need of any of the creatures.

# 3347

Those who believe, and do righteous good deeds, surely, We shall expiate from them their evil deeds and We shall indeed reward them according to the best of that which they used to do.

# 3348

And We have enjoined on man to be dutiful to his parents; but if they strive to make you associate with Me, which you have no knowledge of, then obey them not. Unto Me is your return and I shall tell you what you used to do.

# 3349

And for those who believe and do righteous deeds, surely, We shall admit them among the righteous.

# 3350

Of mankind are some who say: "We believe in Allah." But if they are made to suffer for Allah, they consider the trial of mankind as Allah's punishment; and if victory comes from your Lord, they will say: "Verily, we were with you." Is not Allah Best Aware of what is in the breasts of the creatures

# 3351

And indeed Allah knows those who believe, and verily, He knows the hypocrites.

# 3352

And those who disbelieve say to those who believe: "Follow our way and let us bear your sins." Never will they bear anything of their sins. Surely, they are liars.

# 3353

And verily, they shall bear their own loads, and other loads besides their own; and verily, they shall be questioned on the Day of Resurrection about that which they used to fabricate.

# 3354

And indeed We sent Nuh to his people, and he stayed among them a thousand years less fifty years; so the Deluge overtook them while they were wrongdoers.

# 3355

Then We saved him and the Companions of the Boat, and made it an Ayah for all people.

# 3356

And (remember) Ibrahim when he said to his people: "Worship Allah, and have Taqwa of Him, that is better for you if you know."

# 3357

You worship besides Allah only idols, and you only invent falsehood. Verily, those whom you worship besides Allah have no power to give you provision, so seek from Allah your provision, and worship Him, and be grateful to Him. To Him you will be brought back.

# 3358

And if you deny, then nations before you have denied. And the duty of the Messenger is only to convey plainly."

# 3359

See they not how Allah originates the creation, then repeats it. Verily, that is easy for Allah.

# 3360

Say: "Travel in the land and see how He originated the creation, and then Allah will bring forth the creation of the Hereafter. Verily, Allah is able to do all things."

# 3361

He punishes whom He wills, and shows mercy to whom He wills; and to Him you will be returned.

# 3362

And you cannot escape in the earth or in the heaven. And besides Allah you have neither any protector nor any helper.

# 3363

And those who disbelieve in the Ayat of Allah and meeting with Him, such have no hope of My mercy: and for such there is a painful torment.

# 3364

So nothing was the answer of people except that they said: "Kill him or burn him." Then Allah saved him from the fire. Verily, in this are indeed signs for a people who believe.

# 3365

And (Ibrahim) said: "You have taken idols instead of Allah. The love between you is only in the life of this world, but on the Day of Resurrection, you shall deny each other, and curse each other, and your abode will be the Fire, and you shall have no helper."

# 3366

So, Lut believed in him. He said: "I will emigrate for the sake of my Lord. Verily, He is the All-Mighty, the All-Wise."

# 3367

And We bestowed on him, Ishaq and Ya\`qub, and We ordained among his offspring prophethood and the Book, and We granted him his reward in this world; and verily, in the Hereafter he is indeed among the righteous.

# 3368

And (remember) Lut, when he said to his people: "You commit immoral sins which none has preceded you in (committing) it in all creatures."

# 3369

"Verily, you practice sodomy with men, and rob the wayfarer! And practice Al-Munkar in your meetings." But his people gave no answer except that they said: "Bring Allah's torment upon us if you are one of the truthful."

# 3370

He said: "My Lord! Give me victory over the people who are corrupt."

# 3371

And when Our messengers came to Ibrahim with the glad tidings they said: "Verily, we are going to destroy the people of this town; truly, its people have been wrongdoers."

# 3372

Ibrahim said: "But there is Lut in it." They said: "We know better who is there. We will verily, save him and his family - except his wife, she will be of those who remain behind."

# 3373

And when Our messengers came to Lut, he was grieved because of them, and felt straitened on their account. They said: "Have no fear, and do not grieve! Truly, we shall save you and your family except your wife: she will be of those who remain behind."

# 3374

"Verily, we are about to bring down on the people of this town a great torment from the sky, because they have been rebellious."

# 3375

And indeed We have left thereof an evident Ayah for a folk who understand.

# 3376

And to Madyan, We sent their brother Shu\`ayb. He said: "O my people! Worship Allah and hope for the last Day, and commit no mischief on the earth as mischief-makers."

# 3377

And they denied him; so the earthquake seized them, and they lay, prostrate in their dwellings.

# 3378

And \`Ad and Thamud! And indeed (their destruction) is clearly apparent to you from their (ruined) dwellings. Shaytan made their deeds fair seeming to them, and turned them away from the path, though they were intelligent.

# 3379

And Qarun, Fir\`awn, and Haman. And indeed Musa came to them with clear Ayat, but they were arrogant in the land, yet they could not outstrip Us.

# 3380

So, We punished each for his sins, of them were some on whom We sent a Hasib, and of them were some who were overtaken by As-Sayhah, and of them were some whom We caused the earth to swallow, and of them were some whom We drowned. It was not Allah Who wronged them, but they wronged themselves.

# 3381

The parable of those who seek protectors from other than Allah is that of a spider who builds a house; but indeed, the weakest of houses is the spider's house -- if they but knew.

# 3382

Verily, Allah knows what things they invoke instead of Him. He is the All-Mighty, the All-Wise.

# 3383

And these are the examples We give for mankind; but none will understand them except those who have knowledge (of Allah).

# 3384

Allah created the heavens and the earth with truth. Verily, therein is surely a sign for those who believe.

# 3385

Recite what has been revealed to you of the Book, and perform the Salah. Verily, the Salah prevents from Al-Fahsha' (immoral sins) and Al-Munkar (evil deeds) and the remembering (praising) of Allah is greater indeed. And Allah knows what you do.

# 3386

And argue not with the People of the Scripture, except with that which is better -- except with such of them as do wrong; and say (to them): "We believe in that which has been revealed to us and revealed to you; our God and your God is One, and to Him we have submitted."

# 3387

And thus We have sent down the Book to you, and those whom We gave the Scripture believe therein as also do some of these and none but the disbelievers reject Our Ayat.

# 3388

Neither did you read any book before it nor did you write any book with your right hand. In that case, indeed, the followers of falsehood might have doubted.

# 3389

Nay, but it is clear Ayat, (preserved) in the breasts of those who have been given knowledge. And none but the wrongdoers deny Our Ayat.

# 3390

And they say: "Why are not signs sent down to him from his Lord" Say: "The signs are only with Allah, and I am only a plain warner."

# 3391

Is it not sufficient for them that We have sent down to you the Book which is recited to them Verily, herein is mercy and a reminder for a people who believe.

# 3392

Say: "Sufficient is Allah for a witness between me and you. He knows what is in the heavens and on the earth." And those who believe in falsehood, and disbelieve in Allah, it is they who are the losers.

# 3393

And they ask you to hasten on the torment, and had it not been for a term appointed, the torment would certainly have come to them. And surely, it will come upon them suddenly while they perceive not!

# 3394

They ask you to hasten on the torment. And verily, Hell, of a surety, will encompass the disbelievers.

# 3395

On the Day when the torment shall cover them from above them and from beneath their feet, and it will be said: "Taste what you used to do."

# 3396

O My servants who believe! Certainly, spacious is My earth. Therefore worship Me.

# 3397

Everyone shall taste death. Then unto Us you shall be returned.

# 3398

And those who believe and do righteous good deeds, to them We shall surely give lofty dwellings in Paradise, beneath which rivers flow, to live therein forever. Excellent is the reward for the workers.

# 3399

Those who are patient, and put their trust in their Lord.

# 3400

And so many a moving creature carries not its own provision! Allah provides for it and for you. And He is the All-Hearer, the All-Knower.

# 3401

And if you were to ask them: "Who has created the heavens and the earth and subjected the sun and the moon" They will surely reply: "Allah." How then are they deviating

# 3402

Allah expands the provision for whom He wills of His servants, and straitens it for whom (He wills). Verily, Allah is the All-Knower of everything.

# 3403

And if you were to ask them: "Who sends down water from the sky, and gives life therewith to the earth after its death" They will surely reply: "Allah." Say: "All the praises and thanks be to Allah!" Nay, most of them have no sense.

# 3404

And this life of the world is only an amusement and a play! Verily, the home of the Hereafter -- that is the life indeed, if they but knew.

# 3405

And when they embark on a ship, they invoke Allah, making their faith pure for Him only, but when He brings them safely to land, behold, they give a share of their worship to others.

# 3406

So that they become ingrate for that which We have given them, and that they take their enjoyment, but they will come to know.

# 3407

Have they not seen that We have made a secure sanctuary, while men are being snatched away from all around them Then do they believe in falsehood, and deny the graces of Allah

# 3408

And who does more wrong than he who invents a lie against Allah or denies the truth, when it comes to him Is there not a dwelling in Hell for the disbelievers

# 3409

As for those who strive hard for Us, We will surely guide them to Our paths. And verily, Allah is with the doers of good.

# 3410

Alif Lam Mim.

# 3411

The Romans have been defeated.

# 3412

In the nearest land, and they, after their defeat, will be victorious.

# 3413

In Bid\`i years. The decision of the matter, before and after is only with Allah. And on that day, the believers will rejoice

# 3414

With the help of Allah. He helps whom He wills, and He is the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful.

# 3415

A promise from Allah, and Allah fails not in His promise, but most men know not.

# 3416

They know only the outer appearance of the life of the world, and they are heedless of the Hereafter.

# 3417

(Do they not reflect upon themselves) Thinking and pondering how Allah created various things in the upper and lower realms and in the space between, realizing that this was not created in jest or in vain, but in truth, and that it will continue until an appointed time, the Day of Resurrection

# 3418

Have they not traveled through the earth and observed how was the end of those before them? They were greater than them in power, and they plowed the earth and built it up more than they have built it up, and their messengers came to them with clear evidences. And Allah would not ever have wronged them, but they were wronging themselves.

# 3419

Then evil was the end of those who did evil, because they denied the Ayat of Allah and made a mockery of them.

# 3420

Allah originates the creation, then He will repeat it, then to Him you will be returned.

# 3421

And on the Day when the Hour will be established, the criminals will be plunged into destruction with despair.

# 3422

No intercessors will they have from those whom they made equal with Allah, and they will reject and deny their partners.

# 3423

And on the Day when the Hour will be established -- that Day shall they be separated.

# 3424

Then as for those who believed and did righteous good deeds, such shall be honored and made to enjoy a luxurious life in a Garden of Delight.

# 3425

And as for those who disbelieved and denied Our Ayat, and the meeting of the Hereafter, such shall be brought forth to the torment.

# 3426

So glorify Allah, when you enter the evening, and when you enter the morning.

# 3427

And His is all the praise in the heavens and the earth; and in \`Ashiyya and when Tuzhirun.

# 3428

He brings out the living from the dead, and brings out the dead from the living. And He revives the earth after its death. And thus shall you be brought out.

# 3429

And among His signs is this that He created you from dust, and then -- behold you are human beings scattered!

# 3430

And among His signs is this that He created for you wives from among yourselves, that you may find repose in them, and He has put between you affection and mercy. Verily, in that are indeed signs for a people who reflect.

# 3431

And among His signs is the creation of the heavens and the earth, and the difference of your languages and colors. Verily, in that are indeed signs for men of sound knowledge.

# 3432

And among His signs is your sleep by night and by day, and your seeking His bounty. Verily, in that are indeed signs for a people who listen.

# 3433

And among His signs is that He shows you the lightning, for fear and for hope, and He sends down water from the sky, and therewith revives the earth after its death. Verily, in that are indeed signs for a people who understand.

# 3434

And among His signs is that the heaven and the earth stand by His command. Then afterwards when He will call you by a single call, behold, you will come out from the earth.

# 3435

To Him belongs whatever is in the heavens and the earth. All are obedient to Him.

# 3436

And He it is Who originates the creation, then He will repeat it; and this is easier for Him. His is the highest description in the heavens and in the earth. And He is the All-Mighty, the All-Wise.) Allah says:

# 3437

He sets forth for you a parable from yourselves: Do you have partners among those whom your right hands possess to share as equals in the wealth We have bestowed on you, whom you fear as you fear each other Thus do We explain the signs in detail to a people who have sense.

# 3438

Nay, but those who do wrong follow their own lusts without knowledge. Then who will guide him whom Allah has sent astray And for such there will be no helpers.

# 3439

So, set you your face towards the religion as a Hanif. Allah's Fitrah with which He has created mankind. No change let there be in Allah's Khalq, that is the straight religion, but most men know not.

# 3440

(And remain always) turning in repentance to Him and have Taqwa of Him; and perform the Salah and be not of idolators.

# 3441

Of those who split up their religion, and became sects, each sect rejoicing in that which is with it.

# 3442

And when harm touches men, they cry sincerely only to their Lord, turning to Him in repentance; but when He gives them a taste of His mercy, behold, a party of them associates partners in worship with their Lord.

# 3443

So as to be ungrateful for the graces which We have bestowed on them. Then enjoy; but you will come to know.

# 3444

Or have We revealed to them an authority, which speaks of that which they have been associating with Him

# 3445

And when We cause mankind to taste of mercy, they rejoice therein; but when some evil afflicts them because of what their hands have sent forth, behold, they are in despair!

# 3446

Do they not see that Allah expands the provision for whom He wills and straitens (it for whom He wills). Verily, in that are indeed signs for a people who believe.

# 3447

So, give to the kindred his due, and to Al-Miskin and to the wayfarer. That is best for those who seek Allah's Face; and it is they who will be successful.

# 3448

And that which you give in Riba in order that it may increase from other people's property, has no increase with Allah; but that which you give in Zakah seeking Allah's Face, then those they shall have manifold increase.

# 3449

Allah is He Who created you, then provided food for you, then will cause you to die, then He will give you life. Is there any of your partners that do anything of that Glory be to Him! And Exalted be He above all that they associate.

# 3450

Evil has appeared in Al-Barr and Al-Bahr because of what the hands of men have earned, that He may make them taste a part of that which they have done, in order that they may return.

# 3451

Say: "Travel in the land and see what was the end of those before (you)! Most of them were idolators."

# 3452

So, set you your face to the straight and right religion, before there comes from Allah a Day which none can avert. On that Day men shall be divided.

# 3453

Whosoever disbelieves will suffer from his disbelief, and whosoever does righteous good deeds, then such will prepare a good place for themselves.

# 3454

That He may reward those who believe and do righteous good deeds, out of His bounty. Verily, He likes not the disbelievers.

# 3455

And among His signs is this that He sends the winds as glad tidings, giving you a taste of His mercy, and that the ships may sail at His command, and that you may seek of His bounty, in order that you may be thankful.

# 3456

And indeed We did send Messengers before you to their own peoples. They came to them with clear proofs, then, We took vengeance on those who committed crimes; and it was incumbent upon Us to help the believers.

# 3457

Allah is He Who sends the winds, so that they raise clouds and spread them along the sky as He wills, and then break them into fragments until you see rain drops come forth from their midst! Then when He has made them fall on whom of His servants as He wills, lo, they rejoice!

# 3458

And verily, before that -- just before it was sent down upon them -- they were in despair!

# 3459

Look then at the effects of Allah's mercy, how He revives the earth after its death. Verily, that shall indeed raise the dead, and He is able to do all things.

# 3460

And if We send a wind, and they see it turn yellow -- behold, they then would become unthankful (disbelievers).

# 3461

So verily, you cannot make the dead to hear, nor can you make the deaf to hear the call, when they show their backs and turn away.

# 3462

And you cannot guide the blind from their straying; you can make to hear only those who believe in Our Ayat, and have submitted (to Allah in Islam).

# 3463

Allah is He Who created you in weakness, then gave you strength after weakness, then after strength gave (you) weakness and grey hair. He creates what He wills. And He is the All-Knowing, the All-Powerful.

# 3464

And on the Day that the Hour will be established, the criminals will swear that they stayed not but an hour -- thus were they ever deluded.

# 3465

And those who have been bestowed with knowledge and Faith will say: "Indeed you have stayed according to the decree of Allah, until the Day of Resurrection; so this is the Day of Resurrection, but you knew not."

# 3466

So, on that Day no excuse of theirs will avail those who did wrong, nor will they be allowed to return to seek (Allah's) pleasure.

# 3467

And indeed We have set forth for mankind, in this Qur'an every kind of parable. But if you bring to them any sign or proof, the disbelievers are sure to say (to the believers): "You follow nothing but falsehood and magic."

# 3468

Thus does Allah seal up the hearts of those who know not.

# 3469

So be patient. Verily, the promise of Allah is true; and let not those who have no certainty of faith discourage you (from conveying Allah's Message).

# 3470

Alif Lam Mim.

# 3471

These are Ayat of the Wise Book.

# 3472

A guide and a mercy for the Muhsinin.

# 3473

Those who perform the Salah and give Zakah and they have faith in the Hereafter with certainty.

# 3474

Such are on guidance from their Lord, and such are the successful.

# 3475

And of mankind is he who purchases idle talk (Lahw Al-Hadith) to mislead from the path of Allah without knowledge, and takes it by way of mockery. For such there will be a humiliating torment.

# 3476

And when Our Ayat are recited to such a one, he turns away in pride, as if he heard them not -- as if there were deafness in his ear. So announce to him a painful torment.

# 3477

Verily, those who believe and do righteous good deeds, for them are Gardens of Delight.

# 3478

To abide therein. It is a promise of Allah in truth. And He is the All-Mighty, the All-Wise.

# 3479

He has created the heavens without any pillars that you see, and has set on the earth firm mountains lest it should shake with you. And He has scattered therein moving creatures of all kinds. And We send down water from the sky, and We cause (plants) of every goodly kind to grow therein in pairs,

# 3480

This is the creation of Allah. So, show Me that which those besides Him have created. Nay, the wrongdoers are in plain error.

# 3481

And indeed We bestowed upon Luqman Al-Hikmah saying: "Give thanks to Allah." And whoever gives thanks, he gives thanks for (the good of) himself. And whoever is unthankful, then verily, Allah is All-Rich, Worthy of all praise.

# 3482

And when Luqman said to his son when he was advising him: "O my son! Join not in worship others with Allah. Verily, joining others in worship with Allah is a great Zulm (wrong) indeed."

# 3483

And We have enjoined on man (to be dutiful and good) to his parents. His mother bore him in weakness and hardship upon weakness and hardship, and his weaning is in two years -- give thanks to Me and to your parents. Unto Me is the final destination.

# 3484

But if they strive with you to make you join in worship with Me others that of which you have no knowledge, then obey them not; but behave with them in the world kindly, and follow the path of him who turns to Me in repentance and in obedience. Then to Me will be your return, and I shall tell you what you used to do.

# 3485

"O my son! If it be (anything) equal to the weight of a grain of mustard seed, and though it be in a rock, or in the heavens or on the earth, Allah will bring it forth. Verily, Allah is Subtle, Well-Aware."

# 3486

"O my son! Perform the Salah, enjoin the good, and forbid the evil, and bear with patience whatever befalls you. Verily, these are some of the important commandments."

# 3487

"And turn not your face away from men with pride, nor walk in insolence through the earth. Verily, Allah likes not any arrogant boaster."

# 3488

"And be moderate in your walking, and lower your voice. Verily, the harshest of all voices is the braying of the asses."

# 3489

See you not that Allah has subjected for you whatsoever is in the heavens and whatsoever is on the earth, and has completed and perfected His graces upon you, apparent and hidden Yet of mankind is he who disputes about Allah without knowledge or guidance or a Book giving light!

# 3490

And when it is said to them: "Follow that which Allah has sent down," they say: "Nay, we shall follow that which we found our fathers (following)." Even if Shaytan invites them to the torment of the Fire

# 3491

And whosoever submits his face (himself) to Allah, while he is a Muhsin, then he has grasped the most trustworthy handhold. And to Allah return all matters for decision.

# 3492

And whoever disbelieves, let not his disbelief grieve you. To Us is their return, and We shall inform them what they have done. Verily, Allah is the All-Knower of what is in the breasts.

# 3493

We let them enjoy for a little while, then in the end We shall oblige them to (enter) a great torment.

# 3494

And if you ask them: "Who has created the heavens and the earth," they will certainly say: "Allah." Say: "All the praises and thanks be to Allah!" But most of them know not.

# 3495

To Allah belongs whatsoever is in the heavens and the earth. Verily, Allah, He is Al-Ghani, Worthy of all praise.

# 3496

And if all the trees on the earth were pens and the sea, with seven seas behind it to add to it, yet the Words of Allah would not be exhausted. Verily, Allah is All-Mighty, All-Wise.

# 3497

The creation of you all and the resurrection of you all are only as a single person. Verily, Allah is All-Hearer, All-Seer.

# 3498

See you not that Allah merges the night into the day, and merges the day into the night, and has subjected the sun and the moon, each running its course for a term appointed; and that Allah is All-Aware of what you do.

# 3499

That is because Allah, He is the Truth, and that which they invoke besides Him is falsehood; and that Allah, He is the Most High, the Most Great.

# 3500

See you not that the ships sail through the sea by Allah's grace that He may show you of His signs Verily, in this are signs for every patient, grateful (person).

# 3501

And when waves cover them like shades, they invoke Allah, making their invocations for Him only. But when He brings them safe to land, there are among them those that stop in between. And Our Ayat are not denied except by every Khattar Kafur.

# 3502

O mankind! Have Taqwa of your Lord, and fear a Day when no father can avail aught for his son, nor a son avail aught for his father. Verily, the promise of Allah is true, let not then this present life deceive you, nor let the chief deceiver deceive you about Allah.

# 3503

Verily, Allah, with Him is the knowledge of the Hour, He sends down the rain, and knows that which is in the wombs. No person knows what he will earn tomorrow, and no person knows in what land he will die. Verily, Allah is All-Knower, All-Aware.

# 3504

Alif Lam Mim.

# 3505

The revelation of the Book in which there is no doubt, is from the Lord of all that exists.

# 3506

Or say they: "He has fabricated it" Nay, it is the truth from your Lord, so that you may warn a people to whom no warner has come before you, in order that they may be guided.

# 3507

Allah it is He Who has created the heavens and the earth, and all that is between them in six Days. Then He Istawa over the Throne. You have none, besides Him, as a protector or an intercessor. Will you not then remember

# 3508

He directs the command from the heavens to the earth; then it will go up to Him, in one Day, the space whereof is a thousand years of your reckoning.

# 3509

That is He, the All-Knower of the unseen and the seen, the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful.

# 3510

Who made everything He has created good and He began the creation of man from clay.

# 3511

Then He made his offspring from semen of despised water.

# 3512

Then He fashioned him in due proportion, and breathed into him the soul; and He gave you hearing, sight and the sense of deduction. Little is the thanks you give!

# 3513

And they say: "When we are lost in the earth, shall we indeed be created anew" Nay, but they deny the meeting with their Lord!

# 3514

Say: "The angel of death, who is set over you, will take your souls. Then you shall be brought to your Lord."

# 3515

And if you only could see when the criminals shall hang their heads before their Lord (saying): "Our Lord! We have now seen and heard, so send us back that we will do righteous good deeds. Verily, we now believe with certainty."

# 3516

And if We had willed, surely We would have given every person his guidance, but the Word from Me took effect, that I will fill Hell with Jinn and mankind together.

# 3517

Then taste because of your forgetting the meeting of this Day of yours. Surely, We too will forget you, so taste you the abiding torment for what you used to do.

# 3518

Only those believe in Our Ayat, who, when they are reminded of them, fall down prostrate, and glorify the praises of their Lord, and they are not proud.

# 3519

Their sides forsake their beds, to invoke their Lord in fear and hope, and they spend out of what We have bestowed on them.

# 3520

No person knows what is kept hidden for them of delights of eyes as a reward for what they used to do.

# 3521

Is then he who is a believer like him who is rebellious Not equal are they.

# 3522

As for those who believe and do righteous good deeds, for them are Gardens of Abode as an entertainment for what they used to do.

# 3523

And as for those who rebel, their abode will be the Fire, every time they wish to get away therefrom, they will be put back thereto, and it will be said to them: "Taste you the torment of the Fire which you used to deny."

# 3524

And verily, We will make them taste of the near lighter torment prior to the greater torment, in order that they may return.

# 3525

And who does more wrong than he who is reminded of the Ayat of his Lord, then turns aside therefrom Verily, We shall exact retribution from the criminals.

# 3526

And indeed We gave Musa the Scripture. So, be not you in doubt of meeting him. And We made it a guide to the Children of Israel.

# 3527

And We made from among them, leaders, giving guidance under Our command, when they were patient and used to believe with certainty in Our Ayat.

# 3528

Verily, your Lord will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection, concerning that wherein they used to differ.

# 3529

Is it not a guidance for them: how many generations We have destroyed before them in whose dwellings they do walk about Verily, therein indeed are signs. Would they not then listen

# 3530

Have they not seen how We drive water to the dry land that has no vegetation, and therewith bring forth crops providing food for their cattle and themselves Will they not then see

# 3531

They say: "When will this Fath be, if you are telling the truth"

# 3532

Say: "On the Day of Al-Fath, no profit will it be to those who disbelieve if they (then) believe! Nor will they be granted a respite."

# 3533

So turn aside from them and await, verily, they (too) are awaiting.

# 3534

O Prophet! Have Taqwa of Allah, and obey not the disbelievers and the hypocrites. Verily, Allah is Ever All-Knower, All-Wise.

# 3535

And follow that which is revealed to you from your Lord. Verily, Allah is Well-Acquainted with what you do.

# 3536

And put your trust in Allah, and sufficient is Allah as a Trustee.

# 3537

Allah has not made for any man two hearts inside his body. Neither has He made your wives whom you declare to be like your mothers' backs, your real mothers nor has He made your adopted sons your real sons. That is but your saying with your mouths. But Allah says the truth, and He guides to the way.

# 3538

Call them by their fathers, that is more just with Allah. But if you know not their father's, your brothers in faith and Mawalikum (your freed servants). And there is no sin on you concerning that in which you made a mistake, except in regard to what your hearts deliberately intend. And Allah is Ever Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 3539

The Prophet is closer to the believers than themselves, and his wives are their mothers. And blood relations among each other have closer personal ties in the decree of Allah than the believers and the Muhajirin, except that you do kindness to those brothers. This has been written in the Book.

# 3540

And when We took from the Prophets their covenant, and from you, and from Nuh, Ibrahim, Musa, and \`Isa son of Maryam. We took from them a strong covenant.

# 3541

That He may ask the truthful about their truth. And He has prepared for the disbelievers a painful torment.

# 3542

O you who believe! Remember Allah's favor to you, when there came against you hosts, and We sent against them a wind and forces that you saw not. And Allah is Ever All-Seer of what you do.

# 3543

When they came upon you from above you and from below you, and when the eyes grew wild and the hearts reached to the throats, and you were harboring doubts about Allah.

# 3544

There, the believers were tried and shaken with a mighty shaking.

# 3545

And when the hypocrites and those in whose hearts is a disease said: "Allah and His Messenger promised us nothing but delusion!"

# 3546
