And when a party of them said: "O people of Yathrib! There is no postition for you. Therefore go back!" And a band of them ask for permission of the Prophet saying: "Truly, our homes lie open." And they lay not open. They but wished to flee.

# 3547

And if the enemy had entered from all sides, and they had been exhorted to Al-Fitnah, they would surely have committed it and would have hesitated thereupon but little.

# 3548

And indeed they had already made a covenant with Allah not to turn their backs, and a covenant with Allah must be answered for.

# 3549

Say: "Flight will not avail you if you flee from death or killing and then you will enjoy no more than a little while!"

# 3550

Say: "Who is he who can protect you from Allah if He intends to harm you, or intends mercy on you" And they will not find, besides Allah, for themselves any protector or any helper.

# 3551

Allah already knows those among you who keep back (men) from fighting (in Allah's cause), and those who say to their brethren, "Come here towards us," while they come not to the battle except a little,

# 3552

Being miserly towards you. Then when fear comes, you will see them looking to you, their eyes revolving like one over whom hovers death; but when the fear departs, they will smite you with sharp tongues, miserly towards good. Such have not believed. Therefore, Allah makes their deeds fruitless and that is ever easy for Allah.

# 3553

They think that the Confederates have not yet withdrawn; and if the Confederates should come, they would wish they were in the deserts among the bedouins, seeking news about you; and if they were to be among you, they would not fight but little.

# 3554

Indeed in the Messenger of Allah you have a good example to follow for him who hopes in Allah and the Last Day, and remembers Allah much.

# 3555

And when the believers saw the Confederates, they said: "This is what Allah and His Messenger had promised us; and Allah and His Messenger had spoken the truth." And it only added to their faith and to their submissiveness.

# 3556

Among the believers are men who have been true to their covenant with Allah; of them some have fulfilled their Nahbah; and some of them are still waiting, but they have never changed in the least.

# 3557

That Allah may reward the men of truth for their truth, and punish the hypocrites, if He wills, or accept their repentance by turning to them. Verily, Allah is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 3558

And Allah drove back those who disbelieved in their rage: they gained no advantage. Allah sufficed for the believers in the fighting. And Allah is Ever All-Strong, All-Mighty.

# 3559

And those of the People of the Scripture who backed them, Allah brought them down from their forts and cast terror into their hearts; a group you killed, and a group you made captives.

# 3560

And He caused you to inherit their lands, and their houses, and their riches, and a land which you had not trodden. And Allah is able to do all things.

# 3561

O Prophet! Say to your wives: "If you desire the life of this world, and its glitter, then come! I will make a provision for you and set you free in a handsome manner."

# 3562

"But if you desire Allah and His Messenger, and the Home of the Hereafter, then verily, Allah has prepared for the doers of good among you an enormous reward."

# 3563

O wives of the Prophet! Whoever of you commits an open Fahishah, the torment for her will be doubled, and that is ever easy for Allah.

# 3564

And whosoever of you is obedient to Allah and His Messenger, and does righteous good deeds, We shall give her, her reward twice over, and We have prepared for her a noble provision.

# 3565

O wives of the Prophet! You are not like any other women. If you keep you have Taqwa, then be not soft in speech, lest he in whose heart is a disease should be moved with desire, but speak in an honorable manner.

# 3566

And stay in your houses, and do not Tabarruj yourselves like the Tabarruj of the times of ignorance, and perform the Salah, and give Zakah and obey Allah and His Messenger. Allah wishes only to remove the Ar-Rijs from you, O members of the family, and to purify you with a thorough purification.

# 3567

And remember, that which is recited in your houses of the Ayat of Allah and Al-Hikmah. Verily, Allah is Ever Most Courteous, Well-Acquainted with all things.

# 3568

Verily, the Muslims: men and women, the believers: men and women, the Qanit: men and the women, the men and women who are truthful, the men and the women who are patient, the Khashi\`: men and the women, the men and the women who give Sadaqat, the men and the women who fast, the men and the women who guard their chastity and the men and the women who remember Allah much with their hearts and tongues, Allah has prepared for them forgiveness and a great reward.

# 3569

It is not for a believer, man or woman, when Allah and His Messenger have decreed a matter that they should have any option in their decision. And whoever disobeys Allah and His Messenger, he has indeed strayed into a plain error.

# 3570

And (remember) when you said to him on whom Allah has bestowed grace and you have done a favor: "Keep your wife to yourself, and have Taqwa of Allah." But you did hide in yourself that which Allah will make manifest, you did fear the people whereas Allah had a better right that you should fear Him. So, when Zayd had completed his aim with her, We gave her to you in marriage, so that there may be no difficulty to the believers in respect of the wives of their adopted sons when the latter have no desire to keep them. And Allah's command must be fulfilled.

# 3571

There is no blame on the Prophet in that which Allah has made legal for him. That has been Allah's way with those who have passed away of old. And the command of Allah is a decree determined.

# 3572

Those who convey the Message of Allah and fear Him, and fear none save Allah. And sufficient is Allah as a Reckoner.

# 3573

Muhammad is not the father of any of your men, but he is the Messenger of Allah and the last of the Prophets. And Allah is Ever All-Aware of everything.

# 3574

O you who believe! Remember Allah with much remembrance.

# 3575

And glorify His praises morning and Asila.

# 3576

He it is Who sends Salah on you, and His angels too, that He may bring you out from darkness into light. And He is Ever Most Merciful to the believers.

# 3577

Their greeting on the Day they shall meet Him will be "Salam (Peace!)" And He has prepared for them a generous reward.

# 3578

O Prophet! Verily, We have sent you as witness, and a bearer of glad tidings, and a warner,

# 3579

And as one who invites to Allah by His leave, and as a lamp spreading light.

# 3580

And announce to the believers the glad tidings, that they will have from Allah a great bounty.

# 3581

And obey not the disbelievers and the hypocrites, and harm them not. And put your trust in Allah, and sufficient is Allah as a Trustee.

# 3582

O you who believe! When you marry believing women, and then divorce them before you have sexual intercourse with them, no \`Iddah have you to count in respect of them. So, give them a present, and set them free in a handsome manner.

# 3583

O Prophet! Verily, We have made lawful to you your wives, to whom you have paid their due (dowery), and those (slaves) whom your right hand possesses -- whom Allah has given to you, and the daughters of your paternal uncles and the daughters of your paternal aunts and the daughters of your maternal uncles and the daughters of your maternal aunts who migrated with you, and a believing woman if she offers herself to the Prophet, and the Prophet wishes to marry her -- a privilege for you only, not for the (rest of) the believers. Indeed We know what We have enjoined upon them about their wives and those (slaves) whom their right hands possess, in order that there should be no difficulty on you. And Allah is Ever Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 3584

You can postpone whom you will of them, and you may receive whom you will. And whomsoever you desire of those whom you have set aside, it is no sin on you: that is better that they may be comforted and not grieved, and may all be pleased with what you give them. Allah knows what is in your hearts. And Allah is Ever All-Knowing, Most Forbearing.

# 3585

It is not lawful for you (to marry other) women after this, nor to change them for other wives even though their beauty attracts you, except those whom your right hand possesses. And Allah is Ever a Watcher over all things.

# 3586

O you who believe! Enter not the Prophet's houses, unless permission is given to you for a meal, (and then) not (so early as) to wait for its preparation. But when you are invited, enter, and when you have taken your meal, disperse without sitting for a talk. Verily, such (behavior) annoys the Prophet, and he is shy of (asking) you (to go); but Allah is not shy of (telling you) the truth. And when you ask (his wives) for anything you want, ask them from behind a screen, that is purer for your hearts and for their hearts. And it is not (right) for you that you should annoy Allah's Messenger, nor that you should ever marry his wives after him (his death). Verily, with Allah that shall be an enormity.

# 3587

Whether you reveal anything or conceal it, verily, Allah is Ever All-Knower of everything.

# 3588

It is no sin on them before their fathers, or their sons, or their brothers, or their brother's sons, or the sons of their sisters, or their own (believing) women, or their (female) slaves. And (O ladies) have Taqwa of Allah. Verily, Allah is Ever All-Witness over everything.

# 3589

Allah sends His Salah on the Prophet, and also His angels (do so). O you who believe! Send your Salah on him, and greet him with Taslim.

# 3590

Verily, those who annoy Allah and His Messenger, Allah has cursed them in this world and in the Hereafter, and has prepared for them a humiliating torment.

# 3591

And those who annoy believing men and women undeservedly, they bear the crime of slander and plain sin.

# 3592

O Prophet! Tell your wives and your daughters and the women of the believers to draw their Jalabib over their bodies. That will be better that they should be known so as not to be annoyed. And Allah is Ever Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 3593

If the hypocrites and those in whose hearts is a disease, and those who spread false news among the people in Al-Madinah stop not, We shall certainly let you overpower them, then they will not be able to stay in it as your neighbors but a little while.

# 3594

Accursed, they shall be seized wherever found, and killed with a (terrible) slaughter.

# 3595

That was the way of Allah in the case of those who passed away of old, and you will not find any change in the way of Allah.

# 3596

People ask you concerning the Hour, say: "The knowledge of it is with Allah only. What do you know It may be that the Hour is near!"

# 3597

Verily, Allah has cursed the disbelievers, and has prepared for them a flaming Fire.

# 3598

Wherein they will abide forever, and they will find neither a a protector nor a helper.

# 3599

On the Day when their faces will be turned over in the Fire, they will say: "Oh, would that we had obeyed Allah and obeyed the Messenger."

# 3600

And they will say: "Our Lord! Verily, we obeyed our chiefs and our great ones, and they misled us from the way."

# 3601

"Our Lord! Give them double torment and curse them with a mighty curse!"

# 3602

O you who believe! Be not like those who annoyed Musa, but Allah cleared him of that which they alleged, and he was honorable before Allah.

# 3603

O you who believe! Have Taqwa of Allah and speak (always) the truth.

# 3604

He will direct you to do righteous good deeds and will forgive you your sins. And whosoever obeys Allah and His Messenger, he has indeed achieved a great victory.

# 3605

Truly, We did offer the Amanah to the heavens and the earth, and the mountains, but they declined to bear it and were afraid of it. But man bore it. Verily, he was unjust and ignorant.

# 3606

So that Allah will punish the hypocrites, men and women, and the men and women who are idolators. And Allah will pardon the believers, men and women. And Allah is Ever Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 3607

All praise is due to Allah, to Whom belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is on the earth. His is all praise in the Hereafter, and He is the All-Wise, the All-Aware.

# 3608

He knows that which goes into the earth and that which comes forth from it, and that which descends from the heaven and that which ascends to it. And He is the Most Merciful, the Oft-Forgiving.

# 3609

Those who disbelieve say: "The Hour will not come to us." Say: "Yes, by my Lord, the All-Knower of the Unseen, it will come to you; not even the weight of a speck of dust or less than that or greater escapes His knowledge in the heavens or in the earth but it is in a Clear Book."

# 3610

That He may recompense those who believe and do righteous good deeds. Those, theirs is forgiveness and generous provision.

# 3611

But those who strive against Our Ayat to frustrate them -- those, for them will be a severe painful torment.

# 3612

And those who have been given knowledge see that what is revealed to you from your Lord is the truth, and that it guides to the path of the Exalted in might, Owner of all praise.

# 3613

Those who disbelieve say: "Shall we direct you to a man who will tell you (that) when you have become fully disintegrated into dust with full dispersion, then you will be created (again) anew"

# 3614

Has he invented a lie against Allah, or is there a madness in him Nay, but those who disbelieve in the Hereafter are (themselves) in a torment, and in far error.

# 3615

See they not what is before them and what is behind them, of the heaven and the earth If We will, We shall sink the earth with them, or cause a piece of the heaven to fall upon them. Verily, in this is a sign for every servant who turns (to Allah) in repentance.

# 3616

And indeed We bestowed grace on Dawud from Us (saying): "O you mountains! Glorify with him! And you birds (also)! And We made the iron soft for him."

# 3617

Saying: "Make you perfect coats of mail, and balance well the rings of chain armor \[Sard\], and work you (men) righteousness. Truly, I am All-Seer of what you do."

# 3618

And to Sulayman (We subjected) the wind, its morning was a month's (journey), and its afternoon was a month's (journey). And We caused a fount of Qitr to flow for him, and there were Jinn that worked in front of him, by the leave of his Lord. And whosoever of them turned aside from Our command, We shall cause him to taste of the torment of the blazing Fire.

# 3619

They worked for him as he desired on Maharib, Tamathil, large basins like Jawab and Qudur Rasiyat. "Work you, O family of Dawud, with thanks!" But few of My servants are grateful.

# 3620

Then when We decreed death for him, nothing informed them (Jinn) of his death except a little worm of the earth which kept (slowly) gnawing away at his stick. So when he fell down, the Jinn saw clearly that if they had known the Unseen, they would not have stayed in the humiliating torment.

# 3621

Indeed there was for Saba' a sign in their dwelling place -- two gardens on the right and on the left; (and it was said to them:) "Eat of the provision of your Lord, and be grateful to Him." A fair land and an Oft-Forgiving Lord!

# 3622

But they turned away, so We sent against them flood released from the dam, and We converted their two gardens into gardens producing bitter bad fruit, and Athl, and some few lote trees.

# 3623

Like this We requited them because they were ungrateful disbelievers. And never do We requite in such a way except those who are ungrateful (disbelievers).

# 3624

And We placed, between them and the towns which We had blessed, towns easy to be seen, and We made the stages (of journey) between them easy (saying): "Travel in them safely both by night and day."

# 3625

But they said: "Our Lord! Make the stages between our journey longer," and they wronged themselves; so We made them as tales (in the land), and We dispersed them all totally. Verily, in this are indeed signs for every steadfast, grateful (person).

# 3626

And indeed Iblis did prove true his thought about them, and they followed him, all except a group of true believers.

# 3627

And he had no authority over them, -- except that We might test him who believes in the Hereafter, from him who is in doubt about it. And your Lord is Watchful over everything.

# 3628

Say: "Call upon those whom you assert besides Allah, they possess not even the weight of a speck of dust, either in the heavens or on the earth, nor have they any share in either, nor there is for Him any supporter from among them. "

# 3629

Intercession with Him profits not except for him whom He permits. So much so that when fear is banished from their hearts, they say: "What is it that your Lord has said" They say the truth. And He is the Most High, the Most Great.

# 3630

Say: "Who gives you provision from the heavens and the earth" Say: "Allah. And verily, (either) we or you are rightly guided or in plain error."

# 3631

Say: "You will not be asked about our sins, nor shall we be asked of what you do."

# 3632

Say: "Our Lord will assemble us all together, then He will judge between us with truth. And He is the Just Judge, the All-Knower of the true state of affairs."

# 3633

Say: "Show me those whom you have joined with Him as partners. Nay! But He is Allah, the Almighty, the All-Wise."

# 3634

And We have not sent you except as a giver of glad tidings and a warner to all mankind, and most of men know not.

# 3635

And they say: "When is this promise if you are truthful"

# 3636

Say: "The appointment to you is for a Day, which you cannot put back for an hour nor put forward."

# 3637

And those who disbelieve say: "We believe not in this Qur'an nor in that which was before it." But if you could see when the wrongdoers are made to stand before their Lord, how they will cast the (blaming) word one to another! Those who were deemed weak will say to those who were arrogant: "Had it not been for you, we should certainly have been believers!"

# 3638

And those who were arrogant will say to those who were deemed weak: "Did we keep you back from guidance after it had come to you Nay, but you were criminals."

# 3639

Those who were deemed weak will say to those who were arrogant: "Nay, but it was your plotting by night and day, when you ordered us to disbelieve in Allah and set up rivals to Him!" And each of them (parties) will conceal their own regrets, when they behold the torment. And We shall put iron collars round the necks of those who disbelieved. Are they requited aught except what they used to do

# 3640

And We did not send a warner to a township but those who were given the worldly wealth and luxuries among them said: "We believe not in what you have been sent with."

# 3641

And they say: "We are more in wealth and in children, and we are not going to be punished."

# 3642

Say: "Verily, my Lord expands the provision to whom He wills and restricts, but most men know not."

# 3643

And it is not your wealth, nor your children that bring you nearer to Us, but only he who believes, and does righteous deeds; as for such, there will be multiple rewards for what they did, and they will reside in the high dwellings (Paradise) in peace and security.

# 3644

And those who strive against Our Ayat, to frustrate them, they will be brought to the torment.

# 3645

Say: "Truly, my Lord expands the provision for whom He wills of His servants, and (also) restricts (it) for him, and whatsoever you spend of anything, He will replace it." And He is the Best of those who make provision.

# 3646

And (remember) the Day when He will gather them all together, then He will say to the angels: "Was it you that these people used to worship"

# 3647

They (the angels) will say: "Glorified be You! You are our Protector instead of them. Nay, but they used to worship the Jinn; most of them were believers in them."

# 3648

So Today, none of you can profit or harm one another. And We shall say to those who did wrong: "Taste the torment of the Fire which you used to deny."

# 3649

And when Our Clear Verses are recited to them, they say: "This is naught but a man who wishes to hinder you from that which your fathers used to worship." And they say: "This is nothing but an invented lie." And those who disbelieve say of the truth when it has come to them: "This is nothing but evident magic!"

# 3650

And We had not given them Scriptures that they could study, nor sent to them before you any warner.

# 3651

And those before them denied; these have not received even a tenth of what We had granted to those (of old); yet they denied My Messengers. Then how (terrible) was My denial!

# 3652

Say: "I exhort you to one (thing) only, that you stand up for Allah's sake in pairs and singly, and reflect, there is no madness in your companion. He is only a warner to you in face of a severe torment."

# 3653

Say: "Whatever wage I might have asked of you is yours. My wage is from Allah only, and He is a Witness over all things."

# 3654

Say: "Verily, my Lord sends down the truth, the All-Knower of the Unseen."

# 3655

Say: "The truth has come, and the falsehood can neither create anything nor resurrect."

# 3656

Say: "If (even) I go astray, I shall stray only to my own loss. But if I remain guided, it is because of the Revelation of my Lord to me. Truly, He is All-Hearer, Ever Near."

# 3657

And if you could but see, when they will be terrified with no escape, and they will be seized from a near place.

# 3658

And they will say: "We do believe (now);" but how could they receive (Tanawush) from a place so far off.

# 3659

Indeed they did disbelieve before (in this world), and they (used to) conjecture about the Unseen, from a far place.

# 3660

And a barrier will be set between them and that which they desire, as was done in the past with the people of their kind. Verily, they have been in grave doubt.

# 3661

All praise is due to Allah, Fatir of the heavens and the earth, Who made the angels messengers with wings, two or three or four. He increases in creation what He wills. Verily, Allah is Able to do all things.

# 3662

Whatever of mercy, Allah may grant to mankind, none can withhold it; and whatever He may withhold, none can grant it thereafter. And He is the Almighty, the All-Wise.

# 3663

O mankind! Remember the grace of Allah upon you! Is there any creator other than Allah who provides for you from the sky (rain) and the earth La ilaha illa Huwa. How then are you turning away (from Him)

# 3664

And if they deny you, so were Messengers denied before you. And to Allah return all matters.

# 3665

O mankind! Verily, the promise of Allah is true. So, let not this present life deceive you, and let not the chief deceiver deceive you about Allah.

# 3666

Surely, Shaytan is an enemy to you, so take (treat) him as an enemy. He only invites his followers that they may become the dwellers of the blazing Fire.

# 3667

Those who disbelieve, theirs will be a severe torment; and those who believe and do righteous good deeds, theirs will be forgiveness and a great reward.

# 3668

Is he, then, to whom the evil of his deeds is made fairseeming, so that he considers it as good Verily, Allah sends astray whom He wills, and guides whom He wills. So destroy not yourself in sorrow for them. Truly, Allah is the All-Knower of what they do!

# 3669

And it is Allah Who sends the winds, so that they raise up the clouds, and We drive them to a dead land, and revive therewith the earth after its death. As such (will be) the Resurrection!

# 3670

Whosoever desires Al-\`Izzah then to Allah belongs Al-\`Izzah. To Him ascend the good words, and the righteous deeds exalt it, but those who plot evils, theirs will be a severe torment. And the plotting of such will perish.

# 3671

And Allah did create you from dust, then from Nutfah, then He made you pairs. And no female conceives or gives birth but with His knowledge. And no aged man is granted a length of life nor is a part cut off from his life, but is in a Book. Surely, that is easy for Allah.

# 3672

And the two seas (kinds of water) are not alike: this is palatable, sweet and pleasant to drink, and that is salty and bitter. And from them both you eat fresh tender meat (fish), and derive the ornaments that you wear. And you see the ships cleaving, that you may seek of His bounty, and that you may give thanks.

# 3673

He merges the night into the day, and He merges the day into the night. And He has subjected the sun and the moon, each runs its course for a term appointed. Such is Allah, your Lord; His is the kingdom. And those, whom you invoke or call upon instead of Him, own not even a Qitmir.

# 3674

If you invoke them, they hear your call; and if (in case) they were to hear, they could not grant it to you. And on the Day of Resurrection, they will disown your worshipping them. And none can inform you like Him Who is the All-Knower.

# 3675

O mankind! it is you who stand in need of Allah. But Allah is the Rich, Worthy of all praise.

# 3676

If He willed, He could destroy you and bring about a new creation.

# 3677

And that is not hard for Allah.

# 3678

And no bearer of burdens shall bear another's burden; and if one heavily laden calls another to (bear) his load, nothing of it will be lifted even though he be near of kin. You can warn only those who fear their Lord unseen and perform the Salah. And he who purifies himself (from all kinds of sins), then he purifies only for the benefit of himself. And to Allah is the Return (of all).

# 3679

Not alike are the blind and the seeing.

# 3680

Nor are (depths of) darkness and light.

# 3681

Nor are the shade and the sun's heat.

# 3682

Nor are the living and the dead. Verily, Allah makes whom He wills to hear, but you cannot make hear those who are in graves.

# 3683

You are only a warner.

# 3684

Verily, We have sent you with the truth, a bearer of glad tidings and a warner. And there never was a nation but a warner had passed among them.

# 3685

And if they deny you, those before them also denied. Their Messengers came to them with clear signs, and with the Scriptures, and with the Book giving light.

# 3686

Then I took hold of those who disbelieved, and how terrible was My denial!

# 3687

See you not that Allah sends down water from the sky, and We produce therewith fruits of various colors, and among the mountains are Judad, white and red, of varying colors and (others) Gharabib black.

# 3688

And likewise, men and moving creature and cattle are of various colors. It is only those among His servants who have knowledge that fear Allah. Verily, Allah is Almighty, Oft-Forgiving.

# 3689

Verily, those who recite the Book of Allah, and perform the Salah, and spend out of what We have provided for them, secretly and openly, they hope for a (sure) trade-gain that will never perish.

# 3690

That He may pay them their wages in full, and give them (even) more, out of His grace. Verily, He is Oft-Forgiving, Most Ready to appreciate.

# 3691

And what We have revealed to you of the Book, it is the (very) truth confirming that which was (revealed) before it. Verily, Allah is indeed All-Aware and All-Seer of His servants.

# 3692

Then We gave the Book as inheritance to such of Our servants whom We chose. Then of them are some who wrong themselves, and of them are some who follow a middle course, and of them are some who are, by Allah's leave, foremost in good deeds. That -- that is indeed a great grace.

# 3693

\`Adn (Gardens) will they enter, therein will they be adorned with bracelets of gold and pearls, and their garments therein will be of silk.

# 3694

And they will say: "All praise and thanks be to Allah, Who has removed from us (all) grief. Verily, our Lord is indeed Oft-Forgiving, Most Ready to appreciate."

# 3695

"Who, out of His grace, has lodged us in a home that will last forever, where toil will touch us not nor weariness will touch us."

# 3696

But those who disbelieve, for them will be the fire of Hell. Neither will it have a complete killing effect on them so that they die nor shall its torment be lightened for them. Thus do We requite every disbeliever!

# 3697

Therein they will cry: "Our Lord! Bring us out, we shall do righteous good deeds, not that we used to do." (Allah will reply:) "Did We not give you lives long enough, so that whosoever would receive admonition could receive it And the warner came to you. So taste you. For the wrongdoers there is no helper."

# 3698

Verily, Allah is the All-Knower of the Unseen of the heavens and the earth. Verily, He is the All-Knower of that is in the breasts.

# 3699

He it is Who has made you successors generations after generations in the earth, so whosoever disbelieves, on him will be his disbelief. And the disbelief of the disbelievers adds nothing but hatred of their Lord. And the disbelief of the disbelievers adds nothing but loss.

# 3700

Say: "Have you considered your partners whom you call upon besides Allah Show Me, what they have created of the earth. Or have they any share in the heavens Or have We given them a Book, so that they act on clear proof therefrom Nay, the wrongdoers promise one another nothing but delusions."

# 3701

Verily, Allah grasps the heavens and the earth lest they should move away from their places, and if they were to move away from their places, there is not one that could grasp them after Him. Truly, He is Ever Most Forbearing, Oft-Forgiving.

# 3702

And they swore by Allah their most binding oath that if a warner came to them, they would be more guided than any of the nations; yet when a warner came to them, it increased in them nothing but flight (from the truth).

# 3703

(They took to flight because of their) arrogance in the land and their plotting of evil. But the evil plot encompasses only him who makes it. Then, can they expect anything (else) but the Sunnah (way of dealing) of the peoples of old So, no change will you find in Allah's Sunnah, and no turning off will you find in Allah's Sunnah.

# 3704

Have they not traveled in the land, and seen what was the end of those before them -- though they were superior to them in power Allah is not such that anything in the heavens or in the earth escapes Him. Verily, He is All-Knowing, All-Able.

# 3705

And if Allah were to punish men for that which they earned, He would not leave a moving creature on the surface of the earth; but He gives them respite to an appointed term, and when their term comes, then verily, Allah is Ever All-Seer of His servants.

# 3706

Ya Sin.

# 3707

By the Qur'an, full of wisdom,

# 3708

Truly, you are one of the Messengers,

# 3709

On the straight path.

# 3710

Sent down by the Almighty, the Most Merciful,

# 3711

In order that you may warn a people whose forefathers were not warned, so they are heedless.

# 3712

Indeed the Word has proved true against most of them, so they will not believe.

# 3713

Verily, We have put on their necks iron collars reaching to the chins, so that their heads are raised up.

# 3714

And We have put a barrier before them, and a barrier behind them, and We have covered them up, so that they cannot see.

# 3715

It is the same to them whether you warn them or you warn them not, they will not believe.

# 3716

You can only warn him who follows the Reminder, and fears the Most Gracious unseen. Bear you to such one the glad tidings of forgiveness, and a generous reward.

# 3717

Verily, We give life to the dead, and We record that which they send before (them), and their traces and all things We have recorded with numbers in Imam Mubin (a Clear Book).

# 3718

And put forward to them a similitude; the Dwellers of the Town, when there came Messengers to them.

# 3719

When We sent to them two Messengers, they denied them both; so We reinforced them with a third, and they said: "Verily, we have been sent to you as Messengers."

# 3720

They said: "You are only human beings like ourselves, and the Most Gracious has revealed nothing. You are only telling lies."

# 3721

The Messengers said: "Our Lord knows that we have been sent as Messengers to you,"

# 3722

"And our duty is only to convey plainly."

# 3723

They (people) said: "For us, we see an evil omen from you; if you cease not, we will surely stone you, and a painful torment will touch you from us."

# 3724

They (Messengers) said: "Your evil omens be with you! Because you are admonished Nay, but you are a people mischievous."

# 3725

And there came a man running from the farthest part of the town. He said, "O my people! Obey the Messengers."

# 3726

"Obey those who ask no wages of you, and who are rightly guided."

# 3727

"And why should I not worship Him Who has created me and to Whom you shall be returned."

# 3728

"Shall I take besides Him gods If the Most Gracious intends me any harm, their intercession will be of no use for me whatsoever, nor can they save me."

# 3729

"Then verily, I should be in plain error."

# 3730

"Verily, I have believed in your Lord, so listen to me!"

# 3731

It was said: "Enter Paradise." He said: "Would that my people knew."

# 3732

"That my Lord (Allah) has forgiven me, and made me of the honored ones!"

# 3733

And We sent not against his people after him an army from the heaven, nor was it needful for Us to send (such a thing).

# 3734

It was but one Sayhah and lo! they (all) were still.

# 3735

Alas for mankind! There never came a Messenger to them but they used to mock at him.

# 3736

Do they not see how many of the generations We have destroyed before them Verily, they will not return to them.

# 3737

And surely, all -- everyone of them will be brought before Us.

# 3738

And a sign for them is the dead land. We give it life, and We bring forth from it grains, so that they eat thereof.

# 3739

And We have made therein gardens of date palms and grapes, and We have caused springs of water to gush forth therein.

# 3740

So that they may eat of the fruit thereof -- and their hands made it not. Will they not then give thanks

# 3741

Glory be to Him Who has created all the pairs of that which the earth produces, as well as of their own kind, and of that which they know not.

# 3742

And a sign for them is the night. We withdraw therefrom the day, and behold, they are in darkness.

# 3743

And the sun runs on its fixed course for a term (appointed). That is the decree of the Almighty, the All-Knowing.

# 3744

And the moon, We have decreed for it stages, till it returns like the old dried curved date stalk.

# 3745

It is not for the sun to overtake the moon, nor does the night outstrip the day. They all float, each in an orbit.

# 3746

And an Ayah for them is that We bore their offspring in the laden ship.

# 3747

And We have created for them of the like thereunto, on which they ride.

# 3748

And if We will, We shall drown them, and there will be no shout for them, nor will they be saved.

# 3749

Unless it be a mercy from Us, and as an enjoyment for a while.

# 3750

And when it is said to them: "Beware of that which is before you, and that which is behind you, in order that you may receive mercy."

# 3751

And never came an Ayah from among the Ayat of their Lord to them, but they did turn away from it.

# 3752

And when it is said to them: "Spend of that with which Allah has provided you," those who disbelieve say to those who believe: "Shall we feed those whom, if Allah willed, He would have fed You are only in a plain error."

# 3753

And they say: "When will this promise be fulfilled, if you are truthful"

# 3754

They await only but a single Sayhah which will seize them while they are disputing!

# 3755

Then they will not be able to make bequest, nor they will return to their family.

# 3756

And the Trumpet will be blown and behold from the graves they will come out quickly to their Lord.

# 3757

They will say: "Woe to us! Who has raised us up from our place of sleep." (It will be said to them): "This is what the Most Gracious had promised, and the Messengers spoke truth!"

# 3758

It will be but a single Sayhah, so behold they will all be brought up before Us!

# 3759

This Day, none will be wronged in anything, nor will you be requited anything except that which you used to do.

# 3760

Verily, the dwellers of the Paradise, that Day, will be busy with joyful things.

# 3761

They and their wives will be in pleasant shade, reclining on thrones.

# 3762

They will have therein fruits and all that they ask for.

# 3763

(It will be said to them): "Salam (Peace!)" -- a Word from the Lord, Most Merciful.

# 3764

(It will be said): "And O you the criminals! Get you apart this Day."

# 3765

# 3766

"And that you should worship Me. That is the straight path."

# 3767

"And indeed he did lead astray a great multitude of you. Did you not then understand"

# 3768

This is Hell which you were promised!

# 3769

Burn (enter) therein this Day, for that you used to disbelieve.

# 3770

This Day, We shall seal up their mouths, and their hands will speak to Us, and their legs will bear witness to what they used to earn.

# 3771

And if it had been Our will, We would surely have wiped out their eyes, so that they would struggle for the path, how then would they see

# 3772

And if it had been Our will, We could have transformed them in their places. Then they would have been unable to go forward (move about) nor they could have turned back.

# 3773

And he whom We grant long life -- We reverse him in creation. Will they not then understand

# 3774

And We have not taught him poetry, nor is it suitable for him. This is only a Reminder and a plain Qur'an.

# 3775

That he or it may give warning to him who is living, and that Word may be justified against the disbelievers.

# 3776

Do they not see that We have created for them of what Our Hands have fashioned, the cattle, so that they are their owners.

# 3777

And We have subdued them unto them so that some of them they have for riding and some they eat.

# 3778

And they have (other) benefits from them, and (they get to) drink. Will they not then be grateful

# 3779

And they have taken besides Allah, gods, hoping that they might be helped.

# 3780

They cannot help them, but they will be brought forward as a troop (against those who worshipped them).

# 3781

So, let not their speech then grieve you. Verily, We know what they conceal and what they reveal.

# 3782

Does not man see that We have created him from Nutfah. Yet behold he (stands forth) as an open opponent.

# 3783

And he puts forth for Us a parable, and forgets his own creation. He says: "Who will give life to these bones after they are rotten and have become dust"

# 3784

Say: "He will give life to them Who created them for the first time! And He is the All-Knower of every creation!"

# 3785

He Who produces for you fire out of the green tree, when behold you kindle therewith.

# 3786

Is not He Who created the heavens and the earth, able to create the like of them Yes, indeed! He is the All-Knowing Supreme Creator.

# 3787

Verily, His command, when He intends a thing, is only that He says to it, "Be!" -- and it is!

# 3788

So glorified be He and exalted (above all that they associate with Him), and in Whose Hand is the dominion of all things, and to Him you shall be returned.

# 3789

By those ranged in ranks.

# 3790

By those who drive the clouds in a good way.

# 3791

By those who bring the Dhikr.

# 3793

# 3795

When he said to his people: "Will you not have Taqwa"

# 3913

# 3914

Allah, your Lord and the Lord of your forefathers"

# 3915

# 3916

# 3918

"Salam (peace!) be upon Ilyasin!"

# 3919

Verily, thus do We reward the doers of good.

Verily, he was one of Our believing servants.

# 3921

And verily, Lut was one of the Messengers.

# 3922

When We saved him and his family, all,

# 3923

# 3924

# 3925

# 3926

And verily, Yunus was one of the Messengers.

# 3928

When he ran to the laden ship:

# 3929

Then he (agreed to) cast lots, and he was among the losers.

# 3930

Then a (big) fish swallowed him as he had done an act worthy of blame.

# 3931

Had he not been of them who glorify Allah,

# 3932

He would have indeed remained inside its belly (the fish) till the Day of Resurrection.

# 3933

But We cast him forth on the naked shore while he was sick,

# 3934

# 3935

# 3936

# 3937

# 3938

Or did We create the angels female while they were witnesses

# 3939

Verily, it is of their falsehood that they say:

# 3940

# 3941

Has He (then) chosen daughters rather than sons

# 3942

What is the matter with you How do you decide

# 3943

Will you not then remember

# 3944

Or is there for you a plain authority

# 3945

# 3946

And they have invented a kinship between Him and the Jinn, but the Jinn know well that they have indeed to appear (before Him).

# 3947

Glorified be Allah! (He is free) from what they attribute unto Him!

# 3948

Except the servants of Allah, whom He chooses.

# 3949

So, verily you and those whom you worship

# 3950

Cannot lead astray,

# 3951

Except those who are predestined to burn in Hell!

# 3955

# 3956

# 3957

# 3970

# 3971

Sad. By the Qur'an full of reminding.

# 3972

Those who disbelieve are in false pride and opposition.

# 3973

How many a generation have We destroyed before them! And they cried out when there was no longer time for escape.

# 3974

# 3975

"Has he made the gods into One God. Verily, this is a curious thing!"

# 3976

And the leaders among them went about (saying): "Go on, and remain constant to your gods! Verily, this is a thing designed!"

# 3977

"We have not heard (the like) of this in the religion of these later days. This is nothing but an invention!"

# 3978

"Has the Reminder been sent down to him (alone) from among us" Nay, but they are in doubt about My Reminder! Nay, but they have not tasted (My) torment!

# 3979

Or have they the treasures of the mercy of your Lord, the Almighty, the Real Bestower

# 3980

# 3981

They will be a defeated host like the Confederates of the old times.

# 3982

Before them denied -- the people of Nuh; and \`Ad; and Fir\`awn the man of stakes,

# 3983

# 3984

Not one of them but denied the Messengers; therefore My torment was justified.

# 3985

And these only wait for a single Sayhah there will be no pause or ending thereto.

# 3986

They say: "Our Lord! Hasten to us Qittana before the Day of Reckoning!"

# 3987

Be patient of what they say and remember Our slave Dawud, endued with Al-Ayd. Verily, he was ever oft-returning in all matters and in repentance.

# 3988

Verily, We made the mountains to glorify Our praises with him in the \`Ashi and Ishraq.

# 3989

And (so did) the birds assembled, all obedient to him.

# 3990

We made his kingdom strong and gave him Al-Hikmah and sound judgement in speech and decision.

# 3991

And has the news of the litigants reached you When they climbed over the wall into (his) Mihrab (private chamber of worship);

# 3992

When they entered in upon Dawud, he was terrified of them. They said: "Fear not! (We are) two litigants, one of us has wronged the other, therefore judge between us with truth, and treat us not with injustice, and guide us to the right way.

# 3993

Verily, this my brother (in religion) has ninety-nine ewes, while I have (only) one ewe, and he says: "Hand it over to me, and he overpowered me in speech."

# 3994

\[Dawud\] said: "He has wronged you in demanding your ewe in addition to his ewes. And, verily, many partners oppress one another, except those who believe and do righteous good deeds, and they are few." And Dawud guessed that We have tried him and he sought forgiveness of his Lord, and he fell down prostrate and turned (to Allah) in repentance.

# 3995

So, We forgave him that, and verily, for him is a near access to Us, and a good place of return.

# 3996

O Dawud! Verily, We have placed you as a successor on the earth; so judge you between men in truth (and justice) and follow not your desire -- for it will mislead you from the path of Allah. Verily, those who wander astray from the path of Allah (shall) have a severe torment, because they forgot the Day of Reckoning.

# 3997

And We created not the heaven and the earth and all that is between them without purpose! That is the consideration of those who disbelieve! Then woe to those who disbelieve from the Fire!

# 3998

Shall We treat those who believe and do righteous good deeds as those who cause mischief on the earth Or shall We treat those who have Taqwa as the evildoers

# 3999

(This is) a Book which We have sent down to you, full of blessings, that they may ponder over its Verses, and that men of understanding may remember.

# 4000

And to Dawud We gave Sulayman. How excellent a servant! Verily, he was ever turning in repentance (to Us)!

# 4001

When there were displayed before him, in the afternoon, well trained horses of the highest breed.

# 4002

He said: "I did love the good instead of remembering my Lord," till the time was over, and (the sun) had hidden in the veil (of night).

# 4003

Then he said: "Bring them back to me." Then he began to pass his hand over their legs and their necks.

# 4004

And indeed, We tried Sulayman and We placed on his throne Jasad (a body), and he returned.

# 4005

He said: "My Lord! Forgive me, and bestow upon me a kingdom such as shall not belong to any other after me. Verily, You are the Bestower."

# 4006

So, We subjected to him the wind; it blew gently by his order wherever he willed,

# 4007

And the Shayatin, from every kind of builder and diver,

# 4008

And also others bound in fetters.

# 4009

\[Allah said to Sulayman\]: "This is Our gift, so spend you or withhold, no account will be asked of you."

# 4010

And verily, for him is a near access to Us, and a good (final) return.

# 4011

And remember Our servant Ayyub, when he invoked his Lord (saying): "Verily, Shaytan has afflicted me with distress and torment!"

# 4012

(Allah said to him): "Strike the ground with your foot. This is (a spring of) water to wash in, cool and a drink."

# 4013

And We gave him (back) his family, and along with them the like thereof, as a mercy from Us, and a reminder for those who understand.

# 4014

"And take in your hand a bundle of thin grass and strike therewith (your wife), and break not your oath." Truly, We found him patient. How excellent a servant! Verily, he was ever oft-returning in repentance (to Us)!

# 4015

And remember Our servants, Ibrahim, Ishaq, and Ya\`qub, Ulil-Aydi wal-Absar.

# 4016

# 4017

# 4018

# 4019

This is a Reminder. And verily, for those who have Taqwa is a good final return.

# 4020

\`Adn Paradise, whose doors will be opened for them.

# 4021

# 4027

# 4028

And other of similar kind - all together!

# 4029

# 4030

# 4031

# 4032

# 4033

Verily, that is the very truth -- the mutual dispute of the people of the Fire!

# 4035

# 4038

# 4041

# 4059

The revelation of this Book is from Allah, the Almighty, the All-Wise.

# 4060

Verily, We have sent down the Book to you in truth. So, worship Allah by doing religious deeds sincerely for Him only.

# 4061

Surely, the religion is for Allah only. And those who take protectors besides Him (say): "We worship them only that they may bring us near to Allah." Verily, Allah will judge between them concerning that wherein they differ. Truly, Allah guides not him who is a liar, and a disbeliever.

# 4062

Had Allah willed to take a son, He could have chosen whom He willed out of those whom He created. But glory be to Him! He is Allah, the One, the Irresistible.

# 4063

He has created the heavens and the earth with truth. He makes the night to go in the day and makes the day to go in the night. And He has subjected the sun and the moon. Each running for an appointed term. Verily, He is the Almighty, the Oft-Forgiving.

# 4064

He created you (all) from a single person; then made from him his wife. And He has sent down for you of An\`am eight pairs. He creates you in the wombs of your mothers, creation after creation in three veils of darkness. Such is Allah your Lord. His is the kingdom. La ilaha illa Huwa. How then are you turned away

# 4065

If you disbelieve, then verily, Allah is not in need of you; He likes not disbelief for His servants. And if you are grateful, He is pleased therewith for you. No bearer of burdens shall bear the burden of another. Then to your Lord is your return, and He will inform you what you used to do. Verily, He is the All-Knower of that which is in breasts.

# 4066

And when some hurt touches man, he cries to his Lord, turning to Him in repentance. But when He bestows a favor upon him from Himself, he forgets that for which he cried for before, and he sets up rivals to Allah, in order to mislead others from His path. Say: "Take pleasure in your disbelief for a while, surely, you are (one) of the dwellers of the Fire!"

# 4067

Is one who is obedient to Allah, Ana'a Al-Layl prostrating and standing fearing the Hereafter and hoping for the mercy of his Lord Say: "Are those who know equal to those who know not" It is only men of understanding who will remember.

# 4068

Say: "O My servants who believe, have Taqwa of your Lord. Good is for those who do good in this world, and Allah's earth is spacious! Only those who are patient shall receive their reward in full, without reckoning."

# 4069

# 4070

"And I am commanded (this) in order that I may be the first of the Muslims."

# 4071

Say: "Verily, if I disobey my Lord, I am afraid of the torment of a great Day."

# 4072

# 4073

"So, worship what you like besides Him." Say: "The losers are those who will lose themselves and their families on the Day of Resurrection. Verily, that will be a manifest loss!"

# 4074
