# 4075

Those who avoid At-Taghut by not worshipping them and turn to Allah, for them are glad tidings; so announce the good news to My servants.

# 4076

Those who listen to the Word and follow the best thereof, those are (the ones) whom Allah has guided and those are men of understanding.

# 4077

Is, then one against whom the Word of punishment is justified (equal to the one who avoids evil) Will you rescue him who is in the Fire

# 4078

But those who have Taqwa of their Lord, for them are built lofty rooms, one above another under which rivers flow. (This is) the promise of Allah, and Allah does not fail in (His) promise.

# 4079

See you not that Allah sends down water from the sky, and causes it to penetrate the earth, as water springs, and afterward thereby produces crops of different colors, and afterward they wither and you see them turn yellow; then He makes them dry and broken pieces. Verily, in this is a reminder for men of understanding.

# 4080

Is he whose breast Allah has opened to Islam, so that he is in light from his Lord So, woe to those whose hearts are hardened against remembrance of Allah! They are in plain error!

# 4081

Allah has sent down the Best Statement, a Book, its parts resembling each other, (and) oft-repeated. The skins of those who fear their Lord shiver from it. Then their skin and their heart soften to the remembrance of Allah. That is the guidance of Allah. He guides therewith whom He wills; and whomever Allah sends astray, for him there is no guide.

# 4082

Is he then, who will confront with his face the awful torment on the Day of Resurrection And it will be said to the wrongdoers: "Taste what you used to earn!"

# 4083

Those before them denied, and so the torment came on them from directions they perceived not.

# 4084

So, Allah made them to taste the disgrace in the present life, but greater is the torment of the Hereafter if they only knew!

# 4085

And indeed We have put forth for men, in this Qur'an every kind of parable in order that they may remember.

# 4086

An Arabic Qur'an, without any crookedness (therein) in order that they may have Taqwa of Him.

# 4087

Allah puts forth a parable: a man belonging to many partners disputing with one another, and a man belonging entirely to one master. Are those two equal in comparison All the praises and thanks be to Allah! But most of them know not.

# 4088

Verily, you will die, and verily, they (too) will die.

# 4089

Then, on the Day of Resurrection, you will be disputing before your Lord.

# 4090

Then, who does more wrong than one who utters a lie against Allah, and denies the truth when it comes to him! Is there not in Hell an abode for the disbelievers

# 4091

And he who has brought the truth and (those who) believed therein, they are those who have Taqwa.

# 4092

They shall have all that they will desire with their Lord. That is the reward of the doers of good.

# 4093

So that Allah may expiate from them the evil of what they did and give them the reward, according to the best of what they used to do.

# 4094

Is not Allah Sufficient for His servant Yet they try to frighten you with those besides Him! And whom Allah sends astray, for him there will be no guide.

# 4095

And whomsoever Allah guides, for him there will be no misleader. Is not Allah Almighty, Possessor of Retribution

# 4096

And verily, if you ask them: "Who created the heavens and the earth" Surely, they will say: "Allah." Say: "Tell me then, the things that you invoke besides Allah -- if Allah intended some harm for me, could they remove His harm Or if He intended some mercy for me, could they withhold His mercy" Say: "Sufficient for me is Allah; in Him those who trust must put their trust."

# 4097

Say: "O My people! Work according to your way, I am working. Then you will come to know"

# 4098

"To whom comes a disgracing torment, and on whom descends an everlasting torment."

# 4099

Verily, We have sent down to you the Book for mankind in truth. So, whosoever accepts the guidance, it is only for himself; and whosoever goes astray, he goes astray only to his (own) loss. And you are not a trustee over them.

# 4100

It is Allah Who takes away the souls at the time of their death, and those that die not during their sleep. He keeps those (souls) for which He has ordained death and sends the rest for a term appointed. Verily, in this are signs for a people who think deeply.

# 4101

Have they taken as intercessors besides Allah Say: "Even if they have power over nothing whatever and have no intelligence"

# 4102

Say: "To Allah belongs all intercession. His is the sovereignty of the heavens and the earth. Then to Him you shall be brought back."

# 4103

And when Allah Alone is mentioned, the hearts of those who believe not in the Hereafter are filled with disgust and when those besides Him are mentioned, behold, they rejoice!

# 4104

Say: "O Allah! Creator of the heavens and the earth! All-Knower of the unseen and the seen! You will judge between your servants about that wherein they used to differ."

# 4105

And those who did wrong, if they had all that is on the earth and therewith as much again, they verily, would offer it to ransom themselves therewith on the Day of Resurrection from the evil torment; and there will become apparent to them from Allah what they had not been reckoning.

# 4106

And the evils of that which they earned will become apparent to them, and that which they used to mock at will encircle them.

# 4107

When harm touches man, he calls to Us (for help); then when We have changed it into a favor from Us, he says: "Only because of knowledge I obtained it." Nay, it is only a trial, but most of them know not!

# 4108

Verily, those before them said it, yet (all) that they had earned availed them not.

# 4109

So, the evil results of that which they earned overtook them. And those who did wrong of these will also be overtaken by the evil results for that which they earned; and they will never be able to escape.

# 4110

Do they not know that Allah expands the provision for whom He wills, and straitens it. Verily, in this are signs for the folk who believe!

# 4111

Say: "O My servants who have transgressed against themselves! Despair not of the mercy of Allah, verily, Allah forgives all sins. Truly, He is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful."

# 4112

"And turn in repentance (and in obedience with true faith) to your Lord and submit to Him before the torment comes upon you, (and) then you will not be helped."

# 4113

"And follow the best of that which is sent down to you from your Lord, before the torment comes on you suddenly while you perceive not!"

# 4114

Lest a person should say: "Alas, my grief that I was undutiful to Allah, and I was indeed among those who mocked."

# 4115

Or (lest) he should say: "If only Allah had guided me, I should indeed have been among those who have Taqwa."

# 4116

Or (lest) he should say when he sees the torment: "If only I had another chance, then I should indeed be among the doers of good."

# 4117

Yes! Verily, there came to you My Ayat and you denied them, and were proud and were among the disbelievers.

# 4118

And on the Day of Resurrection you will see those who lied against Allah - their faces will be black. Is there not in Hell an abode for the arrogant

# 4119

And Allah will deliver those who have Taqwa to their places of success. Evil shall touch them not, nor shall they grieve.

# 4120

Allah is the Creator of all things, and He is the Trustee over all things.

# 4121

To Him belong the Maqalid of the heavens and the earth. And those who disbelieve in the Ayat of Allah, such are they who will be the losers.

# 4122

Say: "Do you order me to worship other than Allah O you fools!"

# 4123

And indeed it has been revealed to you, as it was to those before you: "If you join others in worship with Allah, surely your deeds will be in vain, and you will certainly be among the losers."

# 4124

Nay! But worship Allah, and be among the grateful.

# 4125

They made not a just estimate of Allah such as is due to Him. And on the Day of Resurrection the whole of the earth will be grasped by His Hand and the heavens will be rolled up in His Right Hand. Glorified be He, and High be He above all that they associate as partners with Him!

# 4126

And the Trumpet will be blown, and all who are in the heavens and all who are on the earth will swoon away, except him whom Allah wills. Then it will be blown another time, and behold they will be standing, looking on.

# 4127

And the earth will shine with the light of its Lord, and the Book will be presented, and the Prophets and the witnesses will be brought forward, and it will be judged between them with truth, and they will not be wronged.

# 4128

And each person will be paid in full of what he did; and He is Best Aware of what they do.

# 4129

And those who disbelieved will be driven to Hell in groups till when they reach it, the gates thereof will be opened. And its keepers will say: "Did not the Messengers come to you from yourselves, reciting to you the Ayat of your Lord, and warning you of the meeting of this Day of yours" They will say: "Yes," but the Word of torment has been justified against the disbelievers!

# 4130

It will be said: "Enter you the gates of Hell, to abide therein. And what an evil abode of the arrogant!"

# 4131

And those who had Taqwa will be led to Paradise in groups till when they reach it, and its gates will be opened and its keepers will say: "Salam \`Alaykum (peace be upon you)! You have done well, so enter here to abide therein forever."

# 4132

And they will say: "All the praises and thanks be to Allah Who has fulfilled His promise to us and has made us inherit the land. We can dwell in Paradise where we will; how excellent a reward for the workers!"

# 4133

And you will see the angels surrounding the Throne from all round, glorifying the praises of their Lord. And they will be judged with truth. And it will be said, "All the praises and thanks be to Allah, the Lord of all that exits."

# 4134

Ha Mim.

# 4135

The revelation of the Book is from Allah, the Almighty, the All-Knower.

# 4136

The Forgiver of sin, the Acceptor of repentance, the Severe in punishment, the Bestower. La ilaha illa Huwa, to Him is the final return.

# 4137

None disputes in the Ayat of Allah but those who disbelieve. So let not their ability of going about here and there through the land (for their purposes) deceive you!

# 4138

The people of Nuh and the groups after them denied before these; and every nation plotted against their Messenger to seize him, and disputed by means of falsehood to refute therewith the truth. So I seized them, and how was My punishment!

# 4139

Thus has the Word of your Lord been justified against those who disbelieved, that they will be the dwellers of the Fire.

# 4140

Those (angels) who bear the Throne (of Allah) and those around it glorify the praises of their Lord, and believe in Him, and ask forgiveness for those who believe (saying): "Our Lord! You comprehend all things in mercy and knowledge, so forgive those who repent and follow Your way, and save them from the torment of the blazing Fire!

# 4141

Our Lord! And make them enter the \`Adn (Eternal) Gardens which you have promised them -- and to the righteous among their fathers, their wives, and their offspring! Verily, You are the Almighty, the All-Wise.

# 4142

And save them from the sins, and whomsoever You save from the sins that Day, him verily, You have taken into mercy." And that is the supreme success.

# 4143

Those who disbelieve will be addressed: "Indeed, Allah's aversion was greater towards you than your aversion toward yourselves, when you were called to the Faith but you used to refuse."

# 4144

They will say: "Our Lord! You have made us to die twice, and You have given us life twice! Now we confess our sins, then is there any way to get out"

# 4145

(It will be said): "This is because, when Allah Alone was invoked, you disbelieved; but when partners were joined to Him, you believed! So the judgement is only with Allah, the Most High, the Most Great!"

# 4146

It is He Who shows you His Ayat and sends down provision for you from the sky. And none remembers but those who turn in repentance.

# 4147

So, call you upon Allah making religion sincerely for Him, however much the disbelievers may hate.

# 4148

(He is Allah) Owner of high ranks and degrees, the Owner of the Throne. He sends the revelation by His command to any of His servants He wills, that he may warn of the Day of Mutual Meeting.

# 4149

The Day when they will come out, nothing of them will be hidden from Allah. Whose is the kingdom this Day It is Allah's, the One, the Irresistible!

# 4150

This Day shall every person be recompensed for what he earned. This Day no injustice. Truly, Allah is swift in reckoning.

# 4151

And warn them of the Day that is drawing near, when the hearts will be at the throats Kazimin. There will be no friend, nor an intercessor for the wrongdoers, who could be given heed to.

# 4152

Allah knows the fraud of the eyes, and all that the breasts conceal.

# 4153

And Allah judges with truth, while those to whom they invoke besides Him, cannot judge anything. Certainly, Allah! He is the All-Hearer, the All-Seer.

# 4154

Have they not traveled in the land and seen what was the end of those who were before them They were superior to them in strength, and in the traces in the land. But Allah seized them with punishment for their sins. And none had they to protect them from Allah.

# 4155

That was because there came to them their Messengers with clear evidences but they disbelieved (in them). So Allah seized them. Verily, He is All-Strong, Severe in punishment.

# 4156

And indeed We sent Musa with Our Ayat, and a manifest authority,

# 4157

To Fir\`awn, Haman and Qarun, but they called (him): "A sorcerer, a liar!"

# 4158

Then, when he brought them the Truth from Us, they said: "Kill with him the sons of those who believe and let their women live;" but the plots of disbelievers are nothing but in vain!

# 4159

Fir\`awn said: "Leave me to kill Musa, and let him call his Lord! I fear that he may change your religion, or that he may cause mischief to appear in the land!"

# 4160

Musa said: "Verily, I seek refuge in my Lord and your Lord from every arrogant who believes not in the Day of Reckoning!"

# 4161

And a believing man of Fir\`awn's family, who hid his Faith said: "Would you kill a man because he says: \`My Lord is Allah,' and he has come to you with clear signs from your Lord And if he is a liar, upon him will be (the sin of) his lie; but if he is telling the truth, then some of that (calamity) wherewith he threatens you will befall on you." Verily, Allah guides not one who is a transgressor, a liar!

# 4162

"O my people! Yours is the kingdom today, you being dominant in the land. But who will save us from the torment of Allah, should it befall us" Fir\`awn said: "I show you only that which I see, and I guide you only to the path of right policy!"

# 4163

And he who believed said: "O my people! Verily, I fear for you an end like that day (of disaster) of the groups (of old)!"

# 4164

"Like the end of the people of Nuh, and \`Ad, and Thamud and those who came after them. And Allah wills no injustice for (His) servants."

# 4165

"And, O my people! Verily, I fear for you the Day when there will be mutual calling."

# 4166

A Day when you will turn your backs and flee having no protector from Allah. And whomsoever Allah sends astray, for him there is no guide.

# 4167

And indeed Yusuf did come to you, in times gone by, with clear signs, but you ceased not to doubt in that which he did bring to you, till when he died, you said: "No Messenger will Allah send after him." Thus Allah leaves astray him who is a transgressor and a skeptic.

# 4168

Those who dispute about the Ayat of Allah, without any authority that has come to them, it is greatly hateful and disgusting to Allah and to those who believe. Thus does Allah seal up the heart of every arrogant, tyrant.

# 4169

And Fir\`awn said: "O Haman! Build me a lofty tower that I may arrive at the ways --

# 4170

The ways of the heavens, and I may look upon the God of Musa, but verily, I think him to be a liar." Thus it was made fair seeming, in Fir\`awn's eyes, the evil of his deeds, and he was hindered from the path; and the plot of Fir\`awn led to nothing but loss and destruction.

# 4171

And the man who believed said: "O my people! Follow me, I will guide you to the way of right conduct."

# 4172

"O my people! Truly, this life of the world is nothing but an enjoyment, and verily, the Hereafter that is the home that will remain forever."

# 4173

"Whoever does an evil deed, will not be requited except the like thereof; and whosoever does a righteous deed, whether male or female and is a true believer, such will enter Paradise, where they will be provided therein without limit."

# 4174

"And O my people! How is it that I call you to salvation while you call me to the Fire!"

# 4175

"You invite me to disbelieve in Allah, and to join partners in worship with Him of which I have no knowledge; and I invite you to the Almighty, the Oft-Forgiving!"

# 4176

"La Jarama, you call me to one that does not have a claim in this world or in the Hereafter. And our return will be to Allah, and the transgressors, they shall be the dwellers of the Fire!"

# 4177

"And you will remember what I am telling you, and my affair I leave it to Allah. Verily, Allah is the All-Seer of (His) servants."

# 4178

So, Allah saved him from the evils that they plotted (against him), while an evil torment encompassed Fir\`awn's people.

# 4179

The Fire, they are exposed to it, morning and afternoon. And on the Day when the Hour will be established (it will be said to the angels): "Admit Fir\`awn's people into the severest torment!"

# 4180

And, when they will dispute in the Fire, the weak will say to those who were arrogant: "Verily, we followed you, can you then take from us some portion of the Fire"

# 4181

Those who were arrogant will say: "We are all (together) in this (Fire)! Verily, Allah has judged between (His) servants!"

# 4182

And those in the Fire will say to the keepers (angels) of Hell: "Call upon your Lord to lighten for us the torment for a day!"

# 4183

They will say: "Did there not come to you, your Messengers with (clear) evidences" They will say: "Yes." They will reply: "Then call (as you like)! And the invocation of the disbelievers is nothing but in vain!"

# 4184

Verily, We will indeed make victorious Our Messengers and those who believe in this world's life and on the Day when the witnesses will stand forth, --

# 4185

The Day when their excuses will be of no profit to wrongdoers. Theirs will be the curse, and theirs will be the evil abode.

# 4186

And, indeed We gave Musa the guidance, and We caused the Children of Israel to inherit the Scripture --

# 4187

A guide and a reminder for men of understanding.

# 4188

So be patient. Verily, the promise of Allah is true, and ask forgiveness for your fault, and glorify the praises of your Lord in the \`Ashi and in the Ibkar.

# 4189

Verily, those who dispute about the Ayat of Allah, without any authority having come to them, there is nothing else in their breasts except pride. They will never have it. So seek refuge in Allah. Verily, it is He Who is the All-Hearer, the All-Seer.

# 4190

The creation of the heavens and the earth is indeed greater than the creation of mankind; yet, most of the people do not know.

# 4191

And not equal are the blind and those who see; nor those who believe, and do righteous good deeds, and those who do evil. Little do you remember!

# 4192

Verily, the Hour is surely coming, there is no doubt about it, yet most men believe not.

# 4193

And your Lord said: "Call upon Me, I will answer you. Verily, those who scorn My worship they will surely enter Hell in humiliation!"

# 4194

Allah, it is He Who has made the night for you that you may rest therein and the day for you to see. Truly, Allah is full of bounty to mankind; yet, most of mankind give no thanks.

# 4195

That is Allah, your Lord, the Creator of all things, La ilaha ila Huwa. How then are you turning away

# 4196

Thus were turned away those who used to deny the Ayat of Allah.

# 4197

Allah, it is He Who has made for you the earth as a dwelling place and the sky as a canopy, and has given you shape and made your shapes good and pure (looking) and has provided you with good things. That is Allah, your Lord, so Blessed be Allah, the Lord of all that exists.

# 4198

He is the Ever Living, La ilaha illa Huwa; so invoke Him making the religion for Him Alone. All the praises and thanks be to Allah, the Lord of all that exits.

# 4199

Say: "I have been forbidden to worship those whom you worship besides Allah, since there have come to me evidences from my Lord; and I am commanded to submit to the Lord of all that exists.

# 4200

It is He, Who has created you from dust, then from a Nutfah then from a clot (a piece of coagulated blood), then brings you forth as an infant, then (makes you grow) to reach the age of full strength, and afterwards to be old -- though some among you die before -- and that you reach an appointed term in order that you may understand.

# 4201

It is He Who gives life and causes death. And when He decides upon a thing He says to it only: "Be!" - and it is.

# 4202

See you not those who dispute about the Ayat of Allah How are they turning away

# 4203

Those who deny the Book, and that with which We sent Our Messengers they will come to know.

# 4204

When iron collars will be rounded over their necks, and the chains, they shall be dragged along,

# 4205

In the boiling water, then they will be burned in the Fire.

# 4206

Then it will be said to them: "Where are (all) those whom you used to consider partners"

# 4207

"Besides Allah" They will say: "They have vanished from us. Nay, we did not call upon anything before." Thus Allah leads astray the disbelievers.

# 4208

That was because you had been exulting in the earth without any right, and that you used to rejoice extremely.

# 4209

Enter the gates of Hell to abide therein, and (indeed) what an evil abode of the arrogant!

# 4210

So be patient, verily, the promise of Allah is true and whether We show you some part of what We have promised them, or We cause you to die, then still it is to Us they all shall be returned.

# 4211

And, indeed We have sent Messengers before you, of some of them We have related to you their story. And of some We have not related to you their story, and it was not given to any Messenger that he should bring a sign except by the leave of Allah. But, when comes the commandment of Allah, the matter will be decided with truth, and the followers of falsehood will then be lost.

# 4212

Allah, it is He Who has made cattle for you, that you may ride on some of them, and of some you eat.

# 4213

And you have (many other) benefits from them, and that you may reach by their means a desire that is in your breasts, and on them and on ships you are carried.

# 4214

And He shows you His Ayat. Which, then of the Ayat of Allah do you deny

# 4215

Have they not traveled through the earth and seen what was the end of those before them They were more in number than them and mightier in strength, and in the traces in the land; yet all that they used to earn availed them not.

# 4216

Then when their Messengers came to them with clear proofs, they were glad (and proud) with that which they had of the knowledge (of worldly things). And that at which they used to mock, surrounded them.

# 4217

So when they saw Our punishment, they said: "We believe in Allah Alone and reject (all) that we used to associate with Him as (His) partners."

# 4218

Then their Faith could not avail them when they saw Our punishment. (Like) this has been the way of Allah in dealing with His servants. And there the disbelievers lost utterly.

# 4219

Ha Mim.

# 4220

A revelation from the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful.

# 4221

A Book whereof the Ayat are explained in detail -- a Qur'an in Arabic for people who know.

# 4222

Giving glad tidings and warning, but most of them turn away, so they hear not.

# 4223

And they say: "Our hearts are under coverings from that to which you invite us; and in our ears is deafness, and between us and you is a screen, so work you (on your way); verily, we are working (on our way)."

# 4224

Say: "I am only a human being like you. It is revealed to me that your God is One God, therefore take straight path to Him and obedience to Him, and seek forgiveness of Him. And woe to the polytheists.

# 4225

Those who give not the Zakah and they are disbelievers in the Hereafter.

# 4226

Truly, those who believe and do righteous good deeds, for them will be an endless reward that will never stop.

# 4227

Say: "Do you verily disbelieve in Him Who created the earth in two Days And you set up rivals with Him That is the Lord of all that exists."

# 4228

He placed therein firm mountains from above it, and He blessed it, and measured therein its sustenance in four Days equal for all those who ask.

# 4229

Then He rose over (Istawa ila) the heaven when it was smoke, and said to it and to the earth: "Come both of you willingly or unwillingly." They both said: "We come willingly."

# 4230

Then He completed and finished their creation (as) seven heavens in two Days and He made in each heaven its affair. And We adorned the nearest (lowest) heaven with lamps (stars) to be an adornment as well as to guard. Such is the decree of Him, the Almighty, the All-Knower.

# 4231

But if they turn away, then say: "I have warned you of a Sa\`iqah like the Sa\`iqah which overtook \`Ad and Thamud."

# 4232

When the Messengers came to them, from before them and behind them (saying): "Worship none but Allah," they said: "If our Lord had so willed, He would surely have sent down the angels. So, indeed we disbelieve in that with which you have been sent."

# 4233

As for \`Ad, they were arrogant in the land without right, and they said: "Who is mightier than us in strength" See they not that Allah Who created them was mightier in strength than them. And they used to deny Our Ayat!

# 4234

So, We sent upon them a Sarsar wind in days of calamity that We might give them a taste of disgracing torment in this present worldly life. But surely the torment of the Hereafter will be more disgracing, and they will never be helped.

# 4235

And as for Thamud, We showed them the path of truth but they preferred blindness to guidance; so the Sa\`iqah of disgracing torment seized them because of what they used to earn.

# 4236

And We saved those who believed and had Taqwa.

# 4237

And (remember) the Day that the enemies of Allah will be gathered to the Fire, then they will be driven.

# 4238

Till, when they reach it, their hearing (ears) and their eyes and their skins will testify against them as to what they used to do.

# 4239

And they will say to their skins, "Why do you testify against us" They will say: "Allah has caused us to speak - as He causes all things to speak, and He created you the first time, and to Him you are made to return."

# 4240

And you have not been hiding yourselves (in the world), lest your ears and your eyes and your skins should testify against you; but you thought that Allah knew not much of what you were doing.

# 4241

And that thought of yours which you thought about your Lord, has brought you to destruction; and you have become of those utterly lost!

# 4242

Then, if they bear the torment patiently, then the Fire is the home for them, and if they seek to please Allah, yet they are not of those who will ever be allowed to please Allah.

# 4243

And We have assigned for them intimate companions (in this world), who have made fair seeming to them, what was before them and what was behind them. And the Word is justified against them as it was justified against those who were among the previous generations of Jinn and men that had passed away before them. Indeed they (all) were the losers.

# 4244

And those who disbelieve say: "Listen not to this Qur'an, and make noise in the midst of its (recitation) that you may overcome."

# 4245

But surely, We shall cause those who disbelieve to taste a severe torment, and certainly, We shall requite them the worst of what they used to do.

# 4246

That is the recompense of the enemies of Allah: the Fire. Therein will be for them the eternal home, a recompense for that they used to deny Our Ayat.

# 4247

And those who disbelieve will say: "Our Lord! Show us those among Jinn and men who led us astray, that we may crush them under our feet so that they become the lowest."

# 4248

Verily, those who say: "Our Lord is Allah," and then they stand firm, on them the angels will descend (saying): "Fear not, nor grieve! But receive the glad tidings of Paradise which you have been promised!"

# 4249

"We have been your friends in the life of this world and are (so) in the Hereafter. Therein you shall have (all) that your souls desire, and therein you shall have (all) for which you ask."

# 4250

"An entertainment from the Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful."

# 4251

And who is better in speech than he who invites to Allah, and does righteous deeds, and says: "I am one of the Muslims."

# 4252

The good deed and the evil deed cannot be equal. Repel (the evil) with one which is better, then verily he, between whom and you there was enmity, (will become) as though he was a close friend.

# 4253

But none is granted it except those who are patient -- and none is granted it except the owner of the great portion in this world.

# 4254

And if an evil whisper from Shaytan tries to turn you away, then seek refuge in Allah. Verily, He is the All-Hearer, the All-Knower.

# 4255

And from among His signs are the night and the day, and the sun and the moon. Do not prostrate yourselves to the sun nor to the moon, but prostrate yourselves to Allah Who created them, if you worship Him.

# 4256

But if they are too proud, then there are those who are with your Lord glorify Him night and day, and never are they tired.

# 4257

And among His signs; that you see the earth barren, but when We send down water to it, it is stirred to life and growth. Verily, He Who gives it life, surely is able to give life to the dead. Indeed He is Able to do all things.

# 4258

Verily, those who Yulhiduna Fi Our Ayat are not hidden from Us. Is he who is cast into the Fire better or he who comes secure on the Day of Resurrection Do what you will. Verily, He is All-Seer of what you do.

# 4259

Verily, those who disbelieved in the Reminder when it came to them. And verily, it is an honorable well-fortified respected Book.

# 4260

Falsehood cannot come to it from before it or behind it, (it is) sent down by the All-Wise, Worthy of all praise.

# 4261

Nothing is said to you except what was said to the Messengers before you. Verily, your Lord is the Possessor of forgiveness, and (also) the Possessor of painful punishment.

# 4262

And if We had sent this as a Qur'an in a foreign language, they would have said: "Why are not its verses explained in detail What! Not in Arabic nor an Arab" Say: "It is for those who believe, a guide and a cure. And as for those who disbelieve, there is heaviness in their ears, and it is blindness for them. They are called from a place far away."

# 4263

And indeed We gave Musa the Scripture, but dispute arose therein. And had it not been for a Word that went forth before from your Lord, and the matter would have been settled between them. But truly, they are in grave doubt thereto.

# 4264

Whosoever does righteous good deed, it is for himself; and whosoever does evil, it is against himself. And your Lord is not at all unjust to (His) servants.

# 4265

To Him is referred the knowledge of the Hour. No fruit comes out of its sheath, nor does a female conceive nor brings forth (young), except by His knowledge. And on the Day when He will call unto them (saying): "Where are My (so-called) partners" They will say: "We inform You that none of us bears witness to it!"

# 4266

And those whom they used to invoke before (in this world) shall disappear from them, and they will perceive that they have no place of refuge.

# 4267

Man does not get tired of asking for good; but if an evil touches him, then he gives up all hope and is lost in despair.

# 4268

And truly, if We give him a taste of mercy from Us, after some adversity has touched him, he is sure to say: "This is due to my (merit); I think not that the Hour will be established. But if I am brought back to my Lord, surely there will be for me the best with Him. "Then, We verily will show to the disbelievers what they have done, and We shall make them taste a severe torment.

# 4269

And when We show favor to man, he turns away and becomes arrogant; but when evil touches him, then he has recourse to long supplications.

# 4270

Say: "Tell me, if it is from Allah, and you disbelieve in it Who is more astray than one who is in opposition far away."

# 4271

We will show them Our signs in the universes, and within themselves, until it becomes manifest to them that this is the truth. Is it not sufficient in regard to your Lord that He is a Witness over all things

# 4272

Lo, Verily, they are in doubt concerning the meeting with their Lord. Verily, He is surrounding all things!

# 4273

Ha Mim.

# 4274

\`Ain Sin Qaf.

# 4275

Likewise Allah, the Almighty, the All-Wise sends revelation to you as to those before you.

# 4276

To Him belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is on the earth, and He is the Most High, the Most Great.

# 4277

Nearly the heavens might be rent asunder from above them, and the angels glorify the praises of their Lord, and ask for forgiveness for those on the earth. Lo, Verily, Allah is the Oft-Forgiving, the Most Merciful.

# 4278

And as for those who take as protecting friends others besides Him -- Allah is Hafiz over them, and you are not a trustee over them.

# 4279

And thus We have revealed to you a Qur'an in Arabic that you may warn the Mother of the Towns and all around it, and warn (them) of the Day of Assembling of which there is no doubt, a party will be in Paradise and a party in the blazing Fire.

# 4280

And if Allah had willed, He could have made them one nation, but He admits whom He wills to His mercy. And the wrongdoers will have neither a protector nor a helper.

# 4281

Or have they taken protecting friends besides Him But Allah --- He Alone is the protector. And He Who gives life to the dead, and He is Able to do all things.

# 4282

And in whatsoever you differ, the decision thereof is with Allah. Such is Allah, my Lord in Whom I put my trust, and to Him I turn in repentance.

# 4283

The Creator of the heavens and the earth. He has made for you mates from yourselves, and for the cattle (also) mates. By this means He creates you. There is nothing like Him, and He is the All-Hearer, the All-Seer.

# 4284

To Him belong the keys of the heavens and the earth. He enlarges provision for whom He wills, and straitens. Verily, He is the All-Knower of everything.

# 4285

He (Allah) has ordained for you the same religion which He ordained for Nuh, and that which We have revealed to you, and that which We ordained for Ibrahim, Musa and \`Isa saying you should establish religion and make no divisions in it. Intolerable for the idolators is that to which you call them. Allah chooses for Himself whom He wills, and guides unto Himself who turns to Him in repentance.

# 4286

And they divided not till after knowledge had come to them, through transgression between themselves. And had it not been for a Word that went forth before from your Lord for an appointed term, the matter would have been settled between them. And verily, those who were made to inherit the Scripture after them, are in grave doubt concerning it.

# 4287

So unto this then invite (people), and stand firm as you are commanded, and follow not their desires but say: "I believe in whatsoever Allah has sent down of the Book and I am commanded to do justice among you. Allah is our Lord and your Lord. For us our deeds and for you your deeds. There is no dispute between us and you. Allah will assemble us (all), and to Him is the final return."

# 4288

And those who dispute concerning Allah, after it has been accepted, of no use is their dispute before their Lord and on them is wrath, and for them will be a severe torment.

# 4289

It is Allah Who has sent down the Book in truth, and the Balance. And what can make you know that perhaps the Hour is close at hand

# 4290

Those who believe not therein seek to hasten it, while those who believe are fearful of it, and know that it is the very truth. Verily, those who dispute concerning the Hour are certainly in error far away.

# 4291

Allah is very Gracious and Kind to His servants. He gives provisions to whom He wills. And He is the All-Strong, the Almighty.

# 4292

Whosoever desires the reward of the Hereafter, We give him increase in his reward, and whosoever desires the reward of this world, We give him thereof, and he has no portion in the Hereafter.

# 4293

Or have they partners with Allah who have instituted for them a religion which Allah has not ordained And had it not been for a decisive Word, the matter would have been judged between them. And verily, for the wrongdoers there is a painful torment.

# 4294

You will see the wrongdoers fearful of that which they have earned, and it will surely befall them. But those who believe and do righteous deeds (will be) in the flowering meadows of the Gardens. They shall have whatsoever they desire with their Lord. That is the supreme grace.

# 4295

That is whereof Allah gives glad tidings to His servants who believe and do righteous good deeds. Say: "No reward do I ask of you for this except to be kind to me for my kinship with you." And whoever earns a good righteous deed, We shall give him an increase of good in respect thereof. Verily, Allah is Oft-Forgiving, Most Ready to appreciate.

# 4296

Or say they: "He has invented a lie against Allah" If Allah willed, He could have sealed up your heart. And Allah wipes out falsehood, and establishes the truth by His Word. Verily, He knows well what are in the breasts.

# 4297

And He it is Who accepts repentance from His servants, and forgives sins, and He knows what you do.

# 4298

And He answers those who believe and do righteous good deeds, and gives them increase of His bounty. And as for the disbelievers, theirs will be a severe torment.

# 4299

And if Allah were to extend the provision for His servants, they would surely rebel in the earth, but He sends down by measure as He wills. Verily, He is, in respect of His servants, the Well-Aware, the All-Seer.

# 4300

And He it is Who sends down the rain after they have despaired, and spreads His mercy. And He is the Wali, Worthy of all praise.

# 4301

And among His Ayat is the creation of the heavens and the earth, and whatever moving creatures He has dispersed in them both. And He is Able to assemble them whenever He wills.

# 4302

And whatever of misfortune befalls you, it is because of what your hands have earned. And He pardons much.

# 4303

And you cannot escape from Allah in the earth, and besides Allah you have neither any protector nor any helper.

# 4304

And among His signs are the ships in the sea like mountains.

# 4305

If He wills, He causes the wind to cease, then they would become motionless on the surface (of the sea). Verily, in this are signs for everyone patient and grateful.

# 4306

Or He may destroy them because of that which their (people) have earned. And He pardons much.

# 4307

And those who dispute as regards Our Ayat may know that there is no place of refuge for them.

# 4308

So whatever you have been given is but (a passing) enjoyment for this worldly life, but that which is with Allah is better and more lasting for those who believe and put their trust in their Lord.

# 4309

And those who shun the greater sins, and Al-Fawahish, and when they are angry, they forgive.

# 4310

And those who answer the Call of their Lord, and perform the Salah, and who (conduct) their affairs by mutual consultation, and who spend of what We have bestowed on them.

# 4311

And those who, when an oppressive wrong is done to them, take revenge.

# 4312

The recompense for an evil is an evil like thereof; but whoever forgives and makes reconciliation, his reward is with Allah. Verily, He likes not the wrongdoers.

# 4313

And indeed whosoever takes revenge after he has suffered wrong, for such there is no way (of blame) against them.

# 4314

The way is only against those who oppress men and rebel in the earth without justification; for such there will be a painful torment.

# 4315

And verily, whosoever shows patience and forgives, that would truly be from the things recommended by Allah.

# 4316

And whomsoever Allah sends astray, for him there is no protector after Him. And you will see the wrongdoers, when they behold the torment, they will say: "Is there any way of return"

# 4317

And you will see them brought forward to it (Hell) made humble by disgrace, (and) looking with stealthy glance. And those who believe will say: "Verily, the losers are they who lose themselves and their families on the Day of Resurrection." Verily, the wrongdoers will be in a lasting torment.

# 4318

And they will have no protectors to help them other than Allah. And he whom Allah sends astray, for him there is no way.

# 4319

Answer the Call of your Lord before there comes from Allah a Day which cannot be averted. You will have no refuge on that Day nor there will be for you any denying.

# 4320

But if they turn away, We have not sent you as a Hafiz over them. Your duty is to convey. And verily, when We cause man to taste of mercy from Us, he rejoices there at; but when some evil befalls them because of the deeds which their hands have sent forth, then verily, man (becomes) ingrate!

# 4321

To Allah belongs the kingdom of the heavens and the earth. He creates what He wills. He bestows female upon whom He wills, and bestows male upon whom He wills.

# 4322

Or He bestows both males and females, and He renders barren whom He wills. Verily, He is the All-Knower and is Able (to do all things).

# 4323

It is not given to any human being that Allah should speak to him unless (it be) by revelation, or from behind a veil, or (that) He sends a Messenger to reveal what He wills by His leave. Verily, He is Most High, Most Wise.

# 4324

And thus We have sent to you Ruh of Our command. You knew not what is the Book, nor what is Faith. But We have made it a light wherewith We guide whosoever of Our servants We will. And verily, you are indeed guiding to a straight path.

# 4325

The path of Allah to Whom belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is on the earth. Verily, all matters at the end go to Allah.

# 4326

Ha Mim.

# 4327

By the manifest Book.

# 4328

Verily, We have made it a Qur'an in Arabic that you may be able to understand.

# 4329

And verily, it is in the Mother of the Book with Us, indeed exalted, full of wisdom.

# 4330

Shall We then take away the Reminder from you, because you are a people excessive.

# 4331

And how many a Prophet have We sent amongst the men of old.

# 4332

And never came there a Prophet to them but they used to mock at him.

# 4333

Then We destroyed men stronger (in power) than these and the example of the ancients has passed away.

# 4334

And indeed if you ask them: "Who has created the heavens and the earth" They will surely say: "The All-Mighty, the All-Knower created them."

# 4335

Who has made for you the earth like a bed, and has made for you roads therein, in order that you may find your way.

# 4336

And Who sends down water from the sky in due measure, then We revive a dead land therewith, and even so you will be brought forth.

# 4337

And Who has created all the pairs and has appointed for you ships and cattle on which you ride,

# 4338

In order that you may mount on their backs, and then may remember the favor of your Lord when you mount thereon, and say: "Glory to Him Who has subjected this to us, and we could have never had it."

# 4339

And verily, to Our Lord we indeed are to return!"

# 4340

Yet, they assign to some of His servants a share with Him. Verily, man is indeed a manifest ingrate!

# 4341

Or has He taken daughters out of what He has created, and He has selected for you sons

# 4342

And if one of them is informed of the news of that which he sets forth as a parable to the Most Gracious, his face becomes dark, and he is filled with grief!

# 4343

A creature who is brought up in adornments, and who in dispute cannot make itself clear

# 4344

And they make females the angels who themselves are servants of the Most Gracious. Did they witness their creation Their testimony will be recorded, and they will be questioned!

# 4345

And they said: "If it had been the will of the Most Gracious, we should not have worshipped them." They have no knowledge whatsoever of that. They do nothing but lie!

# 4346

Or have We given them any Book before this (the Qur'an) to which they are holding fast

# 4347

Nay! They say: "We found our fathers following a certain way and religion, and we guide ourselves by their footsteps."

# 4348

And similarly, We sent not a warner before you to any town (people) but the luxurious ones among them said: "We found our fathers following a certain way and religion, and we will indeed follow their footsteps."

# 4349

He said: "Even if I bring you better guidance than that which you found your fathers following" They said: "Verily, we disbelieve in that with which you have been sent."

# 4350

So We took revenge on them, then see what was the end of those who denied.

# 4351

And (remember) when Ibrahim said to his father and his people: "Verily, I am innocent of what you worship,"

# 4352

"Except Him Who created me; and verily, He will guide me."

# 4353

And he made it a word lasting among his offspring, that they may turn back.

# 4354

Nay, but I gave to these and their fathers to enjoy, till there came to them the truth, and a Messenger making things clear.

# 4355

And when the truth came to them, they said: "This is magic, and we disbelieve therein."

# 4356

And they say: "Why is not this Qur'an sent down to some great man of the two towns"

# 4357

Is it they who would portion out the mercy of your Lord It is We Who portion out between them their livelihood in this world, and We raised some of them above others in ranks, so that some may employ others in their work. But the mercy of your Lord is better than what they amass.

# 4358

And were it not that mankind would have become of one community, We would have provided for those who disbelieve in the Most Gracious, silver roofs for their houses, and elevators whereby they ascend,

# 4359

And for their houses, doors, and thrones on which they could recline,

# 4360

And adornments of gold. Yet all this would have been nothing but an enjoyment of this world. And the Hereafter with your Lord is for those who have Taqwa.

# 4361

And whosoever Ya\`shu (turns away blindly) from the remembrance of the Most Gracious, We appoint for him Shaytan to be a Qarin (a companion) to him.

# 4362

And verily, they hinder them from the path, but they think that they are guided aright!

# 4363

Till, when (such a one) comes to Us, he says, "Would that between me and you were the distance of the two easts (or the east and west) a worst companion (indeed)!"

# 4364

It will profit you not this Day as you did wrong, (and) that you will be sharers in the punishment.

# 4365

Can you make the deaf to hear, or can you guide the blind or him who is in manifest error

# 4366

And even if We take you away, We shall indeed take vengeance on them.

# 4367

Or (if) We show you that wherewith We threaten them, then verily, We have perfect command over them.

# 4368

So hold you fast to that which is revealed to you. Verily, you are on the straight path.

# 4369

And verily, this is indeed a Dhikr for you and your people, and you will be questioned.

# 4370

And ask whom We sent before you of Our Messengers: "Did We ever appoint gods to be worshipped besides the Most Gracious"

# 4371

And indeed We did send Musa with Our Ayat to Fir\`awn and his chiefs. He said: "Verily, I am a Messenger of the Lord of all that exists."

# 4372

But when he came to them with Our Ayat, behold, they laughed at them.

# 4373

And not an Ayah We showed them but it was greater than its fellow preceding it, and We seized them with torment, in order that they might turn.

# 4374

And they said (to Musa): "O you sorcerer! Invoke your Lord for us according to what He has made a pact with you. Verily, We shall guide ourselves."

# 4375

But when We removed the torment from them, behold, they broke their covenant.

# 4376

And Fir\`awn proclaimed among his people (saying): "O my people! Is not mine the dominion of Egypt, and these rivers flowing underneath me. See you not then"

# 4377

"Am I not better than this one (Musa) who is despicable and can scarcely express himself clearly"

# 4378

Why then are not golden bracelets bestowed on him, or angels sent along with him"

# 4379

Thus he fooled his people, and they obeyed him. Verily, they were ever a people who were rebellious.

# 4380

So when they angered Us, We punished them, and drowned them all.

# 4381

And We made them a precedent, and an example to later generations.

# 4382

And when the son of Maryam is quoted as an example, behold, your people cry aloud thereat.

# 4383

And say: "Are our gods better or is he" They quoted not the above example except for argument. Nay! But they are a quarrelsome people.

# 4384

He was not more than a servant. We granted Our favor to him, and We made him an example for the Children of Israel.

# 4385

And if it were Our will, We would have made angels to replace you on the earth.

# 4386

And he shall be a known sign for (the coming of) the Hour. Therefore have no doubt concerning it. And follow Me! This is the straight path.

# 4387

And let not Shaytan hinder you. Verily, he (Shaytan) to you is a plain enemy.

# 4388

And when \`Isa came with clear proofs, he said: "I have come to you with Al-Hikmah, and in order to make clear to you some of that in which you differ. Therefore have Taqwa of Allah and obey me."

# 4389

"Verily, Allah! He is my Lord and your Lord. So worship Him. This is the straight path."

# 4390

But the sects from among themselves differed. So woe to those who do wrong from the torment of a painful Day!

# 4391

Do they only wait for the Hour that it shall come upon them suddenly while they perceive not

# 4392

Friends on that Day will be foes one to another except those who have Taqwa.

# 4393

My servants! No fear shall be on you this Day, nor shall you grieve,

# 4394

(You) who believed in Our Ayat and were Muslims.

# 4395

Enter Paradise, you and your wives, in happiness.

# 4396

Trays of gold and cups will be passed round them; (there will be) therein all that their souls desire, and all that eyes could delight in and you will abide therein forever.

# 4397

This is the Paradise, which you have been made to inherit because of your deeds that you used to do.

# 4398

Therein for you will be fruits in plenty, of which you will eat (as you desire).

# 4399

Verily, the criminals will be in the torment of Hell to abide therein forever.

# 4400

(The torment) will not be lightened for them, and they will be plunged into destruction with deep regrets, sorrows and in despair therein.

# 4401

We wronged them not, but they were the wrongdoers.

# 4402

And they will cry: "O Malik (keeper of Hell)! Let your Lord make an end of us." He will say: "Verily, you shall abide forever."

# 4403

Indeed We have brought the truth to you, but most of you have a hatred for the truth.

# 4404

Or have they plotted some plan Then We too are planning.

# 4405

Or do they think that We hear not their secrets and their private counsel Yes (We do) and Our messengers are by them, to record.

# 4406

Say: "If the Most Gracious had a son, then I am the first of the worshippers."

# 4407

Glorified is the Lord of the heavens and the earth, the Lord of the Throne! Exalted be He from all that they ascribe (to Him).

# 4408

So leave them (alone) to speak nonsense and play until they meet the Day of theirs which they have been promised.

# 4409

It is He Who is the only God in the heaven and the only God on the earth. And He is the All-Wise, the All-Knower.

# 4410

And Blessed be He to Whom belongs the kingdom of the heavens and the earth, and all that is between them, and with Whom is the knowledge of the Hour, and to Whom you (all) will be returned.

# 4411

And those whom they invoke instead of Him have no power of intercession -- except for those who bear witness to the truth knowingly, and they know.

# 4412

And if you ask them who created them, they will surely say: "Allah." How then are they turned away

# 4413

And his saying: "O my Lord! Verily, these are a people who believe not!"

# 4414

So turn away from them, and say: Salam (peace!) But they will come to know.

# 4415

Ha Mim.

# 4416

By the manifest Book that makes things clear.

# 4417

We sent it down on a blessed night. Verily, We are ever warning.

# 4418

Therein (that night) is decreed every matter, Hakim.

# 4419

As a command from Us. Verily, We are ever sending,

# 4420

(As) a mercy from your Lord. Verily, He is the All-Hearer, the All-Knower.

# 4421

The Lord of the heavens and the earth and all that is between them, if you (but) have a faith with certainty.

# 4422

La ilaha illa Huwa. He gives life and causes death -- your Lord and the Lord of your forefathers.

# 4423

Nay! They play about in doubt.

# 4424

Then wait you for the Day when the sky will bring forth a visible smoke,

# 4425

Covering mankind, this is a painful torment.

# 4426

(They will say): "Our Lord! Remove the torment from us, really we shall become believers!"

# 4427

How can there be for them an admonition, when a Messenger explaining things clearly has already come to them.

# 4428

Then they had turned away from him and said: "(He is) one taught, a madman!"

# 4429

Verily, We shall remove the torment for a while. Verily, you will revert.

# 4430

On the Day when We shall strike you with the great Batshah. Verily, We will exact retribution.

# 4431

And indeed We tried before them Fir\`awn's people, when there came to them a noble Messenger.

# 4432

Saying: "Deliver to me the servants of Allah. Verily, I am to you a Messenger worthy of all trust."

# 4433

"And exalt not yourselves against Allah. Truly, I have come to you with a manifest authority."

# 4434

"And truly, I seek refuge with my Lord and your Lord, lest you should stone me."

# 4435

"But if you believe me not, then keep away from me and leave me alone."

# 4436

So he (Musa) called upon his Lord (saying): "These are indeed the people who are criminals."

# 4437

(Allah said): "Depart you with My servants by night. Surely, you will be pursued."

# 4438

"And leave the sea as it is (quiet and divided). Verily, they are a host to be drowned."

# 4439

How many of gardens and springs that they (Fir\`awn's people) left behind,

# 4440

And green crops (fields) and goodly places,

# 4441

And comforts of life wherein they used to take delight!

# 4442

Thus (it was)! And We made other people inherit them.

# 4443

And the heavens and the earth wept not for them, nor were they given respite.

# 4444

And indeed We saved the Children of Israel from the humiliating torment,

# 4445

From Fir\`awn; verily, he was arrogant and was of the excessive.

# 4446

And We chose them above the nations (Al-\`Alamin) with knowledge,

# 4447

And granted them signs in which there was a plain trial.

# 4448

Verily, these people are saying:

# 4449

"There is nothing but our first death, and we shall not be resurrected."

# 4450

"Then bring back our forefathers, if you speak the truth!"

# 4451

Are they better or the people of Tubba\` and those before them We destroyed them because they were indeed criminals.

# 4452

And We created not the heavens and the earth, and all that is between them, for mere play.

# 4453

We created them not except with truth, but most of them know not.

# 4454

Verily, the Day of Judgement is the time appointed for all of them --

# 4455

The Day when a near relative cannot avail a near relative in aught, and no help can they receive,

# 4456

Except him on whom Allah has mercy. Verily, He is the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful.

# 4457

Verily, the tree of Zaqqum

# 4458

Will be the food of the sinners.

# 4459

Like boiling oil, it will boil in the bellies,

# 4460

Like the boiling of scalding water.

# 4461

(It will be said:) "Seize him and drag him into the midst of blazing Fire,"

# 4462

"Then pour over his head the torment of boiling water."

# 4463

"Taste you (this)! Verily, you were (pretending to be) the mighty, the generous."

# 4464

"Verily, this is that whereof you used to doubt!"

# 4465

Verily, those who have Taqwa, will be in place of security.

# 4466

Among Gardens and Springs,

# 4467

Dressed in Sundus and Istabraq, facing each other,

# 4468

So (it will be). And We shall marry them to Hur (fair females) with wide lovely eyes,

# 4469
